006|011|Say, “Travel the earth and observe the fate of the deniers.”
006|012|Say, “To whom belongs all that’s in the heavens and the earth?” Say, “To Allah.” He made mercy incumbent upon Himself. He will gather you on Resurrection Day, which is beyond doubt. Those who lost their souls won’t believe.
006|013|To Him belongs whatever rests in the night and the day. He is the All-Hearing, the All-Knowing.
006|014|Say, “Should I take a protector other than Allah, the Originator of the heavens and the earth, who feeds and is not fed?” Say, “I am instructed to be the first who submits.” And don’t be among the polytheists.
006|015|Say, “I fear the punishment of a tremendous Day if I were to disobey my Lord.”
006|016|Whoever is spared from it on that Day, He will indeed have shown mercy to him; and that’s the clear success.
006|017|If Allah touches you with adversity, no one can remove it but Him. And if He touches you with good, He is capable of everything.
006|018|He is the Dominant over His beings. He is the All-Wise, the Expert.
006|019|Ask them, “What is greater in testimony?” Say, “Allah is the Witness between me and you. This Quran has been revealed to me, to warn you by it and anyone it reaches. Do you bear witness that there are other gods besides Allah?” Say, “I don’t bear witness.” Say, “He is, but One God, and I am innocent of whatever you associate with Him.”
006|020|Those to whom We gave the Scripture recognize it as they recognize their own children. Yet, those who lost their souls don’t believe.
006|021|Who is more unjust than one who fabricates lies about Allah or rejects His revelations? The wrongdoers won’t succeed.
006|022|On the Day We gather them all together, We will ask those who associated partners with Allah, “Where are those partners you claimed?”
006|023|Their only response will be, “By Allah, our Lord, we were not polytheists.”
006|024|See how they lie to themselves, and how the falsehoods they invented have forsaken them.
006|025|Some of them listen to you, but We placed veils over their hearts, preventing them from understanding it, and deafness in their ears. Even if they witnessed every sign, they wouldn’t believe in it. When they come to argue with you, the disbelievers say, “This is nothing but legends of the ancients.”
006|026|They deter others from it and avoid it themselves. They destroy nothing but themselves, yet they don’t perceive it.
006|027|If only you could see, when they’re made to stand before the Fire. They will plead, “If only we could return, not reject our Lord’s revelations, and be among the believers.”
006|028|What they had concealed before will now appear to them; and even if they were sent back, they would certainly return to what they were forbidden, and most surely they are liars.
006|029|They say, “There is nothing beyond our worldly life, and we won’t be resurrected.”
006|030|If only you could see when they are presented before their Lord. He will ask, “Isn’t this the truth?” They will reply, “Yes, by our Lord.” He will say, “Then taste the punishment for your disbelief.”
006|031|Those who deny the meeting with Allah have lost. When the Hour suddenly overtakes them, they will exclaim, “Woe to us for neglecting this!” And they will bear their burdens on their backs—what a terrible load they bear!
006|032|The life of this world is but a game and a diversion. The Home in the Hereafter is far superior for the righteous. Don’t you understand?
006|033|We know that what they say grieves you. It’s not you they reject, but it is Allah’s verses that the wrongdoers deny.
006|034|Messengers before you were also rejected, but they patiently endured rejection and persecution until Our help arrived. And there is no change to the words of Allah. There has already come to you news about the messengers.
006|035|If their denial becomes unbearable for you, then if you can, seek a tunnel through the earth or a ladder into heaven to bring them a sign. If Allah had willed, He could’ve guided them all. So, don’t be of the ignorant.
006|036|Only those who listen will respond. As for the dead, Allah will resurrect them. Then they will be returned to Him.
006|037|They question, “Why has no sign been sent down to him from his Lord?” Say, “Allah has the power to send down a miracle, but most of them don’t know.”
006|038|There is no creature on earth nor bird that flies with its wings, but they are communities like you. We’ve not neglected anything in the Book. Then to their Lord they will be gathered.
006|039|Those who reject Our signs are deaf and mute, in darkness. Whomever Allah wills, He leaves to stray, and whomever He wills, He sets on a straight path.
006|040|Say, “Consider if Allah’s punishment were to befall you, or the Hour were to arrive, would you call upon anyone other than Allah, if you are truthful?”
006|041|Only Him you would call upon, and if He wills, He could remove what you implored Him for, and you would forget what you associated.
006|042|We sent messengers to communities before you, and We seized them with hardship and distress, so they might humble themselves.
006|043|But when Our might came upon them, they didn’t humble themselves. But their hearts became hard, Satan beautified their deeds for them.
006|044|When they dismissed the reminders given to them, We opened for them the gates of everything. But just as they were rejoicing in what they received, We seized them abruptly, and they were left in despair.
006|045|Thus, the wrongdoers were utterly cut off. Praise be to Allah, the Lord of the worlds.
006|046|Ask, “Imagine if Allah were to take away your hearing and sight, and seal upon your hearts; which god, other than Allah, could restore them to you?” See how We lay out the signs in detail, yet they still turn away.
006|047|Ask, “Imagine if Allah’s punishment came upon you suddenly or predictably; would anyone be destroyed except the wrongdoers?”
006|048|We send messengers only to bring good news and to warn. Those who believe and reform will have no fear, nor will they grieve.
006|049|But those who deny Our messages will suffer torment for their defiant disobedience.
006|050|Say, “I don’t claim to hold Allah’s treasures or to know the unseen. I don’t claim to be an angel either. I only follow what’s revealed to me.” Say, “Can the blind and the seeing be equal? Don’t you reflect?”
006|051|Warn with it those who fear being gathered before their Lord—they have no protector or intercessor besides Him—so that they may become righteous.
006|052|Don’t dismiss those who call upon their Lord morning and evening, desiring His countenance. You are not responsible for their judgment, nor are they responsible for yours. If you dismiss them, you will be among the wrongdoers.
006|053|We test some people through others, so they may ask, “Are these the ones Allah favored among us?” Doesn’t Allah know best those who are thankful?
006|054|When those who believe in Our revelations come to you, say, “Peace be upon you. Your Lord has mandated mercy on Himself. If anyone among you commits wrong out of ignorance, and then repents and reforms his ways, then He is Forgiving and Merciful.”
006|055|In this way, We detail the verses, so that the way of the wicked may become fully apparent.
006|056|Say, “I am forbidden to worship those you invoke besides Allah.” Say, “I won’t follow your whims, for then I would stray and not be among the guided ones.”
006|057|Say, “I am reliant on clear evidence from my Lord, yet you deny it. I don’t have what you eagerly demand. Judgment rests solely with Allah. He states the truth, and He is the best of judges.”
006|058|Say, “If I had control over what you eagerly demand, the matter between us would’ve been settled. But Allah knows the wrongdoers best.
006|059|With Him are the keys to the unseen; none knows them but He. He knows everything on land and in the sea. Not a leaf falls without His knowledge, nor is there a grain in the darkness of the earth, or anything fresh or dry, but it is recorded in a clear book.
006|060|It is He who retrieves your souls at night and knows what you’ve accomplished by day. Then He revives you therein to complete a designated term. Then, to Him will be your return, and He will inform you about your deeds.
006|061|He is the Conqueror over His beings, and He dispatches guardians over you, until, when death approaches one of you, Our messengers retrieve their souls, never neglecting in their duty.
006|062|Then, they are returned to Allah, their true Master. His is the judgment, and He is the fastest of accountants.
006|063|Say, “Who rescues you from the darkness of land and sea when you call upon Him, humbly and privately, ‘If He rescues us from this, we will surely be among the thankful?”
006|064|Say, “It is Allah who saves you from it and from every distress, you still associate others with Him.”
006|065|Say, “He is capable of sending a punishment upon you from above or beneath your feet, or dividing you into factions and making you experience each other’s brutality. See how We diversify the verses, so they might understand.”
006|066|Your people have denied it, even though it’s the truth. Say, “I’m not a manager over you.”
006|067|For every prophecy there is a fixed time, and you will soon come to know.
006|068|When you see those who engage in offensive discussions about Our verses, turn away from them until they engage in a different topic. Should Satan cause you to forget, then once you remember, don’t sit in the company of the unjust people.
006|069|The righteous bear no responsibility for them, but a reminder might assist them in becoming conscious.
006|070|Leave those who treat their religion as amusement and distraction, and whom the worldly life has deceived. However, remind with it, lest a soul be ruined by what it earned, it will have no protector or intercessor besides Allah. Even if it should offer every compensation, it won’t be accepted from it. These are the ones who are doomed by their actions. For them is a drink of boiling water and a severe punishment due to their disbelief.
006|071|Say, “Should we call upon, instead of Allah, those who can neither benefit nor harm us, and turn backward after Allah has guided us? Like one whom the devils have led astray on the earth, bewildered in the wilderness, confused, while his friends call him to guidance, saying, ‘Come to us’.” Say, “Allah’s guidance is the guidance, and we’ve been commanded to submit to the Lord of the universes.”
006|072|“And to establish prayer and revere Him. It is to Him that you will be gathered.”
006|073|It is He who created the heavens and the earth with truth. The Day He says, “Be,” it becomes. His word is the ultimate truth. His is the dominion on the Day when the trumpet is blown; the Knower of the unseen and the seen; He is the Wise, the Expert.
006|074|Abraham told his father, Azar, “Do you take idols as gods? I see you and your people are clearly astrayed.”
006|075|We showed Abraham the empire of the heavens and the earth, so that he could have certainty.
006|076|When the night covered him, he saw a star and said, “This is my lord.” But once it set, he said, “I don’t love things that set.”
006|077|When he saw the moon rising, he said, “This is my lord.” But once it set, he said, “Unless my Lord guides me, I would surely be among the misguided.”
006|078|And when he saw the sun rising, he said, “This is my lord; this is greater.” But once it set, he said, “O my people, I am free from what you associate with Him.
006|079|I have turned my face towards the One who originated the heavens and the earth, as a monotheist, and I’m not of the polytheists.”
006|080|His people debated with him, and he said, “Are you arguing with me about Allah after He has guided me? I don’t fear what you associate with Him, unless my Lord should will something. My Lord encompasses all things in knowledge. Won’t you then remember?
006|081|How can I fear what you associate with Him? Instead, you should fear, for you associate with Allah what He never authorized. So which of the two parties has more right to security, if you know?”
006|082|Those who believe and don’t pollute their faith with injustice—these will have security, and they are guided.
006|083|We gave this reasoning to Abraham against his people. We raise in rank whom We will. Your Lord is Wise and Knowing.
006|084|We granted him Isaac and Jacob; each one We guided. We also guided Noah before. And from his offspring, David, Solomon, Job, Joseph, Moses, and Aaron. We thus reward the good-doers.
006|085|Also, Zechariah, John, Jesus, and Elias—all of the virtuous.
006|086|And Ishmael, Elisha, Jonah, and Lot—and each, we preferred over the worlds.
006|087|And among their ancestors, descendants, and brothers—We chose them, and We guided them to a straight path.
006|088|This is Allah’s guidance; with it, He guides whomever He wills among His servants. If they were to associate others with Him, then all their deeds would be nullified.
006|089|These are the ones to whom We gave the Scripture, wisdom, and prophethood. If these people reject it, We’ve already entrusted it to a people who won’t reject it.
006|090|These are the ones whom Allah has guided, so emulate their guidance. Say, “I ask for no compensation for it. This is but a reminder to all mankind.”
006|091|They don’t appraise Allah with true appraisal when they say, “Allah didn’t reveal anything to any human.” Say, “Then, who revealed the Scripture which Moses brought, a light and guidance for humanity? You treat it as mere sheets of paper, showing some and concealing much. You were taught things that neither you nor your ancestors knew before.” Say, “Allah.” Then, leave them playing in their vain discussions.
006|092|We revealed this blessed Scripture, confirming what preceded it, that you may warn the Mother of Cities and those around it. Those who believe in the Hereafter believe in it, and are constant in their prayers.
006|093|Who is more unjust than one who fabricates lies against Allah or says, “A revelation was given to me,” when nothing was revealed to him, or who says, “I can reveal the like of what Allah has revealed?” If only you could see the wrongdoers in the throes of death, with the angels extending their hands, saying, “Yield up your souls! Today, are you being repaid with a punishment of humiliation for the lies you spoke against Allah, and for your being scornful to His signs.”
006|094|“You’ve come to Us alone, as We created you the first time, leaving behind everything We had bestowed upon you. We don’t see your supposed intercessors with you. The links between you and them have been severed, and all you presumed has let you down.”
006|095|Allah is the splitter of the grain and the kernel, bringing out the living from the dead, and the dead from the living. This is Allah. So, how are you deluded?
006|096|He is the One who breaks the dawn, and has made the night for you to rest, and the sun and moon according to calculations. Such is the design of the Almighty, the All-Knowing.
006|097|It is He who set the stars for you, so you may be guided by them in the darknesses of land and sea. We detailed the signs for people who know.
006|098|It is He who initiated you from a single soul, then from a repository, and then from a depository. We detail the signs for people who understand.
006|099|It is He who sends down rain from the sky. With it, We produce diverse kinds of vegetation: lush greenery, from which We produce clustered grain, and date palms with hanging clusters, vineyards, olives, and pomegranates, similar and dissimilar. Observe their fruits as they grow and ripen. In these are signs for people who believe.
006|100|Yet, they attribute partners to Allah—the jinn—even though He created them. They pierce for Him sons and daughters, without any knowledge. Exalted is He, and high above what they attribute to Him.
006|101|The Originator of the heavens and the earth. How could He have a child when He has no female companion? He created all things and is fully aware of everything.
006|102|Such is Allah, your Lord. There is no deity except He, the Creator of all things. Worship Him alone, for He is in charge of all things.
006|103|No vision can grasp Him, yet He grasps all vision. He is the Subtle, the Expert.
006|104|Clear proofs have come to you from your Lord. Whoever sees, does so for his good; and whoever remains blind, does so to his detriment. “I am not a keeper over you.”
006|105|Thus, We vary the verses, so that they may say, “You have studied,” and that We may make clear for a people who know.
006|106|Follow what has been revealed to you from your Lord, for there is no god but Him, and turn away from the associators.
006|107|If Allah had willed, they wouldn’t have associated. We didn’t make you a guardian over them, nor are you a manager over them.
006|108|Don’t insult those they invoke besides Allah, lest they insult Allah out of hostility and ignorance. We made each community’s deeds seem appealing to them. Eventually, they will return to their Lord, who will inform them of everything they did.
006|109|They swear their strongest oaths by Allah that if a miracle came to them, they would believe in it. Say, “The signs are only with Allah.” And how could you tell, when if it did come, they still wouldn’t believe.
006|110|We will turn their hearts and eyes away, just as they refused to believe in it the first time, leaving them wandering aimlessly in their transgression.
006|111|Even if We sent down the angels to them, made the dead speak to them, and gathered all things before them, they would still not believe, unless Allah wills it. But most of them don’t know.
006|112|Similarly, We’ve assigned enemies for every prophet—human and jinn devils—who inspire each other with embellished, deceitful speech. If your Lord had willed, they wouldn’t have done it. So, leave them and their fabrication.
006|113|This allows the hearts of those who don’t believe in the Hereafter to incline towards it, find satisfaction in it, and persist in their sinful pursuits.
006|114|“Should I seek a judge other than Allah, when it is He who revealed the Scripture to you in detail?” Those to whom We gave the Scripture recognize it as the truth from your Lord, so don’t be of those who doubt.
006|115|The Word of your Lord is perfected in its truth and justice. None can alter His words. He is the All-Hearing, the All-Knowing.
006|116|If you were to obey the majority of those on earth, they would lead you astray from Allah’s path. They follow only conjecture, and they are only guessing.
006|117|Your Lord is the most knowledgeable of those who deviate from His path, and He is fully aware of those who are guided.
006|118|Eat of what Allah’s name was pronounced, if you are believers in His revelations.
006|119|Why shouldn’t you not eat that over which Allah’s name was pronounced, when He has already explained to you what He has forbidden to you, except when you are compelled? Many lead astray by their desires, due to their lack of knowledge. Your Lord is fully aware of the transgressors.
006|120|And abandon all sin, whether open or secret. Those who commit sins will be reimbursed for what they’ve done.
006|121|Don’t eat from what Allah’s name hasn’t been mentioned upon, for it’s sinful. The devils inspire their allies to argue with you. If you were to obey them, you would be polytheists.
006|122|Is one who was dead, to whom We gave life and a light by which he can walk among people, be like the one who is in deep darkness, from which he can’t emerge? Thus, the deeds of the unbelievers have been made appealing to them.
006|123|In every community, We’ve placed its most notorious criminals, to conspire within it. However, they only conspire against themselves, without realizing it.
006|124|When a verse comes to them, they say, “We won’t believe unless we receive the same revelations as Allah’s messengers.” Allah knows best where to place His message. Humiliation from Allah and severe punishment will afflict the criminals for their scheming.
006|125|Whomever Allah wills to guide, He expands his heart to submission. And whomever He wills to misguide, He makes his heart tight and constricted, as if he were ascending into the sky. In this way, Allah lays defilement on those who don’t believe.
006|126|This is the path of your Lord, straight. We detailed the signs for those who pay heed.
006|127|For them is the Home of Peace with their Lord, and He is their Protector as a result of their deeds.
006|128|On the Day when He will gather them all: “O assembly of jinn, you’ve exploited many humans.” Their human allies will say, “Our Lord, we’ve benefited from each other, but we’ve now reached the term that You’ve appointed for us.” He will say, “The Fire is your residence, where you will remain forever, except as Allah wills.” Your Lord is Wise and All-Knowing.
006|129|Thus, We let some wrongdoers befriend each other due to what they used to earn.
006|130|“O community of jinn and humans, didn’t there come to you messengers from among you, relating to you My verses and warning you of the meeting of this Day of yours?” They will respond, “We bear witness against ourselves.” The worldly life deceived them, and they will testify against themselves that they were unbelievers.
006|131|That is because your Lord would not unjustly destroy communities while their people are unaware.
006|132|Every soul will be ranked according to its deeds. Your Lord is not unaware of what they do.
006|133|Your Lord is the Self-Sufficient, full of mercy. If He wills, He can remove you and replace you with anyone He wills, just as He raised you from the descendants of another people.
006|134|What you are promised is coming, and you can’t prevent it.
006|135|Say, “O my people, act according to your ability, and so will I. Soon, you will know who will attain the ultimate Home.” The wrongdoers won’t succeed.
006|136|They assign for Allah a portion of the crops and livestock that He originated, saying, “This is for Allah,” so they claim, and “This is for our partners.” But what’s designated for their partners doesn’t reach Allah, while what’s designated for Allah does reach their partners. Bad indeed is their judgment.
006|137|And thus, many of the idolaters have been led by their partners to kill their children, bringing about their ruin and causing confusion in their religion. If Allah had willed, they wouldn’t have done it. So leave them and what they fabricate.
006|138|They also assert, “These livestock and crops are sanctified; none may eat from except those we allow,” so they claim, and certain animals they deem forbidden to ride. And some animals on which they don’t pronounce the name of Allah, inventing falsehood against Him—He will recompense them for what they’ve been inventing.
006|139|They further allege, “What’s in the womb of these animals is exclusively for our males and is forbidden to our wives.” However, if it’s stillborn, they all share in it. He will recompense them for their allegation. He is All-Wise, All-Knowing.
006|140|Those who killed their children have suffered loss, without knowledge, and forbid what Allah provided for them, fabricating lies against Allah. They strayed and weren’t guided.
006|141|It is He who produced gardens, both trellised and untrellised, and date palms, various crops with different flavors, and olives and pomegranates, similar and dissimilar. Eat from their fruit when it ripens, give its due on the day of its harvest, and don’t be wasteful. He doesn’t like the extravagant.
006|142|Livestock serves as a means of transportation and a source of materials. Consume what Allah provided for you, and don’t follow Satan’s footsteps; he is a clear enemy to you.
006|143|Eight pairs: two of sheep and two of goats. Ask, “Did He prohibit the two males, the two females, or what’s carried in the wombs of the two females? Tell me with knowledge, if you are truthful.”
006|144|And of camels and cattle, two pairs. Ask, “Did He forbid the two males, the two females, or what the wombs of the two females contain? Were you present when Allah issued these prohibitions?” So who is more unjust than one who invents a lie against Allah, to lead people astray without knowledge? Allah doesn’t guide the unjust people.
006|145|Say, “In what was revealed to me, I find no food forbidden for consumption, except for carrion, spilled blood, pork—which is unclean—or a sinful offering dedicated to anyone other than Allah. However, if anyone is compelled by necessity, without willful disobedience or transgression, your Lord is Forgiving and Merciful.”
006|146|To those who are Jewish, We prohibited every animal with uncloven hooves; and of the cattle and the sheep We prohibited to them their fat, except what adheres to their backs or the entrails, or what’s mixed with bone. Thus, We penalized them for their rebelliousness. We are truthful.
006|147|If they accuse you of lying, say, “Your Lord is the possessor of vast mercy, but His punishment won’t be averted from guilty people.”
006|148|Those who associate others will say, “If Allah had willed, we wouldn’t have associated anything with Him, nor would our forefathers, nor would we have prohibited anything.” Likewise, those who came before them also denied until they tasted Our punishment. Say, “Do you have any knowledge you can present to us? You are just following speculation, and you do nothing but lie.”
006|149|Say, ”With Allah lies the decisive argument. Had He willed, He would have guided you all.”
006|150|Say, “Bring forth your witnesses who can testify that Allah has forbidden this.” If they do testify, don’t testify with them. And don’t follow the inclinations of those who deny Our signs, those who don’t believe in the Hereafter, those who equate others with their Lord.
006|151|Say, “Come, I will recite what your Lord prohibited for you: don’t associate anything with Him; honor your parents; don’t kill your children from fear of poverty—We provide for you and them; don’t approach immoralities, whether open or secret; and don’t take a life that Allah deemed sacred, except in the course of justice. These are His commandments to you, so you may know.”
006|152|And don’t come near the wealth of the orphan, except in the best manner, until he reaches maturity. Give full measure and weight in justice. We never burden a soul beyond its capacity. And when you speak, be just, even if it concerns a close relative. And fulfill your covenant with Allah. This, He has commanded you, so you may avoid wrongdoing.
006|153|This is My path, straight, so follow it. Don’t follow other paths, for they will lead you astray from His path. Allah has commanded this to you, so you may refrain from wrongdoing.
006|154|We gave Moses the Scripture, complete for those who do good, explaining all things, as guidance and mercy, so they may believe in the encounter with their Lord.
006|155|And this is a blessed Scripture that We revealed. Follow it and be righteous, so you may receive mercy.
006|156|Lest you say, “The Scripture was revealed to two communities before us, and we were unaware of their teachings.”
006|157|Or perhaps you might say, “Had the Scripture been revealed to us, we would’ve been more rightly guided than they.” Now, clear evidence, guidance, and mercy have come to you from your Lord. Who is more unjust than one who denies Allah’s messages and turns away from them? We will repay those who turn away from Our revelations with the severest punishment, because of their turning away.
006|158|Are they awaiting the descent of the angels, the arrival of your Lord Himself, or the manifestation of some of your Lord’s signs? On the day when some of these signs from your Lord do appear, faith won’t benefit any soul which didn’t believe before, or which didn’t earn any good by its faith. Say, “Wait; we, too, are waiting.”
006|159|As for those who divided their religion and became denominations, you have no association with them. Their case rests with Allah, and He will then inform them about their deeds.
006|160|Whoever presents a good deed will receive a tenfold equivalent. But whoever commits evil acts will only be repaid equivalently and won’t be wronged.
006|161|Say, “My Lord has guided me to a straight path, an upright religion, the community of Abraham the Monotheist, who wasn’t among the polytheists.”
006|162|Say, “My prayers, my devotion, my living, and my dying are all for Allah, the Lord of the worlds.
006|163|There is no partner for Him. To this I have been commanded, and I am the first of the Submitters.”
006|164|Say, “Should I seek a lord other than Allah, when He is the Lord of all things?” No soul earns except against itself, and no bearer of burdens will bear the burdens of another. Then to your Lord is your return, and He will inform you about your disagreements.
006|165|It is He who made you successors on earth and elevated some of you above others in ranks—to test you through what He gave you. Your Lord is swift in retribution, and He is Forgiving and Merciful.
007|001|Alif. Lam. Meem. Saad.
007|002|A Scripture was revealed to you, so let there be no anxiety in your heart because of it. Use it to warn, and as a reminder for the believers.
007|003|Follow what was revealed to you from your Lord, and don’t follow other masters beside Him. Yet, little do you remember.
007|004|How many a town have We destroyed! Our might came upon them by night or while they were taking a midday nap.
007|005|When Our wrath befell them, their only plea was, “Indeed, we were wrongdoers.”
007|006|We will question those to whom the messengers were sent, and We will question the messengers themselves.
007|007|We will narrate their stories to them with knowledge, for We were not absent.
007|008|On that Day, the weighing is the truth. Those whose scales are heavy will find success.
007|009|However, those with light scales will have lost their souls, for they had denied Our signs.
007|010|We established you on earth and provided for your sustenance and growth. Yet, seldom do you give thanks.
007|011|We created you, then We fashioned you, then We said to the angels, “Prostrate yourselves before Adam.” They all prostrated, except Iblis, he was not of those who prostrated.
007|012|He asked, “What prevented you from prostrating when I commanded you?” He replied, “I am superior to him; You created me from fire, but You created him from mud.”
007|013|He said, “Descend from this place; it’s not for you to be arrogant here! Get out, for you are disgraced!”
007|014|He pleaded, “Delay me until the Day they are resurrected.”
007|015|He replied, “You are granted a delay.”
007|016|He said, “Since You caused me to stray, I will sit in wait for them on Your straight path.
007|017|Then, I will come at them from before them and from behind them, from their right and their left. And You won’t find most of them as thankful.”
007|018|He said, “Get out of it, despised and defeated. Whoever among them follows you—I will fill up Hell with you all.
007|019|And you, Adam, reside with your wife in Paradise, and eat freely from wherever you wish; but don’t approach that tree, lest you become of the wrongdoers.”
007|020|Then Satan whispered to them, revealing their hidden nudity. He said, “Your Lord only forbade you this tree to prevent you from becoming angels or achieving immortality.”
007|021|And he swore to them, “I am truly a sincere advisor to you.”
007|022|Thus, he cunningly deceived them. And when they tasted the fruit of the tree, their nudity was exposed to them, and they started covering themselves with leaves from the Garden. Then their Lord called out to them, “Didn’t I prohibit you from that tree and warn you that Satan is your avowed enemy?”
007|023|They responded, “Our Lord, we have wronged ourselves. If You don’t forgive us and have mercy on us, we will be among the losers.”
007|024|He said, “Descend, with enmity among some of you. For you will have on the earth a settlement and enjoyment until a time.”
007|025|He added, “There, you will live; there, you will die, and from there, you will be resurrected.”
007|026|O Children of Adam, We provided you with clothing to cover your bodies and for fineries. But the clothing of piety—that is the best. These are among Allah’s verses, so they may take heed.
007|027|O Children of Adam, let not Satan tempt you, as he expelled your parents from Paradise, stripping them of their clothing to show them their nudity. He and his type see you from where you don’t see them. We made the devils allies to those who don’t believe.
007|028|When they commit an immoral act, they say, “We found our ancestors doing it, and Allah commanded us to do it.” Say, “Allah never commands immorality. Do you say about Allah what you don’t know?”
007|029|Say, “My Lord commands justice. Set your faces towards every place of worship, and pray to Him, devoting your faith to Him alone. Just as He originated you, so will you return.”
007|030|Some He has guided, and some deserved to lose their way. They’ve taken the devils as allies instead of Allah, thinking they are guided.
007|031|O Children of Adam, take your adornment at every place of prayer. Eat and drink, but don’t commit excesses, for He doesn’t like the extravagant.
007|032|Say, “Who prohibited the beautiful things that Allah produced for His beings, and the wholesome sustenance?” Say, “They are for those who believe during their life in this world, exclusively for them on Resurrection Day.” Thus, We detail the verses for people who know.
007|033|Say, “My Lord forbids shameless acts, whether open or hidden, and sin, and oppression, and associating anything with Allah without His permission, and speaking about Allah without knowledge.”
007|034|Every nation has an appointed time. When their appointed time comes, they won’t be able to delay it by a single hour. nor will they be able to advance it.
007|035|O Children of Adam, when messengers come to you from among you, conveying My messages to you, those who adhere to righteousness and reform will have no fear, nor will they grieve.
007|036|But those who deny Our verses and treat them with arrogance are the residents of the Fire, where they will dwell forever.
007|037|Who is more unjust than one who fabricates lies against Allah or denies His verses? These must have their share as decreed. Until Our messengers come to take their souls, they will ask, “Where are those you used to invoke besides Allah?” They will respond, “They have forsaken us.” And they will testify against themselves that they were unbelievers.
007|038|He will say, “Enter among the communities of jinn and humans that have gone before you into the Fire.” Every time a community enters, it will curse its predecessor. Until, when they have all arrived therein, the last of them will say about the first, “Our Lord, these misled us, so give them a double punishment in the Fire.” He will say, “Each will receive a double, but you don’t know.”
007|039|The first of them will say to the last, “You have no advantage over us, so taste the punishment for what you used to earn.”
007|040|Those who denied our verses and were arrogant towards them—for them, the gates of Heaven won’t open, nor will they enter Paradise, until a camel can pass through the eye of a needle. Thus do We recompense the wrongdoers.
007|041|For them will be beds in Hell, and from over them will be coverings. Thus do We recompense the wrongdoers.
007|042|As for those who believe and live righteously—We don’t burden any soul beyond its scope—these are the inhabitants of Paradise, where they will reside forever.
007|043|We will remove any ill feeling from their hearts, beneath them rivers will flow, and they will exclaim, “Praise be to Allah, who guided us to this. Had Allah not guided us, we wouldn’t have been guided. The messengers of our Lord truly brought the truth.” And they will be called, “This is the Paradise which you are made to inherit because of what you used to do.”
007|044|The inhabitants of Paradise will call out to the inhabitants of the Fire, “We found what our Lord promised us to be true; did you find your Lord’s promise to be true?” They will answer, “Yes.” An announcer between them will proclaim, “The curse of Allah is upon the wrongdoers.
007|045|Those who obstructed Allah’s path, sought to make it crooked, and denied the Hereafter.”
007|046|Between them is a partition, and on the Heights are men who recognize everyone by their marks. They will call out to the residents of Paradise, “Peace be upon you.” They haven’t yet entered it, but they hope to.
007|047|And when their gaze is directed towards the dwellers of the Fire, they will say, “Our Lord, don’t place us with the wrongdoers.”
007|048|The people on the Heights will call out to men they recognize by their features, saying, “Your hoardings availed you nothing, nor did your arrogance.
007|049|Are these the ones you swore Allah would never touch with mercy?” “Enter Paradise; there is no fear for you, nor will you grieve.”
007|050|The dwellers of the Fire will plead with the dwellers of Paradise, “Pour some water over us, or with some of what Allah has provided you with.” They will reply, “Allah prohibited them to the unbelievers.”
007|051|Those who treated their religion as a pastime and amusement, and whom the worldly life deceived. Today, We will neglect them, as they neglected the meeting of this Day and denied Our signs.
007|052|We provided them with a Scripture which We detailed with knowledge, a guide and mercy for those who believe.
007|053|Are they merely waiting for its interpretation? The day its interpretation comes, those who had previously ignored it will say, “Indeed, the messengers of our Lord came with the truth. Do we have any intercessors who will intercede for us now? Or could we be sent back to behave differently?” They have lost their souls, and what they used to invent has failed them.
007|054|Your Lord is Allah, who created the heavens and the earth in six periods, then He positioned Himself on the throne. He makes the night cover the day, which is in rapid pursuit of it. He made the sun, the moon, and the stars subservient; all are obedient to His command. Blessed is Allah, the Lord of all realms.
007|055|Call upon your Lord humbly and privately. He doesn’t love the transgressors.
007|056|Don’t cause corruption on earth after its reformation. And call upon Him in fear and aspiration. The mercy of Allah is close to those who do good.
007|057|It is He who sends the winds, heralding His mercy. When they carry heavy clouds, We drive them to a lifeless land, and then We release the rain, producing all kinds of fruits. Thus We will bring out the dead; perhaps you will reflect.
007|058|Fertile land yields its produce by its Lord’s permission, while infertile land produces but little. Thus, We diversify the signs for those who are grateful.
007|059|We sent Noah to his people, and he said, “O my people, worship Allah. You have no deity other than Him. I fear for you the punishment of a great day.”
007|060|The chiefs of his people said, “We see you in manifest error.”
007|061|He said, “O my people, there is no error in me. Rather, I am a messenger from the Lord of the worlds.
007|062|I convey to you my Lord’s messages, I offer you sincere advice, and I know from Allah what you don’t know.”
007|063|“Are you astonished that a reminder from your Lord has come to you through one of your own, to warn you and that you may guard yourselves, so that you may receive mercy?”
007|064|But they rejected him, so We saved him and those with him in the Ark, and We drowned those who denied Our revelations. They were blind people.
007|065|To Aad, their brother Hud. He said, “O my people, worship Allah; You have no other god besides Him. Won’t you then be righteous?”
007|066|The disbelieving leaders of his people responded, “We see you as foolish, and we think you’re a liar.”
007|067|He replied, “O my people, I am not foolish; I am a messenger from the Lord of the worlds.
007|068|“I convey to you the messages of my Lord, and I am a reliable counselor for you.”
007|069|“Do you find it strange that a message from your Lord has come to you through a man from amongst you, to warn you? Remember, He made you successors after Noah’s people and increased your stature. Remember Allah’s blessings, so you may thrive.”
007|070|They replied, “Did you come to us to make us worship Allah alone and give up what our fathers worshiped? If you are truthful, bring us what you threaten us with.”
007|071|He replied, “Condemnation and wrath from your Lord have befallen you. Are you arguing with me over names you and your ancestors invented that Allah didn’t authorize? So wait, and I will wait with you.”
007|072|We saved him and those with him by a mercy from Us, and We obliterated those who denied Our signs and were not believers.
007|073|To Thamud, their brother Saleh. He pleaded, “O my people, worship Allah; You have no other god besides Him. A clear sign has come to you from your Lord: this she-camel of Allah is a sign for you. Let her graze on Allah’s earth, and don’t harm her, lest a severe punishment befalls you.”
007|074|“Remember, He made you successors after Aad, and He established you in the land. You construct palaces on its plains and carve out homes in the mountains. Remember Allah’s blessings, and don’t cause corruption in the land.”
007|075|The arrogant leaders among his people said to those oppressed who believed, “Do you believe that Saleh is sent by his Lord?” They replied, “Yes, we believe in the message he brought.”
007|076|The arrogant ones replied, “We reject what you’ve believed in.”
007|077|So, they hamstrung the she-camel, brazenly defying their Lord’s command, and said, “O Saleh, bring upon us what you threaten us with, if you are one of the messengers.”
007|078|So the earthquake seized them, leaving them lifeless in their homes.
007|079|So he turned away from them, saying, “O my people, I have delivered my Lord’s message to you, and I advised you sincerely, but you don’t appreciate advisers.”
007|080|And Lot told his people, “You commit an immorality no one in the world has ever perpetrated before.”
007|081|“You lust after men instead of women. Indeed, you are a people of excess.”
007|082|His people responded, “Expel them from your village; they are purist people.”
007|083|So, We saved him and his family, except for his wife; she was one of those who lingered behind.
007|084|And We rained upon them a downpour. Consider the fate of those who committed wrongdoings.
007|085|To Midian, their brother Shuaib. He said, “O my people, worship Allah; you have no other god but Him. Clear proof has come to you from your Lord. Maintain just measures and weights, do not devalue people’s goods, and don’t spread corruption on earth after it was set right. This is better for you, if only you are believers.”
007|086|“Don’t sit on every trail, intimidating and hindering from the path of Allah those who believe in Him, seeking to make it crooked. Remember when you were few, and He multiplied you. And consider the fate of the wrongdoers.”
007|087|“Given that some of you have believed in what I was sent with, and some haven’t, be patient until Allah renders His judgment between us. He is the best of judges.”
007|088|The arrogant leaders from his community declared, “O Shuaib, we will expel you and those who believed with you from our town, unless you return to our religion.” He responded, “Even against our will?”
007|089|“We would be fabricating a lie against Allah if we returned to your religion after Allah has rescued us from it. It’s not for us to return to it unless Allah, our Lord, permits. Our Lord encompasses everything in His knowledge. In Allah, we’ve placed our trust. Our Lord, decide between us and our people in truth, for You are the best decision maker.”
007|090|The disbelieving elites among his people said, “If you follow Shuaib, you will surely be among the losers.”
007|091|A tremor overtook them, and they lay lifeless in their homes.
007|092|Those who denied Shuai—it is as though they had never thrived there. Those who denied Shuaib—they were the losers.
007|093|Then he turned away from them and said, “O my people, I have conveyed to you my Lord’s messages, and I have advised you. So, How could I grieve for a people who reject faith?”
007|094|Whenever We sent a prophet to a city, We tested its people with adversity and hardship so that they might turn in humility.
007|095|Then, We replaced their hardship with ease until they multiplied and said, “Our ancestors, too, experienced hardship and ease.” Suddenly, We seized them unawares.
007|096|Had the residents of the towns believed and been righteous, We would’ve opened upon them blessings from the sky and the earth. But they denied the truth, so We seized them on account of their misdeeds.
007|097|Are the people of the towns feeling secure from Our punishment coming upon them suddenly at night while they sleep?
007|098|Are the townsfolk carefree that Our punishment won’t come to them in the daytime while they play?
007|099|Do they feel safe from Allah’s scheme? None feel secure from Allah’s scheme except the losers.
007|100|Doesn’t it guide those who inherit the earth after its inhabitants, that if We wish, We could afflict them because of their sins and seal their hearts, so they would not hear?
007|101|These are the towns; We tell you their stories. Their messengers came to them with evident signs, but they would not believe in what they had already rejected. Thus, Allah seals the hearts of the unbelievers.
007|102|We found most of them not true to their commitments; We found most of them sinful.
007|103|Then, after them, We sent Moses with Our signs to Pharaoh and his establishment, but they were unjust toward them. See, then, how was the end of the corrupters.
007|104|Moses said, “O Pharaoh, I am a messenger from the Lord of the worlds.”
007|105|“Rightly so, I can’t say anything other than the truth about Allah. I’ve come to you with clear proof from your Lord, so release the Children of Israel with me.”
007|106|He responded, “If you have a miracle, then present it, if you are truthful.”
007|107|So, he threw down his staff, and behold, it turned into a conspicuous serpent.
007|108|And he exposed his hand, and suddenly, it was white for all to see.
007|109|Pharaoh’s council exclaimed, “This man is a skilled magician!”
007|110|“He intends to expel you from your land; what, then, do you command?”
007|111|They proposed, “Put off him and his brother for some time, and send envoys to the cities.”
007|112|“To gather and bring to you every accomplished magician.”
007|113|So, the magicians arrived at Pharaoh’s presence, and they inquired, “Will we be rewarded if we triumph?”
007|114|He answered, “Yes, and you will be among the ones closest to me.”
007|115|They asked, “O Moses, should you throw first, or should we?”
007|116|He replied, “You throw.” And when they performed their enchantment, they cast a spell upon the people’s eyes, struck fear in their hearts, and exhibited a magnificent spectacle of sorcery.
007|117|Then, We revealed to Moses, “Throw down your staff.” And suddenly, it swallowed the illusions they had fabricated.
007|118|So, the truth was established, and what they were doing became null.
007|119|They were defeated there and then, and were utterly humiliated.
007|120|The magicians fell prostrate.
007|121|They proclaimed, “We have believed in the Lord of the worlds.
007|122|The Lord of Moses and Aaron.”
007|123|Pharaoh said, “You dare to believe in him before I give you permission? You hatched this plot in the city to expel its inhabitants. But you will soon know.”
007|124|“I will sever your hands and feet on opposite sides; then I will crucify you all.”
007|125|They responded, “Indeed, to our Lord we will return.”
007|126|“You are penalizing us merely because we believed in our Lord’s signs when they came to us.” “Our Lord, pour upon us patience and receive our souls in submission.”
007|127|The elite among Pharaoh’s people questioned, “Will you let Moses and his people cause disorder in the land and forsake you and your gods?” He replied, “We will kill their sons and spare their women; we have absolute power over them.”
007|128|Moses said to his people, “Seek help from Allah and be patient. The earth belongs to Allah; He grants it to whomever He wills among His servants. And the end is for the righteous.”
007|129|They replied, “We were oppressed before you came to us and after you arrived.” He replied, “Perhaps your Lord will destroy your enemy and make you inherit the land, then He will observe how you conduct yourselves.”
007|130|We afflicted Pharaoh’s people with drought and crop failure so they might take heed.
007|131|Whenever good fortune came their way, they would say, “This is our due.” But when adversity struck them, they attributed it to an ill omen of Moses and those with him. Surely, their misfortune was ordained by Allah, but most of them know not.
007|132|They said, “Whatever sign you bring to fascinate us, we won’t believe in you.”
007|133|So, We unleashed upon them the flood, locusts, lice, frogs, and blood—all detailed signs. Yet they persisted in arrogance; they were a sinful people.
007|134|Whenever a calamity struck them, they would plead, “O Moses, pray to your Lord for us, under His promise to you. If you lift this affliction from us, we will believe in you and let the Children of Israel go with you.”
007|135|Yet when We removed from them the plague until a term which they should reach, they broke their promise.
007|136|As a result, We exacted retribution from them and drowned them in the sea, for they denied Our signs and paid them no heed.
007|137|We granted the oppressed the inheritance of the Eastern and Western parts of land We had blessed. Thus, the benevolent promise of your Lord to the Children of Israel was fulfilled, in recognition of their patience. And we destroyed what Pharaoh and his people were constructing and what they were establishing.
007|138|We led the Children of Israel across the sea. Upon encountering a people kneeling before their idols, they said, “O Moses, make a god for us, as they have gods.” He responded, “You are truly an ignorant people.”
007|139|“These people are doomed for their destruction, and what they do is futile.”
007|140|He said, “Would I seek for you a god other than Allah, while He has preferred you over the worlds?”
007|141|And remember when We rescued you from Pharaoh’s people, who subjected you to the harshest torment, killing your sons and sparing your women. That was a severe trial from your Lord.
007|142|We set a meeting with Moses for thirty nights, which We completed with another ten; so the term of his Lord was completed in forty nights. Moses instructed his brother Aaron, “Take my place among my people, act rightly, and don’t follow the way of the mischief-makers.”
007|143|When Moses arrived for Our appointment, and his Lord spoke to him, he pleaded, “My Lord, allow me to see You.” He replied, “You won’t see Me, but look at the mountain; if it remains in its place, you’ll see Me.” When his Lord revealed His glory to the mountain, He made it crumble to dust, and Moses fell down fainting. Upon regaining consciousness, he exclaimed, “Glory be to You, I turn to You in repentance, I am the first of the believers.”
007|144|He said, “O Moses, I have chosen you over people by My Messages and My speech. Therefore, take what I’ve given you, and be among the grateful.”
007|145|We inscribed for him on the Tablets comprehensive instructions and detailed explanation for everything. “Adhere to them, and instruct your people to uphold the best of them. I will show you the dwelling of the wicked.”
007|146|I will divert from My signs those who behave arrogantly without right on Earth. Even if they witness every sign, they won’t believe in it. If they see the path of righteousness, they won’t adopt it. But if they see the path of error, they will embrace it. This is because they denied Our signs and remained heedless of them.
007|147|Those who deny Our revelations and the meeting in the Hereafter—their deeds will come to nothing. Won’t they be repaid for what they’ve done?
007|148|In Moses’ absence, his people fabricated a calf from their jewelry—a body that emitted a mooing sound. Couldn’t they see that it could neither speak to them nor guide them on a path? They took it as an object of worship and were in the wrong.
007|149|And when regret overcame them and saw that they were astray, they lamented, “Unless our Lord bestows His mercy upon us and forgives us, we will surely be among the losers.”
007|150|When Moses returned to his people, angered and grieved, he exclaimed, “What a terrible thing you did in my absence! Were you so eager to defy your Lord’s commands?” He threw down the Tablets and seized his brother by the head, dragging him towards himself. He said, “Son of my mother, the people took advantage of my weaknesses and almost killed me. Don’t let the enemies gloat over me, and don’t count me among the wrongdoing people.”
007|151|He prayed, “My Lord, forgive me and my brother, and in Your mercy, admit me and my brother, for You are the most merciful of the merciful.”
007|152|Those who idolized the calf incurred wrath from their Lord, and humiliation in this life. Thus do We recompense the inventors of lies.
007|153|But those who commit misdeeds and then repent and believe—Surely your Lord, after this, is Forgiving, Merciful.
007|154|When Moses’ anger had subsided, he picked up the Tablets; within their engraving was guidance and mercy for those who fear their Lord.
007|155|Moses selected seventy men from his people for Our appointed meeting. When the tremor seized them, he said, “My Lord, if You had willed, You could’ve destroyed them—and me—before. Will You destroy us for the deeds of the foolish among us? This is but Your test, by which You lead astray whom You will and guide whom You will. You are our Protector, so forgive us and have mercy on us. You are the Best of those who forgive.
007|156|Therefore, prescribe for us good in this world and in the Hereafter. We have turned to You.” He replied, “My punishment—I afflict with it whom I wish, but My mercy encompasses all things. I will specify it for those who conduct themselves righteously, give charity, and believe in Our revelations.”
007|157|Those who follow the Messenger, the illiterate prophet, whom they find referenced in their own Torah and Gospel—he guides them towards righteousness, forbids them from evil, permits for them all good things, forbids them from all impure things, and removes from them their burdens and the shackles that had bound them. Those who believe in him, honor him, assist him, and follow the light that was sent down with him—these are the ones who will succeed.
007|158|Say, “O people, I am Allah’s Messenger to you all—to whom belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth. There is no deity except Him; He gives life and causes death.” So, believe in Allah and His Messenger, the Gentile Prophet, who believes in Allah and His words. Follow him, so that you may be guided.
007|159|Among the people of Moses, a community exists that guides with truth and by which they establish justice.
007|160|We divided them into twelve tribes, distinct nations. When his people asked Moses for water, We instructed, “Strike the rock with your staff.” From it, twelve springs gushed forth; each tribe recognized its designated drinking place. We shaded them with clouds and sent down upon them manna and quails: “Eat from the good things We provided you.” They didn’t wrong Us, but they wronged themselves.
007|161|They were instructed, “Settle in this town, eat from it wherever you wish, say, ‘Relinquish,’ and enter the gate humbly; We will forgive your sins and enhance the reward for the doers of good.”
007|162|But the wrongdoers among them changed the words they were given to something different, so We sent down upon them a punishment from the sky due to their wrongdoing.
007|163|Ask them about the town by the sea, where they violated the Sabbath. Fish would surface in abundance on their Sabbath days, but not on the days they didn’t observe the Sabbath. We tested them in this manner due to their defiance.
007|164|Some of them questioned, “Why do you preach to people whom Allah is about to destroy or punish severely?” They replied, “To have an excuse before your Lord, and perhaps they may become righteous.”
007|165|So, when they forgot what they had been reminded of, We saved those who prohibited wrong, and We seized those who did wrong with a severe punishment because they were transgressors.
007|166|And when they continued disregarding the reminders, We said to them, “Be despicable apes.”
007|167|Your Lord declared that He would send against them, until the Day of Resurrection, those who will inflict terrible suffering on them. Your Lord is swift in penalty; but He is also Forgiving, Most Merciful.
007|168|We dispersed them into communities throughout the earth. Some of them are righteous, while some are less so. We tested them with both good and bad circumstances, so they might return.
007|169|After them, succeeded generations who inherited the Scripture, they chose the fleeting pleasures of this world, saying, “We will be forgiven.” And if similar pleasures came their way, they would again seize them. Weren’t they bound by a covenant to uphold the Scripture and to speak nothing but the truth about Allah? Didn’t they study what was in it? The home of the Hereafter is better for the righteous. Don’t you understand?
007|170|Those who adhere to the Scripture and perform prayers—We won’t let the reward of the reformers be lost.
007|171|We held the mountain over them like a canopy, and they feared it would fall upon them. “Hold firmly to what We’ve given you, and remember what’s in it, so you may be protected.”
007|172|And when your Lord took out from the children of Adam—from their loins—their descendants and made them testify of themselves: “Am I not your Lord?” They responded, “Yes, we testify.” Lest you should say on the Resurrection Day, “We were unaware of this.”
007|173|Or lest you say, “It was only that our ancestors associated before, and we were but descendants after them. Will You destroy us because of the deeds of the fabricators?”
007|174|Thus, We detail the verses, so they may return.
007|175|Tell them the story of the one to whom We presented Our signs, but he shrugged them off; thus, Satan followed him, and he became one of the deviants.
007|176|Had We willed, We could’ve raised him by their means, but he clung to the earth and pursued his desires. His example is that of a dog: if you chase him, he pants, or if you leave him, he still pants. That’s the likeness of the people who deny Our verses. So, tell the stories so they may reflect.
007|177|How terrible is the example of the people who deny Our revelations and wrong themselves!
007|178|Whomever Allah guides—he is the guided; and whomever He sends astray—those are the ones who are the losers.
007|179|We’ve destined for Hell many jinns and humans. They have hearts with which they don’t understand, eyes with which they don’t see, and ears with which they don’t hear. They are like cattle; rather, they are more astray. These are the heedless ones.
007|180|To Allah belong the most beautiful names; so call upon Him by them, and avoid those who disrespect His names. They will be recompensed for their deeds.
007|181|Among those We’ve created is a community who guide by truth and by it establish justice.
007|182|Those who reject Our communications—We will lead them gradually from where they don’t know.
007|183|I will give them time. My plan is firm.
007|184|Or don’t they think? There is no madness in their friend. He is but a transparent warner.
007|185|Didn’t they contemplate the dominion of the heavens and the earth, and what Allah created, and that their term might be near? In what statement after this will they believe?
007|186|Whomever Allah misguides—there is no guide for him. And He leaves them in their transgression, wandering blindly.
007|187|They ask you about the Hour, “When will it arrive?” Respond, “The knowledge of it lies only with my Lord. Only He will reveal it when its time comes. It hangs heavily in the heavens and the earth, and it will come upon you only unexpectedly.” They ask you as if you are privy to it. Say, “Only Allah possesses knowledge of it, yet most people are unaware.”
007|188|Say, “I have no power to benefit or harm myself, except as Allah wills. If I knew the unseen, I would’ve acquired much good, and no harm would’ve touched me. I am only a warner and a bearer of good news to those who believe.”
007|189|It is He who created you from a single person, and made its spouse from it, so he might find comfort in her. When he mates with her, she carries a light burden that she can hardly feel. When it becomes heavy, they pray to Allah, their Lord, “If You grant us a healthy child, we will surely be among the grateful.”
007|190|Yet, when He grants them a healthy child, they associate partners to Him in what He gave them. Exalted is Allah, far above the partners they associate with Him.
007|191|Do they ascribe to Him partners who create nothing, yet are themselves created?
007|192|They can’t help them, nor can they help themselves.
007|193|And if you invite them for guidance, they won’t follow you. It is the same whether you call them or you remain silent.
007|194|Those whom you call upon besides Allah are servants like you. So call upon them, and let them respond to you, if you are truthful.
007|195|Do they have legs with which they walk? Or hands with which they strike? Or eyes with which they see? Or ears with which they hear? Say, “Call upon your ‘associates’, then scheme against me, and give me no respite.”
007|196|“My protector is Allah, who revealed the Book, and He protects the righteous.”
007|197|Those you call upon besides Him can’t help you, nor can they help themselves.
007|198|And if you invite them for guidance, they can’t hear. You may see them looking towards you, but they don’t see.
007|199|Accept forgiveness, commend what’s right, and turn away from the ignorant.
007|200|If an evil suggestion from Satan should assault you, seek refuge in Allah. He is All-Hearing, All-Knowing.
007|201|Those who are righteous, when an impulse from Satan strikes them, they remind themselves, and immediately see clearly.
007|202|And their brethren prolong them in error, and then cease not.
007|203|When you don’t bring them a verse, they say, “Why can’t you make one up?” Say, “I only follow what’s revealed to me by my Lord. These are insights from your Lord, and guidance and mercy for people who believe.”
007|204|When the Quran is read, then listen to it attentively, so you may receive mercy.
007|205|And remember your Lord within yourself, with humility and reverence, and without raising your voice, in the morning and the evening, and don’t be among the unmindful.
007|206|Those who are in your Lord’s presence aren’t too proud to worship Him. They glorify Him, and to Him they prostrate.
008|001|They ask you about the spoils. Say, “The spoils belong to Allah and the Messenger.” So fear Allah, settle your disputes, and obey Allah and His Messenger, if you are believers.
008|002|The believers are those whose hearts tremble when Allah is mentioned, whose faith is strengthened when His verses are recited to them, and who trust their Lord.
008|003|Those who perform the prayers and spend from what We provide for them.
008|004|These are the true believers. They have elevated ranks with their Lord, forgiveness, and a generous provision.
008|005|Just as your Lord brought you out of your home truthfully, despite the reluctance of some believers.
008|006|They argued with you about the truth after it had become clear, as if they were driven towards death while they looked on.
008|007|Allah promised you that one of the two parties would be yours, but you wished the unarmed one would be yours. However, Allah wanted to establish the truth by His words, and to root out the unbelievers.
008|008|To confirm the truth and to nullify falsehood, even if the guilty hate it.
008|009|Recall when you implored your Lord for help, He responded, “I am sending you a thousand angels in ranks.”
008|010|Allah made this but good news, and an assurance to your hearts. Victory comes only from Allah. Allah is Mighty and Wise.
008|011|He caused drowsiness to overcome you, granting you tranquility from Himself. He sent down rain from the sky to purify you, to rid you of Satan’s pollution, to strengthen your hearts, and to steady your steps.
008|012|Your Lord inspired the angels: “I am with you, so firm up those who believe. I will instill terror into the hearts of those who disbelieve. Strike at the necks, and strike off every fingertip of theirs.”
008|013|This is because they defied Allah and His Messenger. Whoever defies Allah and His Messenger—surely, Allah is severe in retribution.
008|014|“This is yours, so taste it.” And for the unbelievers is the punishment of the Fire.
008|015|O you who believe, when you confront the unbelievers on the march, never turn your backs to them.
008|016|On that day, whoever turns their back to them—unless maneuvering for battle or intending to join another group—has incurred wrath from Allah, and his abode is Hell, a most terrible destination.
008|017|You didn’t kill them, but it was Allah who killed them. And you threw not when you threw, but it was Allah who threw—to test the believers with a good test from Him. Allah is All-Hearing, All-Knowing.
008|018|Thus, Allah thwarts the schemes of the unbelievers.
008|019|If you seek victory, victory has indeed come to you. If you cease, it’s better for you, but if you return, We too will return. Your forces won’t avail you at all, even if they are numerous. Allah is with the believers.
008|020|O you who believe, obey Allah and His Messenger, and don’t turn away from him while you listen.
008|021|And don’t be like those who say, “We hear,” but they listen not.
008|022|The worst of creatures in the sight of Allah are the deaf and dumb who don’t understand.
008|023|If Allah had found any goodness in them, He would’ve made them hear. Yet, even if He had, they would still have turned away in defiance.
008|024|O you who believe, respond to Allah and the Messenger when he calls you to what gives you life. And know that Allah intervenes between a person and his heart, and that to Him you will be gathered.
008|025|And fear a trial that doesn’t exclusively affect the wrongdoers among you, and know that Allah’s retribution is severe.
008|026|And remember when you were few, weak in the land, fearing that people might abduct you. Then he sheltered you, strengthened you with His victory, and supplied you with good things, so you could express gratitude.
008|027|O you who believe, don’t betray Allah and the Messenger, nor betray your trusts while you know.
008|028|Know that your possessions and your children are a test, and that with Allah, there is a great reward.
008|029|O you who believe, if you fear Allah, He will grant you discernment, purify you of your sins, and forgive you. Allah is of abundant bounty.
008|030|Remember when those who disbelieve planned against you, to capture, to kill, or to expel you. They planned, and Allah planned; but Allah is the best of planners.
008|031|When Our revelations are recited to them, they say, “We’ve heard. If we wanted, we could say the same; these are nothing but myths of the ancients.”
008|032|They also say, “O Allah, if this is the truth from You, then rain down stones from the sky upon us, or inflict upon us a harsh punishment.”
008|033|Allah would not punish them while you are among them, nor would Allah punish them while they are seeking forgiveness.
008|034|Why should Allah not punish them, when they block access to the Sacred Mosque, even though they weren’t its rightful guardians? Its true guardians are the pious, but most don’t know.
008|035|Their prayers at the House are nothing more than whistling and clapping. So, taste the punishment for having disbelieved.
008|036|Those who disbelieve squander their wealth to deter people from Allah’s path. They will continue to spend it, then it will become a source of regret for them. Eventually, they will be defeated, and the unbelievers will be gathered in Hell.
008|037|In order that Allah may distinguish the wicked from the good, stack the wicked upon each other, bundle them together, and cast them into Hell. These are the losers.
008|038|Tell the disbelievers: if they desist, what has passed will be forgiven them. But if they resume, the precedent of the ancients has already been established.
008|039|Fight them until there is no more oppression and religion belongs wholly to Allah. But if they cease, then Allah sees well all that they do.
008|040|Should they turn away, then know that Allah is your Protector. An excellent Protector and an excellent Helper.
008|041|Know that whatever spoils you acquire, a fifth of it is for Allah, the Messenger, the relatives, the orphans, the needy, and the refugees, provided you believe in Allah and in what We revealed to Our servant on the Day of Decisiveness—the day the two forces clashed. Allah has power over all things.
008|042|When you were on the near bank, they were on the far bank, and the caravan was below you. Had you made a mutual appointment, you would’ve failed to keep it. But Allah intended to accomplish a predestined matter, so that those who perished would perish by clear evidence, and those who survived would survive by clear evidence. Allah is All-Hearing, All-Knowing.
008|043|When Allah made them appear few in your dream. Had He shown them to you as numerous, you would’ve faltered and would’ve disputed in the matter. But Allah saved the situation. He knows what lies within hearts.
008|044|When you confronted them, He made them appear fewer in your eyes, and made you appear fewer in their eyes, so that Allah might accomplish a matter already destined. To Allah, all matters are returned.
008|045|O you who believe! When you meet a detachment, stand firm and remember Allah much, so you may succeed.
008|046|Obey Allah and His Messenger, and don’t quarrel, lest you fail and your momentum dissipates. And be patient; Allah is with the patient.
008|047|Don’t be like those who left their homes boastfully, to be seen by people, and to obstruct Allah’s path. Allah encompasses what they do.
008|048|Satan made their deeds seem attractive to them, and said, “No one among the people can defeat you today, and I am by your side.” But, when the two parties sighted each other, he withdrew on his heels and said, “I am innocent of you; I see what you don’t see; I fear Allah, and Allah is severe in penalty.”
008|049|The hypocrites and those with sick hearts said, “Their religion deluded these people.” But whoever relies on Allah—Allah is Mighty and Wise.
008|050|If only you could see, when the angels take the souls of those who disbelieve, striking their faces and their backs: “Taste the suffering of the Blaze.”
008|051|This is because of what your hands sent ahead, and Allah is not unjust to the beings.
008|052|Similar to the situation of Pharaoh’s people and those before them. They denied Allah’s signs, so Allah seized them for their sins. Allah is powerful and severe in penalty.
008|053|This is because Allah would not change a blessing He bestowed upon a people until they change what’s within themselves. Allah is All-Hearing, All-Knowing.
008|054|Similar to the situation of Pharaoh’s people and those before them. They rejected their Lord’s signs, so We destroyed them for their sins, and We drowned Pharaoh’s people. They were all wrongdoers.
008|055|The worst living creatures in Allah’s sight are those who disbelieve; they won’t believe.
008|056|Those with whom you’ve made a treaty, yet they breach their agreement every time—they aren’t righteous.
008|057|If you encounter them in battle, make them a fearsome example for others who follow them, so they may take heed.
008|058|If you fear betrayal from a people, throw back to them on equal terms. Allah doesn’t love the deceitful.
008|059|Let not the unbelievers assume they are ahead. They won’t cause failure.
008|060|Prepare against them all the forces and cavalry you can muster, to frighten thereby Allah’s enemies and your enemies, and others besides them unknown to you, but known to Allah. Whatever you spend in Allah’s way will be repaid to you fully, and you won’t be wronged.
008|061|And if they incline towards peace, incline towards it, and trust in Allah. Indeed He is the All-Hearing, the All-Knowing.
008|062|If they intend to deceive you, then Allah is sufficient for you. It is He who supported you with His help and with the believers.
008|063|And He united their hearts. Had you spent all that’s on earth, you couldn’t have united their hearts, but Allah united them. He is Mighty and Wise.
008|064|O Prophet, suffice yourself with Allah and the believers who follow you.
008|065|O Prophet, rouse the believers to fight. If there are among you twenty who are steadfast, they will defeat two hundred. And if there are a hundred of you, they will defeat a thousand of the unbelievers, for they are a people void of understanding.
008|066|Now, Allah has lightened your burden, knowing that you have a weakness. If there are a hundred steadfast among you, they will defeat two hundred. And if there are a thousand of you, they will defeat two thousand by Allah’s permission. Allah is with the patient.
008|067|It’s not for a prophet to take captives until he has thoroughly subdued the land. You desire the goods of this world, while Allah desires the Hereafter. Allah is Mighty and Wise.
008|068|Were it not for a prior decree from Allah, a severe punishment would’ve touched you for what you’ve taken.
008|069|So consume what you’ve gained, lawful and good, and remain conscious of Allah. Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.
008|070|O Prophet, say to those who are captives in your custody, “If Allah knows any good in your hearts, He will give you something better than what was taken from you, and He will forgive you. Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.”
008|071|If they intend to betray you, they have previously betrayed Allah, and He overpowered them. Allah is Knowing and Wise.
008|072|Those who believed, emigrated, and striven in Allah’s way with their wealth and lives and those who provided shelter and assistance are allies of one another. However, for those who believed and didn’t emigrate, you owe them no protection until they emigrate. However, if they seek your assistance in faith, then you should support them, except against a people with whom you have a treaty. Allah observes all your actions.
008|073|The unbelievers are allies of one another. If you don’t do the same, there will be turmoil on earth and great corruption.
008|074|Those who believed, emigrated, and striven for Allah’s cause and those who provided shelter and aid are the true believers. For them is forgiveness and a generous provision.
008|075|As for those who have believed later, emigrated, and struggled alongside you, they are of you. However, according to the book of Allah, blood relations have precedence. Allah has knowledge of all things.
009|001|A declaration of dissolution from Allah and His Messenger is hereby issued to the polytheists with whom you had entered into a treaty.
009|002|Travel the land freely for four months, but be aware that you can’t evade Allah’s grip, and that Allah will disgrace the disbelievers.
009|003|A proclamation from Allah and His Messenger to all people on the day of the Great Pilgrimage: Allah disowns the polytheists, as does His Messenger. If you repent, it will be good for you, but if you turn away, know that you can’t evade Allah. Inform those who disbelieve of severe punishment.
009|004|However, to those polytheists with whom you’ve made a treaty, and who didn’t violate any of its terms, nor supported anyone against you, complete their treaty until its period. Allah loves the righteous.
009|005|When the Sacred Months have passed, slay the polytheists wherever you find them. Capture them, besiege them, and ambush them at every possible location. However, if they repent, establish prayer, and give in charity, let them go their way. Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.
009|006|If any of the polytheists seeks your protection, grant it to him, so that he may hear the Word of Allah. Then escort him to where he can be safe, for they are a people who lack knowledge.
009|007|How can a treaty exist between Allah and His Messenger and the polytheists, except with those with whom you made a treaty at the Sacred Mosque? As long as they remain upright towards you, remain upright towards them. Allah loves the righteous.
009|008|How can it be when they gain dominance over you, they respect neither kinship nor treaty with you? They appease you with their mouths, but their hearts refuse, and most of them are sinful.
009|009|They sold Allah’s verses for a trivial gain and obstructed His path. How awful is what they’ve been doing.
009|010|Towards a believer, they respect neither kinship nor treaty. These are the aggressors.
009|011|If they repent, establish prayer, and give in charity, then they are your brothers in faith. We explain the verses for people who know.
009|012|However, if they violate their oaths after their treaty, and they attack your religion, then fight the leaders of disbelief, for their oaths are nothing to them, so they may cease.
009|013|Will you not fight against those who broke their oaths, sought to expel the Messenger, and initiated hostilities against you? Do you fear them? Allah is the one you should fear, if you are believers.
009|014|Fight them; Allah will punish them by your hands, disgrace them, give you victory over them, and heal the hearts of a believing people.
009|015|And He makes the anger in their hearts subside. And Allah forgives whomever He wills; Allah is Knowing and Wise.
009|016|Do you think you will be left without Allah distinguishing those among you who strive and form alliances solely with Allah, His Messenger, and the believers? Allah is Acquainted with what you do.
009|017|The polytheists, steadfast in their disbelief, are not fit to maintain Allah’s sanctuaries. Their deeds have become worthless, and they will reside eternally in the Fire.
009|018|Allah’s sanctuaries are only maintained by those who have believed in Allah and the Last Day, establish prayer, give purifying alms, and fear none but Allah. These individuals are most likely to be guided.
009|019|Do you equate providing water to pilgrims and maintaining the Sacred Mosque with those who believe in Allah and the Last Day, and strive in the cause of Allah? They aren’t equal in Allah’s sight. Allah doesn’t guide the unjust people.
009|020|Those who believe, emigrate, and strive with their wealth and lives in Allah’s path hold a higher rank in Allah’s sight. These are the successful ones.
009|021|Their Lord gives them good news of His mercy and approval and gardens where they will enjoy eternal bliss.
009|022|They will abide there forever. With Allah is a great reward.
