009|023|O you who believe, don’t take your parents and siblings as allies if they favor disbelief over faith. Whoever of you does so, those are the wrongdoers.
009|024|Say, “If your parents, children, siblings, spouses, relatives, the wealth you’ve acquired, the business you fear may decline, and the homes you cherish are dearer to you than Allah, His Messenger, and striving in His path, then wait until Allah brings about His decree.” Allah doesn’t guide the sinful people.
009|025|Allah granted you victories in numerous regions, but on the day of Hunain, your vast numbers impressed you, yet they availed you nothing. The earth, vast as it is, seemed to close in on you, and you turned back in retreat.
009|026|Then, Allah sent down His tranquility upon His Messenger and the believers. He sent down forces you didn’t see and tormented those disbelieving. This is the compensation for the unbelievers.
009|027|Afterward, Allah will relent towards whom He wills. Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.
009|028|O you who believe, the Idolaters are impure, so they shouldn’t approach the Sacred Mosque after this year. If you fear financial loss, Allah will enrich you out of His grace, if He wills. Allah is All-Knowing, All-Wise.
009|029|Fight those who don’t believe in Allah or the Last Day from among the People of the Scripture, who don’t forbid what Allah and His Messenger have forbidden, and who don’t embrace the religion of truth, until they pay the tax willingly and feel subdued.
009|030|The Jews say, “Uzair is the son of Allah,” and the Christians say, “The Messiah is the son of Allah.” These are their words; they mimic the utterances of those who disbelieved before. May Allah destroy them; how misguided they are!
009|031|They’ve taken their priests and saints as lords besides Allah; as well as the Messiah, the son of Mary. Yet, they were commanded to worship only One God. There is no god but He. Glory be to Him above what they associate with Him.
009|032|They seek to extinguish Allah’s light with their words, but Allah is insistent upon perfecting His light, despite the hatred of the unbelievers.
009|033|It is He who sent His Messenger with guidance and the religion of truth, to make it prevail over all religions, despite the hatred of the associators.
009|034|O you who believe, many religious leaders and scholars consume people’s wealth wrongfully and deter from the path of Allah. To those who hoard gold and silver, and don’t spend it in Allah’s way, announce to them a painful punishment.
009|035|On the day when it will be heated in the fire of Hell, and with it their foreheads, sides, and backs will be branded: “This is what you hoarded for yourselves, so taste what you hoarded.”
009|036|Since the day Allah created the heavens and the earth, Allah ordained twelve months in a year, four of which are sanctified. This is the correct order, so make no mistake about them. Fight the polytheists collectively, as they fight you collectively, and know that Allah is with the righteous.
009|037|Postponement is an increase in disbelief, leading the unbelievers astray. They permit it one year and forbid it another, to align with the number sanctified by Allah, thus allowing what Allah has prohibited. Their evil deeds are made appealing to them. Allah does not guide the disbelieving people.
009|038|O you who believe, when you’re called to mobilize in Allah’s way, why do you cling heavily to the earth? Do you prefer the worldly life over the Hereafter? The enjoyment of this earthly life, compared to the Hereafter, is insignificant.
009|039|If you don’t mobilize, He will inflict a severe punishment upon you and replace you with another people. And you won’t harm Him in the least. Allah is capable of all things.
009|040|If you don’t support him, Allah has already supported him. When the unbelievers expelled him, he was one of two in the cave; he said to his friend, “Don’t worry, Allah is with us.” Then, Allah sent down His tranquility upon him, reinforced him with troops you didn’t see, and made the word of the unbelievers the lowest, while Allah’s word is the highest. Allah is Mighty and Wise.
009|041|Mobilize, light or heavy, and strive with your wealth and lives in Allah’s cause. This is better for you, if you only knew.
009|042|They would’ve followed you if there had been immediate gain and a short journey, but the distance seemed too great for them. They will swear by Allah, “If we could, we would’ve gone out with you.” They destroy themselves, and Allah knows that they are lying.
009|043|Allah would pardon you! Why did you give them leave before it became clear to you those who were truthful and you knew the liars?
009|044|Those who genuinely believe in Allah and the Last Day wouldn’t seek exemption from striving with their wealth and their lives. Allah is fully aware of the righteous.
009|045|Only those who don’t believe in Allah and the Last Day seek exemption from you. Their hearts are filled with doubt, and they waver in their indecision.
009|046|Had they intended to mobilize, they would’ve made some preparation for it. However, Allah disapproved of their departure, so He held them back, and they were told, “Stay with those who remain behind.”
009|047|Had they mobilized with you, they would’ve only added to your difficulties, spreading rumors and discord among you. Some of you are prone to listen to them. Allah is fully aware of the wrongdoers.
009|048|They sought dissension before and turned matters for you, until the truth emerged, and Allah’s decree prevailed, much to their dismay.
009|049|Among them are those who say, “Please excuse me, and don’t tempt me.” They have already fallen into temptation. Hell will engulf the unbelievers.
009|050|If good fortune comes your way, it troubles them, but if a calamity strikes you, they say, “We had taken our precautions in advance,” and they depart rejoicing.
009|051|Say, “Nothing will happen to us except what Allah has destined for us. He is our Protector. In Allah should the believers place their trust.”
009|052|Say, “You can anticipate for us one of two favorable outcomes, while we await for you either Allah’s punishment or defeat at our hands. So wait; we, too, are waiting.”
009|053|Say, “Spend willingly or unwillingly, it won’t be accepted from you, for you are a wicked people.”
009|054|Their contributions aren’t accepted because they reject Allah and His Messenger. Furthermore, they only attend prayer lazily, and they spend only grudgingly.
009|055|Let not their wealth or their children impress you. Allah intends to torment them with them in this life, and their souls depart while they are unbelievers.
009|056|They swear by Allah that they are of you, but they are not of you. They are people who cause discord.
009|057|If they could find a refuge, a cave, or any place to retreat, they would rush headlong to it.
009|058|Among them are those who criticize you regarding the distribution of alms. If they are given a portion, they are pleased, but if they are not given, they become angry.
009|059|They should be satisfied with what Allah and His Messenger have given them, saying, “Allah is sufficient for us. Allah will grant us from His bounty, and so will His Messenger. We are toward Allah desirous.”
009|060|The charities are for the poor, the needy, its administrators, for reconciling hearts, for the freeing of slaves, for those in debt, for Allah’s cause, and for the homeless. This is a decree from Allah, and Allah is All-Knowing, All-Wise.
009|061|Among them are those who slander the Prophet, saying, “He is all ears.” Say, “He listens for your good. He believes in Allah, trusts the believers, and is a mercy to those who believe among you.” Those who slander Allah’s Messenger, for them is a painful punishment.
009|062|They swear by Allah to appease you. However, it is Allah and His Messenger they should seek to please, if they are believers.
009|063|Don’t they know that whoever opposes Allah and His Messenger, for him is the Fire of Hell, to remain in it eternally? That is the great humiliation.
009|064|The hypocrites are apprehensive that a Chapter may be revealed that will inform them of what’s in their hearts. Say, “Mock on, but Allah will expose what you fear.”
009|065|If you question them, they will say, “We were only conversing and playing.” Say, “Do you make a mockery of Allah, His revelations, and His Messenger?”
009|066|Make no excuses. You have disbelieved after your belief. Should we forgive some of you, we will punish others: they have been guilty sinners.
009|067|The hypocritical men and women are akin to one another. They order what is wrong, forbid what is right, and they close their hands. They forgot Allah, so He disregards them. The hypocrites are the sinners.
009|068|Allah has promised the hypocrites, men and women, and the unbelievers the Fire of Hell, where they will dwell forever. It is their just compensation. Allah has cursed them, and they will endure perpetual torment.
009|069|They are like those before you who were stronger, wealthier, and had more offspring. They enjoyed their own benefit, and you’ve enjoyed your own benefit, and you indulged the same as they indulged. Their deeds have become worthless in this world and the Hereafter. They are the losers.
009|070|Didn’t they hear the stories of their predecessors—the people of Noah, Aad, Thamud, the people of Abraham, the inhabitants of Midian, and the Overturned Cities? Their messengers came to them with clear signs. Allah didn’t wrong them, it was themselves they wronged.
009|071|The believing men and women are allies of one another. They advocate righteousness, forbid evil, establish prayer, give in charity, and obey Allah and His Messenger. Those—Allah will have mercy on them. Allah is Mighty and Wise.
009|072|Allah promised the believing men and women gardens through which rivers flow, where they will abide forever, and beautiful mansions in the Gardens of Eternity. But the greatest of all is Allah’s approval. This is the ultimate triumph.
009|073|O Prophet, strive against the unbelievers and the hypocrites, and be harsh with them. Their ultimate abode is Hell—a terrible destination.
009|074|They swear by Allah that they said nothing, yet they did utter words of disbelief and renounced faith after their submission. They plotted things beyond their reach. Their resentment only arises because Allah and His Messenger have enriched them through His favor. If they repent, it will be better for them. But if they turn away, Allah will severely punish them in this world and the Hereafter. They will have no protector or helper on earth.
009|075|Among them are those who pledged to Allah: “If he gives us from his bounty, we will give in charity and be among the righteous.”
009|076|Yet, when He bestowed His bounty upon them, they were stingy with it, turned their backs, and distanced themselves.
009|077|Thus, He punished them with hypocrisy in their hearts, until the Day they will meet Him, due to their breach of their promise to Allah and their dishonesty.
009|078|Don’t they know that Allah knows their secrets and their private conversations, and that Allah is the Knower of the unseen?
009|079|Those who criticize the believers who willingly give out in charity, and ridicule those who find nothing to give except their own efforts, Allah will ridicule them, and they will have a painful punishment.
009|080|Whether you ask forgiveness for them or not, even if you were to ask for it seventy times, Allah will not forgive them. This is because they denied Allah and His Messenger. Allah doesn’t guide the immoral people.
009|081|Those who stayed behind rejoiced in staying behind the Messenger of Allah, and they disliked striving with their wealth and lives in Allah’s cause. They said, “Don’t venture out in the heat.” Say, “The fire of Hell is hotter still—if only they could understand.”
009|082|So let them laugh a little and cry much as recompense for what they used to earn.
009|083|If Allah returns you to a group of them, and they ask for your permission to go out, say, “You will never march with me, nor will you fight an enemy with me. You were content to remain inactive the first time, so stay with those who stay behind.”
009|084|Never pray for any of them who dies, nor shall you stand at his graveside. They denied Allah and His Messenger, and they died while they were sinners.
009|085|Let not their wealth and their children impress you. Allah wants to punish them via them in this life, and their souls pass away while they are unbelievers.
009|086|When a chapter is revealed, stating: “Believe in Allah and strive with His Messenger,” the affluent among them ask for your exemption, saying, “Let us be with those who stay behind.”
009|087|They are content to be with those who stay behind; their hearts were sealed, so they don’t understand.
009|088|However, the Messenger and those who believed with him strive with their wealth and their lives. For these will be the good things, and it is they who will be successful.
009|089|Allah has prepared for them gardens under which rivers flow, wherein they will abide forever. That’s the supreme success.
009|090|Some Desert Arabs came with excuses, seeking an exemption, and those who lied to Allah and His Messenger sat. A painful punishment will strike those among them who disbelieved.
009|091|There is no blame upon the weak, nor upon the sick, nor upon those who find nothing to spend, provided they are true toward Allah and His messenger. There is no blame on those who do good. Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.
009|092|Nor on those who, when they came to you asking to be transported, and you said, “I have nothing to transport you on,” they turned away, their eyes overflowing with tears out of sadness that they couldn’t find the means to spend.
009|093|The blame lies only with those who ask your permission while they are wealthy. They prefer to remain with those who stay behind, and Allah has sealed their hearts, leaving them devoid of understanding.
009|094|They will make excuses to you when you return to them. Say, “Don’t make excuses; we won’t believe you. Allah has informed us of your intentions. Allah and His Messenger will observe your actions, and you will be returned to the Knower of the unseen and the seen, who will inform you of everything you did.”
009|095|Upon your return to them, they will swear by Allah, hoping you will accept their excuses. Distance yourself from them, for they are impure, and their dwelling is Hell—a just compensation for their actions.
009|096|They swear to you to gain your approval, but even if you approve of them, Allah doesn’t approve of the sinful people.
009|097|The Desert Arabs are the staunchest in disbelief and hypocrisy, and least likely to know the boundaries that Allah revealed to His Messenger. Allah is All-Knowing, All-Wise.
009|098|Among the Desert Arabs, some consider what they spend as a loss, and they await misfortunes to befall you. Yet, they will be afflicted by misfortunes. Allah is All-Hearing, All-Knowing.
009|099|However, among the Desert Arabs are those who believe in Allah and the Last Day, and regard their contributions as a means to draw closer to Allah, and the prayers of the Messenger. Indeed, it will bring them nearer, and Allah will admit them into His mercy. Allah is Forgiving, Most Merciful.
009|100|The pioneers—the first of the Emigrants and the Helpers—and those who followed them in goodness: Allah is pleased with them, and they are pleased with Him. He prepared for them Gardens through which rivers flow, where they will dwell forever. This is the supreme achievement.
009|101|Among the Desert Arabs around you, some are hypocrites, as well as among the city dwellers. They are persistent in hypocrisy. You don’t know them, but We certainly do. We will punish them twice; then they will be returned to a severe punishment.
009|102|And there are those who admit their sins, and they have mixed a righteous deed with another that was bad. Perhaps Allah will relent towards them. Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.
009|103|Receive from their wealth a charity to purify and cleanse them, and pray for them. Your prayers bring them tranquility. Allah is All-Hearing, All-Knowing.
009|104|Don’t they know that it is Allah who accepts repentance from His beings and receives charities, and that it is Allah who is the Acceptor of repentance and the Merciful?
009|105|Say, “Work! Allah will see your work and so will His Messenger and the believers. Then you will be returned to the Knower of the unseen and the seen, and He will inform you of everything you did.”
009|106|And others deferred to the decree of Allah, whether He will punish them or whether He will forgive them. Allah is All-Knowing, All-Wise.
009|107|Those who have established a mosque with the intent to cause harm, promote disbelief, sow discord among believers, and as an outpost for those who have previously waged war against Allah and His Messenger, they will swear, “we intended nothing but good.” Still, Allah bears witness that they are liars.
009|108|Don’t ever stand therein. A mosque established on righteousness from its very beginning is more deserving of your attendance. Within it are men who love to purify themselves, and Allah loves those who purify themselves.
009|109|Is one who lays the foundation of his building based on righteousness and seeking Allah’s approval better, or one who erects his building on the brink of a collapsing cliff that collapses with him into the fire of Hell? Allah does not guide the wrongdoing people.
009|110|The building which they built won’t cease to be a cause of skepticism in their hearts, until their hearts are cut. Allah is All-Knowing, All-Wise.
009|111|Allah has bought from the believers their lives and their wealth because Paradise is for them. They fight for Allah’s cause. They slay and are slain. This promise is binding on Him in the Torah, the Gospel, and the Quran. Who is more faithful to his covenant than Allah? So, rejoice in the deal you’ve made. This is the ultimate triumph.
009|112|Those who repent, worship, praise, journey, bow down, prostrate themselves, advocate for righteousness, forbid evil, and observe Allah’s limits—give good news to the believers.
009|113|It’s not for the Prophet and the believers to seek forgiveness for the polytheists, even if they were their relatives, after it became clear to them that they are inhabitants of the blazing Fire.
009|114|Abraham’s plea for his father’s forgiveness was only due to a promise he had made to him. But when it became clear to him that he is an enemy to Allah, he dissociated himself from him. Abraham was compassionate and forbearing.
009|115|Allah wouldn’t misguide a people after He has guided them, until He has made clear to them what they should avoid. Allah is knowledgeable of all things.
009|116|To Allah belongs the kingdom of the heavens and the earth; He gives life and causes death. You have no protector or helper other than Allah.
009|117|Allah accepted the repentance of the Prophet, the emigrants, and the helpers who followed him during the hour of difficulty, after the hearts of a group of them had almost deviated. Then, He accepted their repentance. He is Kind and Merciful towards them.
009|118|Also, the three were left behind; until, the earth, in all its vastness, became constricted for them, and their souls became narrowed for them, and they realized that there was no refuge from Allah, except toward Him. Then, He turned to them in mercy so they could repent. Allah is the Acceptor of Repentance, the Most Merciful.
009|119|O you who believe, fear Allah, and be among the truthful.
009|120|It’s not for the inhabitants of the city and the Desert Arabs around them to stay behind Allah’s Messenger, or to prefer themselves over him. Because they don’t suffer from thirst, fatigue, or hunger striving in the cause of Allah, nor take a step that infuriates the unbelievers, nor gain any advantage over an enemy, but it is recorded for them as a righteous deed. Truly, Allah does not waste the reward of those who do good.
009|121|No expenditure they make, small or large, or any ground they march across, will go unrecorded for them. Allah will reward them according to the best of their deeds.
009|122|It is not for the believers to march out altogether. From every division that sets out, a group from each division should remain behind to gain knowledge in the religion, and to warn their people when they return to them, so they may beware.
009|123|O you who believe, fight those of the unbelievers who attack you, and let them find harshness in you; and know that Allah is with the righteous.
009|124|Whenever a chapter is revealed, some of them ask, “Which of you has this increased in faith?” As for those who have believed, it increases their faith and they are rejoicing.
009|125|But as for those in whose hearts is disease, it increases their filth to their filth; and they die while they are unbelievers.
009|126|Don’t they see that they are tested once or twice every year? They still neither repent, nor do they remember.
009|127|Whenever a chapter is revealed, they glance at each other, asking, “Does anyone see you?” Then, they turn away. Allah has turned their hearts away, because they are a people who don’t understand.
009|128|There has come to you a messenger from among yourselves. Your hardship distresses him; he is deeply concerned for you; to the believers, he is kind and merciful.
009|129|But if they turn away, say, “Allah is sufficient for me. There is no god but He. On Him I have relied, and He is the Lord of the Grand Throne.”
010|001|Alif. Lam. Ra. These are the verses of the Wise Book.
010|002|Is it a wonder to people that We revealed to a man from among them: “Warn humankind, and give good news to those who believe that they have a sure footing with their Lord?” Yet the unbelievers say, “This is definitely an obvious magician.”
010|003|Your Lord is Allah, who created the heavens and the earth in six periods, then established Himself on the Throne, governing all affairs. There is no intercessor except after His permission. That is Allah, your Lord, so worship Him. Will you not reflect?
010|004|To Him is your return, all of you. The promise of Allah is true. He originates creation, then He repeats it, to reward those who believe and perform righteous deeds with justice. But for those who disbelieve, for them is a drink of boiling water and painful punishment due to their denial.
010|005|It is He who made the sun shining and the moon luminous, and determined its phases, so you may calculate the years and the passage of time. Allah didn’t create this except with truth. He explains the signs in detail for people who know.
010|006|In the alternation of night and day, and in what Allah created in the heavens and the earth, are signs for people who are mindful.
010|007|Those who don’t anticipate meeting Us and are content with life in this world, feel safe in it, and are ignorant of Our signs.
010|008|For them, their refuge will be the Fire, because of what they used to earn.
010|009|But for those who believe and perform righteous deeds, their Lord will guide them by their faith. Rivers will flow beneath them in the Gardens of Bliss.
010|010|Their prayer therein will be, “Glorified are You, O Allah,” and their greeting therein will be, “Peace.” And the conclusion of their prayer will be, “Praise be to Allah, the Lord of the universes.”
010|011|If Allah were to hasten evil for people, as they hasten good, their time would have been over. But We leave those who don’t look forward to meeting Us in their transgressions, blundering.
010|012|When adversity touches a person, he prays to Us, whether lying on his side, sitting, or standing. But when We remove his adversity, he proceeds as if he had not reached out to Us in a predicament. Thus, the deeds of the transgressors are made to appear pleasing to them.
010|013|We destroyed generations before you when they committed injustices. Their messengers had come to them with clear proofs, but were not going to believe. Thus do We recompense the guilty people.
010|014|Then We made you successors in the earth after them—to see how you will behave.
010|015|When Our clear verses are conveyed to them, those who don’t expect to meet Us say, “Bring us a Quran other than this, or change it.” Say, “It’s not for me to modify it of my own. I only follow what’s revealed to me. Should I disobey my Lord, I fear the punishment of a great Day.”
010|016|Say, “Had Allah willed, I wouldn’t have conveyed it to you, nor would He have made it known to you. I have lived among you a lifetime before it; will you not use your reason?”
010|017|Who is more unjust than he who invents a lie about Allah or denies His signs? Surely, the transgressors won’t succeed.
010|018|They worship, aside from Allah, what can neither harm them nor benefit them, and they say, “These are our intercessors with Allah.” Say, “Are you informing Allah of something He doesn’t know in the heavens or on earth?” Glorified is He and far above what they associate with Him.
010|019|Humanity was once a single community, before differences emerged. If not for a prior decree from your Lord, their disputes would’ve been settled.
010|020|They say, “If only a miracle from his Lord would come to him.” Say, “The unseen belongs to Allah. So wait; I am waiting with you.”
010|021|When We grant humans mercy after hardship has touched them, they scheme against Our revelations. Say, “Allah is swifter in planning.” Indeed, Our messengers write down what you scheme.
010|022|It is He who transports you across land and sea. When you are aboard ships, sailing with a favorable wind, rejoicing in it, a gale strikes. The waves come at them from every side, and they think they are encompassed, they call upon Allah, devoting their religion sincerely to Him: “If You save us from this, we will surely be among the thankful.”
010|023|But when He saves them, they transgress unjustly on earth. O people, your transgression is only against yourselves—the enjoyment of worldly life. Then, to Us is your return, and We will inform you of what you used to do.
010|024|The likeness of the life of this world is as water which We send down from the sky; it mingles with the earth’s vegetation from which people and animals eat. But when the earth takes on its adornment and is beautified, and its people think they have mastery over it, Our order comes to it, by night or by day, and We render it a harvested field, as if it had not flourished the day before. So do We explain the verses for a people who ponder.
010|025|Allah invites to the Home of Peace and guides whom He wills to a straight path.
010|026|For those who do good, there is excellence, and more. No darkness will cover their faces, nor will they be humiliated. These are the inhabitants of Paradise, dwelling therein forever.
010|027|Those who commit evil will be repaid with an equivalent evil, and humiliation will cover them. They will have no one to protect them from Allah—as if their faces are covered with pieces of the pitch-dark night. These are the inhabitants of the Fire, where they will abide eternally.
010|028|On the Day when We gather them all together, We will say to those who associated, “Stay in your place, you and your partners.” We will separate between them, and their partners will say, “It wasn’t us you were worshiping.”
010|029|“Allah is sufficient as a witness between us and you; we were unaware of your worship.”
010|030|There, every soul will be recompensed for its deeds. They will be returned to Allah, their Lord, the True, and the false gods they invented will vanish from them.
010|031|Ask them, “Who sustains you from the heavens and the earth? Who controls hearing and sight? Who brings the living from the dead, and the dead from the living? Who orchestrates all affairs?” They will answer, “Allah.” Then say, “Won’t you be cautious?”
010|032|This is Allah, your true Lord. What is there beyond truth except falsehood? How are you then turned away?
010|033|Thus is the word of your Lord justified against those who sin: they don’t believe.
010|034|Say, “Can any of your associates initiate creation and then repeat it?” Say, “Allah initiates creation and then repeats it. How are you led astray?”
010|035|Say, “Can any of your associates guide to the truth?” Say, “Allah alone guides to the truth. Is He who guides to the truth more deserving of being followed, or he who does not guide unless he himself is guided? What is wrong with you? How do you judge?”
010|036|The majority of them follow nothing but conjecture, which can never replace the truth. Allah is aware of what they do.
010|037|This Quran could not have been fabricated by someone other than Allah. It confirms what came before it and thoroughly explains the Scripture. There is no doubt about it; it is from the Lord of the universes.
010|038|Or do they say, “He made it up”? Say, “Then produce a chapter like it, and call upon anyone you can, other than Allah, if you are truthful.”
010|039|They reject what they can’t comprehend, even before its interpretation reaches them. Likewise, those before them also rejected the truth. So, observe the fate of the wrongdoers.
010|040|Among them are those who believe in it, and those who don’t. Your Lord knows best about the corruptors.
010|041|If they accuse you of lying, say, “For me are my deeds, and for you are yours. You are innocent of what I do, and I am innocent of what you do.”
010|042|Among them are those who listen to you. But can you make the deaf hear, even though they can’t comprehend?
010|043|Among them are those who look at you. But can you guide the blind, even if they can’t see?
010|044|Allah doesn’t do any injustice to people, instead, people do injustice to themselves.
010|045|On the Day when He gathers them all, it will seem as if they had only lingered for an hour of a day, familiarizing themselves with each other. Those who denied the encounter with Allah and were not guided will be the ones to suffer loss.
010|046|Whether We show you some of what We’ve promised them, or We take your life before that, their ultimate return is to Us. Then, Allah is the Witness over what they do.
010|047|Every nation has a messenger. When their messenger arrives, judgment is passed upon them justly, and they won’t be wronged.
010|048|They inquire, “When will this promise be fulfilled, if you are truthful?”
010|049|Reply, “I have no control over any harm or benefit to myself, except as Allah wills. For every nation, there is a predetermined time. When their time arrives, they can neither delay it by an hour nor advance it.”
010|050|Say, “Have you considered: whether His punishment comes to you by night or by day, how much of it will the criminals seek to hasten?”
010|051|“Will you only believe when it happens? Now? Even though you were impatient for it?”
010|052|Then, those who acted unjustly will be told, “Taste the everlasting torment. Are you being compensated except for what you used to earn?”
010|053|They question you, “Is this the truth?” Respond, “Yes, by my Lord, it’s the truth, and you can’t escape from it.”
010|054|If every wrongdoer possessed all that exists on earth, he would seek to ransom himself by it. Yet, when they witness the punishment, they will conceal their regret. They will be judged justly, and they won’t be wronged.
010|055|Unquestionably! All that’s in the heavens and on earth belongs to Allah. Indeed, the promise of Allah is always true, yet most of them don’t have the knowledge.
010|056|It is He who gives life and causes death, and to Him you will be returned.
010|057|O mankind, there has come to you advice from your Lord and healing for what’s in the hearts, and guidance and mercy for the believers.
010|058|Say, “In the grace and mercy of Allah, let them rejoice. It is better than what they hoard.”
010|059|Say, “Did you consider what Allah sent down to you of provision, and yet you’ve made some of it lawful and some of it unlawful?” Ask, “Does Allah give you permission, or are you inventing lies about Allah?”
010|060|What will those who fabricate falsehoods about Allah think on Resurrection Day? Allah is bountiful towards humankind, but most of them aren’t grateful.
010|061|Whatever activity you conduct, any portion of the Quran you recite, or whatever you are doing, We are witness over you when you are engaged in it. Not even an atom’s weight in the earth or sky escapes your Lord’s knowledge, nor is there anything smaller or larger that isn’t documented in a clear record.
010|062|Indeed, Allah’s allies will have no fear, nor will they grieve.
010|063|Those who believe and are righteous.
010|064|There is good news for them in this life and the Hereafter. Allah’s promises are unchangeable. That is the supreme victory.
010|065|Let not their words dishearten you. All power and honor belong to Allah; He is the All-Hearing, the All-Knowing.
010|066|Everything in the heavens and earth belongs to Allah. Those who invoke others besides Allah aren’t truly following associates; they follow nothing but conjecture and what their own selves desire.
010|067|It is He who made the night for your rest and the day making things visible. In this are signs for those who listen.
010|068|They say, “Allah has begotten a son.” Glorified is He; He is the Self-Sufficient. Everything in the heavens and on earth is His. Do you have any evidence for this, or are you attributing what you don’t know to Allah?
010|069|Say, “Those who fabricate lies about Allah won’t succeed.”
010|070|Some enjoyment in this life, but they will ultimately return to Us, and We will subject them to severe punishment for their disbelief.
010|071|Tell them the story of Noah, who said to his people, “O my people, if my presence among you and my reminders of Allah’s messages are burdensome to you, I have placed my trust in Allah. So, gather your plan, with your associates, make your intentions clear, and don’t hesitate.”
010|072|“If you turn away, I didn’t ask you for any wage; my reward is only from Allah, and I was commanded to be among those who submit.”
010|073|Yet, they rejected him. So, We saved him and those with him in the Ark, made them successors, and drowned those who denied Our revelations. Observe the end of those who were warned.
010|074|After him, We sent other messengers to their peoples, and they came to them with clear proofs. But they were not to believe what they had initially denied. Thus, We seal over the hearts of the transgressors.
010|075|Then, after them, We sent Moses and Aaron, with Our signs, to Pharaoh and his chiefs. But they showed arrogance, and they were indeed a criminal people.
010|076|When the truth from Us came to them, they said, “This is nothing but clear magic.”
010|077|Moses replied, “Do you call the truth magic when it comes to you? Magicians won’t succeed.”
010|078|They said, “Did you come to divert us from the traditions of our ancestors and gain supremacy in the land? We will never believe in you.”
010|079|Pharaoh then commanded, “Bring to me every knowledgeable sorcerer.”
010|080|When the magicians came, Moses said to them, “Throw down whatever you will.”
010|081|And when they cast their spells, Moses said, “What you’ve produced is a mere illusion, and Allah will nullify it. Allah doesn’t let the work of the corrupters succeed.”
010|082|“Allah confirms the truth with His words, even if the wrongdoers hate it.”
010|083|Only a minority from his own people believed in Moses, fearing Pharaoh’s tyranny and his priests’ retribution. Pharaoh was arrogant in the land, and he was one of the transgressors.
010|084|Moses urged, “O my people, if you have believed in Allah, then rely upon Him, if you have submitted.”
010|085|They responded, “In Allah, we place our trust. Our Lord, make us not a trial for the wrongdoing people.”
010|086|“And, through Your mercy, deliver us from the disbelieving people.”
010|087|We revealed to Moses and his brother: “Establish homes in Egypt for your people, make your homes places of worship, perform the prayers, and give good news to the believers.”
010|088|Moses prayed: “Our Lord, You’ve given Pharaoh and his elites splendor and wealth in the worldly life, our Lord, that they may lead people astray from your path. Our Lord, obliterate their wealth and harden their hearts, so they won’t believe until they witness the severe punishment.”
010|089|He replied, “Your prayer has been answered. Remain upright, and don’t follow the path of those who lack knowledge.”
010|090|We led the Children of Israel across the sea, while Pharaoh and his troops pursued them with hostility and aggression. When the certainty of drowning dawned upon him, he said, “I believe that there is no god except the One in whom the Children of Israel believe, and I am among the submitters.”
010|091|Now? And before you were disobeying and were among the corrupters?
010|092|Today, We will preserve your body, as a sign for those who come after you. Yet most people are oblivious to Our signs.
010|093|We granted the Children of Israel a privileged status and gave them good things. However, they didn’t differ until after knowledge had come to them. Your Lord will resolve their disputes on Resurrection Day.
010|094|If you doubt what We’ve revealed to you, ask those who have been reading the Scripture before you. The truth has come to you from your Lord, so don’t be among the doubters.
010|095|And don’t be among those who deny Allah’s messages, lest you be among the losers.
010|096|Those upon whom your Lord’s decree has been realized won’t believe.
010|097|Even if every sign were to come to them—until they see the severe punishment.
010|098|No community has ever believed and benefited from their faith except the people of Jonah. When they believed, We lifted from them the torment of disgrace in this worldly life, and We permitted them to enjoy for a while.
010|099|If your Lord had willed, everyone on earth would have believed. Would you then compel people to become believers?
010|100|No soul can believe except by the permission of Allah. And He places defilement upon those who don’t reason.
010|101|Say, “Observe what’s in the heavens and the earth.” But neither signs nor warnings will avail those who don’t believe.
010|102|Do they expect anything but the likes of the days of those who passed before them? Say, “Then wait; I am waiting with you.”
010|103|Thus, We rescue Our messengers and those who believe. Thus, it is incumbent upon Us to save the believers.
010|104|Say, “O people, if you doubt my religion, I don’t worship those whom you worship besides Allah, but I worship Allah, who ultimately takes your life. I have been commanded to be among the believers.”
010|105|Be upright to the religion of pure monotheism, and never count yourself among the polytheists.
010|106|Don’t call upon entities other than Allah, who can neither benefit nor harm you. If you do so, you position yourself with the wrongdoers.
010|107|If Allah touches you with harm, there is no one to remove it but Him. And if He intends goodness for you, there is none who can repel His Favor. He bestows it upon whom He wills of His servants. He is the Forgiving, the Merciful.
010|108|Say, “O people, the truth has come to you from your Lord. He who accepts guidance, does so for his own good; he who goes astray, does so at his own peril. I am not a manager over you.”
010|109|Follow what has been revealed to you, and be patient until Allah brings about His judgment. He is the best of judges.
011|001|Alif. Lam. Ra. A Book whose verses were perfected, then detailed, from the One who is All-Wise, All-Knowing.
011|002|Worship none but Allah. “I am to you from Him a warner, and a bearer of good news.”
011|003|“Seek forgiveness from your Lord and repent to Him. He will grant you enjoyment of good for a time appointed, and bestow His grace on every possessor of grace. But if you turn away, I fear for you the punishment of a momentous Day.”
011|004|To Allah is your return, and He is capable of everything.
011|005|They conceal their inner selves as if to hide from Him. Even when they cover themselves with their clothes, He knows what they conceal and disclose. He is aware of what lies within the hearts.
011|006|Every living being on earth depends on Allah for its sustenance. He knows its dwelling and its repository. All is in a clear record.
011|007|It is He who created the heavens and the earth in six periods while His throne was upon the water, to test who among you is best in conduct. If you say, “You will be resurrected after death,” those who disbelieve will say, “This is nothing but obvious sorcery.”
011|008|If We postpone their punishment until a set time, they will question, “What holds it back?” On the day it reaches them, it won’t be averted from them, and they will be trapped by what they used to ridicule.
011|009|If We give man a taste of mercy from Us, and then We withdraw it from him, he is despairing and ungrateful.
011|010|But if We let him taste a favor after hardship has touched him, he will say, “Gone are afflictions from me.” He becomes joyful and proud.
011|011|Except for those who are patient and do righteous deeds—for them is forgiveness and a great reward.
011|012|Perhaps you would leave some of what’s revealed to you, and you may be disheartened because they say, “Why has no treasure been sent down to him?” or “An angel came with him?” You are just a warner, and Allah is a custodian over everything.
011|013|Or do they say, “He made it up?” Say, “Then produce ten similar chapters, made up, and call upon whomsoever you can—excluding Allah—if you are truthful.”
011|014|If they don’t respond to you, then know that it was revealed with Allah’s knowledge, and that there is no god except Him. So, will you then not surrender?
011|015|Those who desire the worldly life and its adornments—We will pay them fully for their deeds in it, without any reduction.
011|016|These are the ones, who, in the Hereafter, will have nothing but the Fire. Their efforts will have been wasted, and their actions become void.
011|017|Is one who relies on clear evidence from his Lord, reinforced by testimony from Him? Before this, the Scripture of Moses for guidance and mercy, and they believe in it. But whoever denies it from the factions, the Fire is his promised destination. So, don’t doubt it. It’s the truth from your Lord, but most people refuse to believe.
011|018|Who is more unjust than one who invents a lie against Allah? These will be presented before their Lord, and the witnesses will proclaim, “These are the ones who lied concerning their Lord.” Behold, the curse of Allah is upon the wrongdoers.
011|019|Those who deter others from Allah’s path, seek to twist it, and they are unbelievers in the Hereafter.
011|020|They will find no escape on earth, nor any protectors apart from Allah. For them, the punishment will be multiplied, as they could not hear, and they could not see.
011|021|These are the ones who have lost their souls, and the illusions they invented have vanished from them.
011|022|Indeed, in the Hereafter, they will be the greatest losers.
011|023|As for those who believe, do righteous deeds, and humble themselves before their Lord, they will be the inhabitants of Paradise, residing there forever.
011|024|Consider the two groups: one is blind and deaf, while the other can see and hear. Are they equal in comparison? Will you not think?
011|025|We sent Noah to his people, saying, “I am a clear warner to you.”
011|026|“Worship none but Allah. I fear for you the torment of a painful Day.”
011|027|The disbelieving nobles among his people responded, “We see you as nothing more than a man like us, and only the most inferior among us, those lacking in judgment, follow you. We see no advantage in you over us; in fact, we think you are liars.”
011|028|He replied, “O my people, what if I am backed by clear evidence from my Lord, and He bestowed His mercy upon me, yet you fail to recognize it? Can we impose it upon you against your will?”
011|029|“O my people, I ask no reward from you; my reward is only from Allah. I will not drive away those who have believed. They are going to meet their Lord. But I see that you are a people steeped in ignorance.”
011|030|“O my people, who would support me against Allah if I drove them away? Will you not then mind?”
011|031|“I don’t pretend to hold the treasures of Allah, nor to know the unseen, and I don’t claim to be an angel. I don’t say that Allah won’t bless those you scorn. Allah knows what’s in their hearts. If I were to do so, I would be among the wrongdoers.”
011|032|They replied, “O Noah, you’ve debated with us extensively. Now bring upon us what you threaten us with, if you are truthful.”
011|033|He replied, “Only Allah can bring it upon you, if He wills, and you won’t be able to evade it.”
011|034|“Even if I were to advise you earnestly, my advice wouldn’t benefit you should Allah intend to misguide you. He is your Lord, and to Him, you will be returned.”
011|035|If they accuse you of making it up, say, “If I made it up, then the sin rests upon me, and I am innocent of the sins you commit.”
011|036|It was communicated to Noah, “None of your people will believe, except those who have already believed; therefore, don’t be disheartened by their actions.”
011|037|“And build the Ark under Our observation and Our inspiration, and don’t address Me concerning those who have wronged; they are to be drowned.”
011|038|While he was constructing the Ark, the leaders of his people would mock him whenever they passed by. He would respond, “If you ridicule us, we too will ridicule you, just as you ridicule us.”
011|039|“You will certainly know who will face humiliating punishment and on whom will descend a lasting penalty.”
011|040|When Our decree came to pass, and the volcano erupted, We instructed, “Load onto it a pair of every kind, along with your family—except for the condemned—and the believers.” Yet, only a few believed with him.
011|041|He declared, “Embark! In the name of Allah, its course and anchorage. My Lord is Forgiving and Merciful.”
011|042|And so, it sailed with them amidst waves as mountains. Noah called out to his son, who was separate from them, “O my son, come aboard with us, and don’t be with the unbelievers.”
011|043|He replied, “I will seek refuge on a mountain; it will protect me from the water.” He said, “Today, there is no protection against Allah’s decree, except for those who receive His mercy.” And the waves surged between them, and he was among the drowned.
011|044|Then the command was issued, “O Earth, absorb your water,” and “O Sky, clear away.” The water receded, the event was concluded, and it settled on Mount Judi. And it was declared, “Away with the wrongdoing people!”
011|045|Noah called out to his Lord, and said, “My Lord, my son is of my family. Your promise is true, and You are the most fair of all judges.”
011|046|He responded, “O Noah, he is not of your family; he is of unrighteous conduct. Don’t ask Me about what you don’t know. I admonish you so that you don’t be among the ignorant.”
011|047|He pleaded, “O my Lord, I seek refuge in You from asking You about what I don’t understand. If you don’t forgive me and show me mercy, I will be among the losers.”
011|048|It was said, “O Noah, disembark in peace from Us, and blessings upon you, and upon nations who are with you. But to other nations, we will give enjoyment for a time, then from us will come a severe punishment.”
011|049|These are some of the accounts of the unseen, which We reveal to you. Neither you nor your people knew them before this. So, be patient. The ultimate outcome is for the righteous.
011|050|To Aad, their brother Hud. He said, “O my people, worship Allah; you have no god other than Him. You but invent lies.”
011|051|“O my people, I ask for no compensation from you. My reward is only from the One who originated me. Don’t you understand?”
011|052|“O my people, seek forgiveness from your Lord, and turn to Him in repentance. He will send abundant rain from the sky and will increase your strength, and you should not return to your wrongdoing.”
011|053|They replied, “O Hud, you didn’t provide us clear evidence, and we won’t forsake our gods on your say-so. We don’t believe you.”
011|054|“We can only conclude that some of our gods afflicted you with evil.” He replied, “I call upon Allah to witness, and you to witness, that I’m innocent of what you associate.
011|055|Besides Him. Therefore, all of you plot against me without any delay.
011|056|I place my trust in Allah, my Lord, and your Lord. There is no living being that He doesn’t hold by its forelock. Certainly, my Lord is on a straight path.
011|057|If you turn away, I have conveyed to you the message I was sent with. My Lord will replace you with other people, and you won’t harm Him at all. My Lord is the Guardian over all things.”
011|058|And when Our decree was issued, We delivered Hud and those who had faith with him, by Our mercy, and We saved them from a harsh punishment.
011|059|And that was Aad, who denied their Lord’s signs, disobeyed His messengers, and followed the command of every stubborn tyrant.
011|060|They were followed by a curse in this world and on Resurrection Day. Unquestionably, Aad rejected their Lord. So, away with Aad, the people of Hud.
011|061|To Thamud, their brother Saleh implored, “O my people, worship Allah; you have no deity other than Him. He initiated you from the earth and established you upon it. Seek His forgiveness, and repent to Him. My Lord is Near and Responsive.”
011|062|They responded, “O Saleh, we had high hopes in you before this. Are you prohibiting us from worshiping what our ancestors worshiped? We are deeply uncertain about what you are inviting us to.”
011|063|He replied, “O my people, do you see that I have clear evidence from my Lord, and that He bestowed His mercy upon me? Who could help me against Allah if I were to disobey Him? You would only cause me greater loss.”
011|064|“O my people, this is Allah’s she-camel for you as a symbol. Let her graze on Allah’s earth and don’t harm her, lest a swift punishment overtakes you.”
011|065|Yet, they hamstrung her. He then declared, “Enjoy yourselves in your homes for three days. This is an irrevocable prophecy.”
011|066|When Our decree came to pass, We saved Saleh and those who believed with him, by Our mercy, from the disgrace of that day. Your Lord is the All-Powerful, the Almighty.
011|067|And a loud scream seized the wrongdoers; and they became corpses in their homes.
011|068|As if they had never flourished there. Thamud denied their Lord, so away with Thamud!
011|069|Our messengers came to Abraham with good news. They said, “Peace,” and he answered, “Peace,” and promptly brought a roasted calf.
011|070|But when he saw their hands not reaching for it, he grew suspicious and felt a sense of apprehension. They said, “Fear not; we’ve been sent to the people of Lot.”
011|071|And his wife was standing, and she laughed. Then We gave her the joyful news of Isaac and, following Isaac, Jacob.
011|072|She exclaimed, “Wondrous indeed! Will I give birth while I am an old woman, and this husband of mine is an old man? This is truly a strange thing!”
011|073|They replied, “Are you amazed at Allah’s decree? May Allah’s mercy and blessings be upon you, O family of the house. He is Praiseworthy, Most Glorious.”
011|074|Once Abraham’s fear subsided and the good news reached him, he began to argue with Us for Lot’s people.
011|075|Abraham was compassionate, tender-hearted, and oft-returning.
011|076|“O Abraham, desist from this. Your Lord’s decree has come, and their punishment is irreversible.”
011|077|When Our messengers arrived at Lot’s, he was distressed and felt powerless, unable to protect them. He exclaimed, “This is a difficult day.”
011|078|His people, accustomed to sinful acts, came rushing towards him. He pleaded, “O my people, these are my daughters; they are purer for you. So fear Allah, and don’t disgrace me before my guests. Isn’t there a rational man among you?”
011|079|They responded, “You know well we have no right to your daughters, and you know what we want.”
011|080|He said, “If only I had the strength or could rely on a strong support.”
011|081|They said, “O Lot, we are the messengers of your Lord. They won’t reach you. So travel with your family during the cover of the night, and let none of you look back, except your wife. She will be struck by what strikes them. Their appointed time is the morning—isn’t the morning near?”
011|082|When Our command came, we overturned it completely, and We rained down upon it stones of baked clay.
011|083|Designated by your Lord, and they are never far from the wrongdoers.
011|084|To Midian, their brother Shuaib. He warned, “O my people, worship Allah; you have no deity other than Him. Don’t short-change in measurement and weight. I see you in good condition, but I fear the punishment of a besieging day for you.”
011|085|“O my people, give full measure and weight with justice, don’t cheat people out of their rights, and don’t commit corruption in the land.
011|086|The remainder from Allah is better for you, if you are believers. And I’m not a keeper over you.”
011|087|They responded, “O Shuaib, does your prayer command us to abandon what our ancestors worshiped, or to refrain from doing with our wealth what we please? Indeed, you are the forbearing, the right-guided!”
011|088|He responded, “O my people, did you consider: if I am on clear evidence from my Lord and He provided me with a good provision from Him? I don’t want to be in conflict with you about what I prohibit for you. I only desire reform to the best of my ability. My success is only through Allah. I have placed my trust upon Him, and to Him, I turn.”
011|089|“O my people, let not your opposition to me cause you to suffer the same fate as the people of Noah or Salih. And the people of Lot aren’t far from you.”
011|090|“And seek forgiveness from your Lord, then repent to Him. My Lord is Merciful and Affectionate.”
011|091|They said, “O Shuaib, we don’t grasp much of what you say, and we see you as weak among us. Were it not for your family, we would’ve stoned you, for you have no influence over us.”
011|092|He replied, “Is my family more esteemed to you than Allah, and you’ve pushed Him behind your backs? My Lord is fully aware of what you do.”
011|093|“O my people, do as you will, and I will act. You will then know who will face a humiliating punishment and who is a liar. Wait; I am waiting with you.”
011|094|When Our decree came, We saved Shuaib and those who believed with him, by mercy from Us. And the shriek overtook the wrongdoers, and they became corpses in their homes.
011|095|As if they had never flourished there. So, away with Midian, just as Thamud was done away with.
011|096|We sent Moses with Our signs and a clear mandate.
011|097|To Pharaoh and his nobility, but they followed Pharaoh’s dictates, although Pharoah’s dictates weren’t rational.
011|098|On the Day of Resurrection, he will lead his people into the Fire—a horrendous place to be led to.
011|099|They were pursued by a curse in this life—and on Resurrection Day. What a horrid gift they chose!
011|100|These are some of the stories of the communities that We narrate to you. Some of them are still standing, others are stubble.
011|101|We didn’t wrong them, but they wronged themselves. Their gods, which they invoked besides Allah, availed them nothing when your Lord’s command arrived; they only added to their ruin.
011|102|Such is your Lord’s grip when He seizes the communities while they are immersed in wrongdoing. Indeed, His grip is painful and severe.
011|103|This is a warning for those who fear the punishment of the Hereafter. That’s a Day for which the people will be gathered, and that’s a Day witnessed.
011|104|We only delay it for a determined period.
011|105|When that day arrives, no soul will speak except by His leave. Some will be miserable, while others will be happy.
011|106|As for those who are miserable, they will be in the Fire, where they will sigh and wail.
011|107|They will dwell there for as long as the heavens and the earth last, unless your Lord wills differently. Your Lord accomplishes what He intends.
011|108|As for the happy, they will be in Paradise, residing for as long as the heavens and the earth last, unless your Lord wills differently—a gift without end.
011|109|So don’t be in doubt about what these people worship. They only worship as their ancestors did before. We will give them their full recompense, without any reduction.
011|110|We gave Moses the Scripture, but disputes arose concerning it. If not for a prior decree from your Lord, their disputes would’ve been resolved. Yet they remain deeply uncertain about it.
011|111|Your Lord will fully pay them for their deeds. Surely He is well aware of everything they do.
011|112|So be upright, as you’ve been commanded, and whoever repents with you. And don’t transgress. He sees all that you do.
011|113|And don’t incline towards those who do wrong, lest the Fire should touch you. You would then have no protectors other than Allah, and you wouldn’t be helped.
011|114|Establish the prayer at the two ends of the day, and during parts of the night. Good deeds take away bad deeds. This is a reminder for the mindful.
011|115|And be patient, for surely Allah won’t waste the reward of those who do good.
011|116|If there had been, among the generations before you, people with discernment to ward off corruption on earth—except for the few whom We saved. But the wrongdoers pursued the luxuries they were granted and became transgressors.
011|117|Your Lord would never unjustly destroy communities while their inhabitants work towards reform.
011|118|Had your Lord willed, He could’ve made humanity a single community, but people will continue to differ.
011|119|Except those on whom your Lord has mercy—and for that reason He created them—and the word of your Lord has been fulfilled: “I will fill hell with jinn and humans together.”
011|120|We narrate to you the stories of the messengers to strengthen your heart. In these, the truth has come to you, along with guidance and reminders for the believers.
011|121|Say to those who don’t believe, “Work according to your ability; and we are working.”
011|122|“And wait; we, too, are waiting.”
011|123|To Allah belongs the unseen of the heavens and the earth. All matters are returned to Him. Worship Him and put your trust in Him. Your Lord is not unaware of what you do.
012|001|Alif. Lam. Ra. These are the verses of the clear, enlightening Scripture.
012|002|We revealed it as an Arabic Quran, so that you may understand.
012|003|Through this Quran, we narrate to you the most accurate of stories, although you were previously unaware.
012|004|Joseph said to his father, “O my father, I saw eleven stars, and the sun, and the moon; I saw them prostrating to me.”
012|005|He responded, “O my son, don’t disclose your vision to your brothers, lest they conspire against you. For Satan is man’s outright enemy.
012|006|Your Lord will choose you, teach you the interpretation of narratives, and complete His favor upon you and upon Jacob’s lineage, as He completed it before upon your forefathers, Abraham and Isaac. Your Lord is All-Knowing, All-Wise.
012|007|In the story of Joseph and his brothers, there are signs for those who inquire.
012|008|They grumbled, “Our father is more affectionate to Joseph and his brother than to us, despite our greater number. Our father is clearly misguided.”
012|009|“Kill Joseph, or throw him out to a distant land, so that your father’s attention will be exclusively yours. After which, you can be people of righteousness.”
012|010|One of them suggested, “Don’t kill Joseph, but if you are committed to doing something, throw him into the bottom of a well. Some passing caravan may pick him up.”
012|011|They said, “O our father, why don’t you trust us with Joseph, while we are truly his well-wishers?
012|012|Let him join us tomorrow for play and fun. We will surely protect him.”
012|013|He replied, “It saddens me that you should take him away. I fear a wolf might devour him while you’re negligent of him.”
012|014|They replied, “If a wolf were to devour him while we’re a strong group, then we would be truly losers.”
012|015|So, when they took him and agreed to put him into the bottom of the well, We inspired him: “You will inform them of this deed of theirs when they don’t realize.”
012|016|And they came to their father at night, crying.
012|017|They said, “O our father, we were racing each other and left Joseph with our belongings, and a wolf ate him. But you won’t believe us, even if we are truthful.”
012|018|And they presented his shirt, stained with false blood. He said, “Rather, your souls lured you into something. Yet patience is beautiful. May Allah’s help be sought against what you claim.”
012|019|A passing caravan arrived, and they sent their water drawer. He lowered his bucket and said, “Oh, good news! Here is a boy!” And they concealed him as merchandise, but Allah knew well what they did.
012|020|They sold him for a low price, a few coins, so little did they value him.
012|021|The man from Egypt who bought him said to his wife, “Make his stay comfortable; perhaps he can benefit us, or we might adopt him as a son.” And thus, We established Joseph in the land, and We taught him the interpretation of events. Allah’s command is always executed, but most people don’t know.
012|022|Upon reaching his maturity, We gifted him with wisdom and knowledge. This is how We reward those who do good.
012|023|And she, in whose house he was, sought to seduce him. She closed the doors and said, “Come to me!” He responded, “Allah forbid! He is my master, he treats me well, and the wrongdoers never succeed.”
012|024|She desired him, and he desired her had he not seen his Lord’s evidence. Thus, We diverted evil and indecency from him; he was one of Our devoted servants.
012|025|They raced to the door, and she tore his shirt from behind. They encountered her husband at the door, to whom she cried, “What’s the penalty for someone who intended harm to your family, if not imprisonment or a severe punishment?”
012|026|He said, “It was she who tried to seduce me.” A witness from her family suggested, “If his shirt is torn from the front, then she told the truth, and he is the liar.
012|027|But if his shirt is torn from the back, she has lied, and he is the truthful one.”
012|028|Seeing his shirt torn from the back, he said, “This is one of your cunning tricks. Your scheming is indeed considerable.”
012|029|“Joseph, overlook this. And you, woman, ask forgiveness for your sin. You are certainly in the wrong.”
012|030|Some women in the city said, “The governor’s wife is trying to seduce her servant; she is deeply in love with him. We see her as clearly misguided.”
012|031|Upon hearing their whispers, she invited them over, prepared a feast for them, and gave each of them a knife. She then commanded, “Come out before them!” When they saw him, they marveled at him and cut their hands, exclaiming, “Allah preserve us! This is not a human! This is none other than a noble angel.”
012|032|She said, “This is the one for whom you blamed me for. Yes, I tried to seduce him, but he firmly resisted. If he doesn’t do as I command him, he will be imprisoned and will become humiliated.”
012|033|He said, “My Lord, prison is more desirable to me than what they call me to. Unless You divert their plot from me, I might incline toward them and become of the ignorant.”
012|034|His Lord answered his prayer and averted their scheme from him. He is the All-Hearing, the All-Knowing.
012|035|It seemed good to them, after they had seen the proofs, to imprison him for a time.
012|036|Two young men entered the prison with him. One of them said, “I saw myself pressing wine.” The other said, “I saw myself carrying bread on my head, from which birds were eating. Tell us its interpretation, for we see you as a man of virtue.”
012|037|He replied, “I will inform you of their interpretation before your meal arrives. This is from the knowledge that my Lord has taught me. I have departed from the creed of people who don’t believe in Allah and deny the Hereafter.
012|038|“I adhere to the faith of my forefathers, Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob. It’s not for us to associate partners with Allah. This is from Allah’s grace upon us and upon humanity, yet most people are not thankful.”
012|039|“My fellow inmates, are many different lords better, or Allah, the One, the Supreme?
012|040|You are only worshiping names that you and your fathers have invented, without having any authority from Allah. The command rests solely with Allah. He decreed that you worship none but Him. This is the right religion, but most people don’t know.
012|041|O my fellow prisoners, one of you will serve his master wine, while the other will be crucified, and birds will eat from his head. The issue you inquired about has been decided.”
012|042|He said to the one he thought would be released, “Mention me to your master.” But Satan caused him to forget his lord’s mention, so he remained in prison for some years.
012|043|The king said, “I saw seven fat cows being eaten by seven lean ones, and seven green spikes of grain and others dry. O nobles, interpret my vision for me, if you can interpret visions.”
012|044|They replied, “A jumble of dreams, and we don’t know the interpretation of dreams.”
012|045|Then the one of the two who was saved, remembered after a period of time, and said, “I will tell you its interpretation, so send me.”
012|046|“Joseph, O truthful one, explain to us seven fat cows being eaten by seven lean ones, and seven green spikes of grain and others dry, that I may return to the people, so they may know.”
012|047|He said, “You will cultivate for seven consecutive years, and what you harvest, leave it in its spikes, except for a little which you will eat.”
012|048|“Then will follow seven difficult years which will consume what you saved for them, except for a little of what you have stored.”
012|049|“Then, after that, there will come a year in which the people will receive abundant rain and will press.”
012|050|The king said, “Bring him to me!” And when the messenger came to him, he said, “Return to your master and ask him about the women who cut their hands. My Lord is fully aware of their scheming.”
012|051|Then, when they were asked, “What was your aim when you tried to seduce Joseph, “What was your motive when you tried to seduce Joseph?” They responded, “Allah forbid! We know of no ill conduct on his part.” The governor’s wife then confessed, “Now the truth has now emerged; it was I who sought to seduce him, and he is truthful.”
012|052|“This is so he may know that I didn’t betray him in his absence, and that Allah doesn’t guide the scheming of the betrayers.”
012|053|“I don’t claim innocence for myself. The soul is predisposed to evil, except those my Lord bestows mercy upon. My Lord is Forgiving and Merciful.”
012|054|The king said, “Bring him to me. I will appoint him exclusively for myself.” When he talked to him, he said, “Today, you are with us established and trusted.”
012|055|He proposed, “Appoint me over the land’s storehouses; I am a reliable and knowledgeable custodian.”
012|056|Thus, We established Joseph in the land, granting him the freedom to reside wherever he desired. We bestow Our mercy upon whom We will, and We never let the reward of the righteous be lost.
012|057|But, the reward of the Hereafter is better for those who believe and maintain righteousness.
012|058|Joseph’s brothers came, and he recognized them when they arrived, but they didn’t recognize him.
012|059|While preparing their supplies, he said, “Bring me your brother from your father’s side. Don’t you see that I give full measure and am the best of hosts?”
012|060|“If you don’t bring him to me, you will receive no supplies from me, and you won’t be permitted near me.”
012|061|They replied, “We will convince his father to send him with us, and we will surely do it.”
012|062|He then instructed his servants, “Place their money back into their saddlebags, so they may recognize it when they return to their family, that they might return.”
012|063|Upon their return to their father, they pleaded, “Father, we will be denied further supplies unless you send our brother with us. Indeed, we are his protectors.”
012|064|He replied, “Shall I entrust him to you, when I had previously entrusted his brother to you? But Allah is the best guardian, and He is the most merciful of the merciful.”
012|065|When they opened their bags, they discovered their money had been restored to them. They exclaimed, “Father, what more could we desire? This is our money, returned to us in full. Now, we can give food to our family, safeguard our brother, and acquire an additional load of provisions. That extra load is easily obtainable for us.”
012|066|He responded, “I won’t send him with you, until you swear by Allah, that you will bring him back to me, unless you become surrounded.” And when they gave him their promise, he said, “Allah is the overseer of what we say.”
012|067|He said, “My sons, don’t enter from one gate, but enter from different gates. I cannot avail you against Allah at all. The decree belongs solely to Allah. I trust in Him, and upon Him, those who trust should trust.”
012|068|Despite entering as their father had instructed them, it didn’t alter Allah’s plan. But it was a need in Jacob’s soul. He was endowed with knowledge from what We had taught him, but most people don’t know.
012|069|When they presented themselves to Joseph, he drew his brother close to him, and he whispered, “I am your brother, so don’t be disheartened by their behavior.”
012|070|As he prepared their provisions, he discreetly placed the goblet in his brother’s saddlebag. Then a herald shouted, “O people of the caravan! You are surely thieves!”
012|071|Upon being summoned, they were asked, “What have you lost?”
012|072|“We lost the king’s goblet,” they replied. “Whoever brings it will receive a camel-load, and I guarantee it.”
012|073|They responded, “By Allah, you surely know that we didn’t come to cause disorder in the land, and we aren’t thieves.”
012|074|They were further asked, “What should be his penalty if you are proven to be lying?”
012|075|They replied, “His penalty—if it’s found in his bag—will be that he will become yours. This is how we penalize the wrongdoers.”
012|076|He began with their bags before his brother’s, and eventually, he retrieved it from his brother’s bag. Thus did We devise a plan for Joseph. He couldn’t have detained his brother under the king’s law, unless Allah had so willed. We raise in ranks whom We will, and above every possessor of knowledge, there is One more knowledgeable.
012|077|They exclaimed, “If he has stolen, a brother of his committed theft before.” But Joseph kept this to himself and didn’t disclose it to them. He said, “You’re in a worse position, and Allah knows best what you describe.”
012|078|They pleaded, “O Noble one, he has an elderly father, so take one of us in his place. We see you as a good-doer.”
012|079|He replied, “Allah forbid that we should take anyone but him with whom we found our property. Otherwise, we would be unjust.”
012|080|When they despaired of him, they withdrew to confer privately. Their eldest said, “Don’t you remember that your father received a solemn pledge from you before Allah, and how you were previously lax towards Joseph? I won’t leave this land until my father permits me, or Allah decides for me. He is the best of judges.”
012|081|“Go back to your father, and say, ‘O our father, your son committed theft, and we testify only to what we know, and we couldn’t guard against the unforeseen.’”
012|082|“Also, ask about the town where we’ve been, the caravan in which we returned; we are being truthful.”
012|083|He said, “Rather, your souls lured you to something. Yet, patience is beautiful. Perhaps Allah will bring them all back to me. He is the All-Knowing, the All-Wise.”
012|084|Then he turned away from them, lamenting, “Oh, my grief for Joseph!” His eyes turned white from grief, and he became depressed.
012|085|They exclaimed, “By Allah, you won’t stop remembering Joseph until you ruin your health, or until you pass away.”
012|086|He replied, “I only express my distress and anguish to Allah, and I know from Allah what you don’t know.”
012|087|“O my sons, go and search for Joseph and his brother, and never despair of Allah’s mercy. None despairs of Allah’s mercy except the disbelieving people.”
012|088|Upon entering his presence, they pleaded, “Your Excellency, adversity has touched us and our family, and we brought only a paltry sum. Please, give us full measure and be charitable to us. Truly, Allah rewards the charitable.”
012|089|He asked, “Do you remember what you did with Joseph and his brother in your ignorance?”
012|090|They exclaimed, “Could you possibly be Joseph?” He confirmed, “I am Joseph, and this is my brother. Allah has indeed been gracious to us. Whoever is righteous and patient—Allah never wastes the reward of the good-doers.”
012|091|They admitted, “By Allah, truly Allah has preferred you over us, and we were indeed at fault.”
012|092|He responded, “There will be no blame on you today. May Allah forgive you, for He is the Most Merciful of the merciful.”
012|093|“Take my shirt, and lay it over my father’s face, and he will regain his sight. And bring your entire family to me.”
012|094|As the caravan departed, their father said, “I can sense the scent of Joseph, even though you think I’m senile.”
012|095|They replied, “By Allah, you are still in your old delusions.”
012|096|When the bearer of good news arrived, he placed it on his face, and he regained his sight. He said, “Didn’t I tell you that I know from Allah what you don’t know?”
012|097|They pleaded, “O our father, seek forgiveness for our transgressions; we were indeed in the wrong.”
012|098|He replied, “I will seek your forgiveness from my Lord. He is the Forgiving, the Merciful.”

He has been good to me, releasing me from prison and bringing you from the desert after Satan had stirred up strife between me and my brothers. My Lord is Most Kind to whom He wills. He is the All-Knowing, the All-Wise.”
012|101|“My Lord, You’ve granted me some authority and taught me some interpretation of events—the Originator of the heavens and the earth. You’re my Protector in this world and the Hereafter. Receive my soul in submission, and unite me with the righteous.”
012|102|These are some of the narratives that We reveal to you. You weren’t present with them when they conspired and agreed on their plan.
012|103|Despite your eagerness, most people aren’t believers.

012|105|How many signs in the heavens and on earth do they pass by, yet they turn away from them?
