013|001|Alif, Lam, Meem, Ra. These are the verses of the Scripture. What was revealed to you from your Lord is the truth, yet most people don’t believe.
013|002|It is Allah who raised the skies without any pillars you can see, then He established Himself upon the Throne. He subjected the sun and the moon, each running for a set term. He conducts all affairs and explains the signs, so that you may be certain of meeting your Lord.
013|003|It is He who spread the earth, placed mountains and rivers on it, and of every fruit, He made therein two mates. He covers the night with the day. In that are signs for people who give thought.
013|004|On earth are adjacent terrains, vineyards, fields of crops, and date palms, from shared or separate roots, irrigated with the same water. We make some taste better than others. In this are signs for people who reason.
013|005|If you’re amazed, even amazing is their statement: “When we are dust, will we be created anew?” These are the ones who denied their Lord. They will have shackles around their necks. They will be the inhabitants of the Fire, dwelling therein forever.
013|006|They eagerly want you to bring about bad before good, even though there were instances before them. Your Lord is abundant in forgiveness for people, despite their wrongdoings, and yet, your Lord is severe in retribution.
013|007|Those who disbelieve ask, “Why has no miracle been sent down to him from his Lord?” You are but a warner; and for every people, there is a guide.
013|008|Allah knows what every female carries, and what the wombs diminish or increase. Everything with Him is of due proportion.
013|009|He is the Knower of the unseen and the witnessed, the Grand, the Most High.
013|010|It’s the same whether one of you conceals his speech or declares it openly, and whether one hides in the night or goes out freely in the day.
013|011|Guardians are stationed before and behind him, safeguarding him by Allah’s command. Allah won’t change people’s condition until they change what’s within themselves. If Allah intends for a people ill, there is no repelling it, and they have no defender or supporter besides Him.
013|012|It is He who shows you lightning, causing fear and hope, and produces the heavy clouds.
013|013|The thunder glorifies His praise, as do the angels, out of awe for Him. He releases thunderbolts and strikes with them whom He wills. Yet they argue about Allah, despite Him being tremendous in might and authority.
013|014|To Him is the call of truth. Those they pray to besides Him can’t respond to them with a thing, except like one who reaches his hand out to the water, only for it never to reach his mouth. The prayers of the unbelievers are but in vain.
013|015|To Allah do all those in the heavens and the earth bow down, willingly or unwillingly, and their shadows in the mornings and the afternoons.
013|016|Ask, “Who is the Lord of the heavens and the earth?” Answer, “Allah.” Then ask, “Have you taken other than Him allies, who can neither benefit nor harm themselves?” Say, “Are the blind and the sighted equal? Or are darkness and light alike? Or have they ascribed partners to Allah who supposedly created creations similar to His, so that creation appeared similar to them?” Say, “Allah is the Creator of everything, He is the One, the Overpowering.”
013|017|He sends down water from the sky, and valleys flow according to their capacity. The torrent carries overflowing foam, akin to what emerges from metals when melted for crafting jewelry and tools. Thus, Allah illustrates truth and falsehood. The foam dissipates, but what benefits humanity remains on earth. Thus, Allah presents parables.
013|018|For those who respond to their Lord is the best. But for those who don’t respond to Him—even if they possessed everything on earth, and an equivalent besides, they would offer it to ransom themselves. These will face a terrible reckoning, and their housing will be Hell—a dreadful dwelling.
013|019|Is one who knows that what has been revealed to you from your Lord is the truth like the one who is blind? Only people of understanding will remember.
013|020|Those who honor the covenant of Allah and don’t break the contract.
013|021|And those who join what Allah has commanded to be joined, revere their Lord, and dread the dire reckoning.
013|022|Those who patiently seek their Lord’s presence, pray regularly, spend out of what We’ve provided for them—secretly and openly—and repel evil with good, for them is the ultimate home.
013|023|The Gardens of Eden, which they will enter, along with the righteous among their parents, spouses, and offspring. Angels will enter upon them from every gate.
013|024|“Peace be upon you due to your patience. How wonderful is the final home!”
013|025|And those who break the covenant of Allah after its ratification, sever what Allah has commanded to be joined, and spread corruption on earth, upon them is the curse, and they will have a wretched home.
013|026|Allah expands the provision for whom He wills and measures it. They rejoice in the worldly life, while the worldly life, compared to the Hereafter, is but temporary enjoyment.
013|027|The disbelievers argue, “Why has a sign not been sent down upon him from his Lord?” Answer, “Allah leads astray whom He wills, and He guides to Himself those who turn back.”
013|028|Those who believe and whose hearts find tranquility in the remembrance of Allah—for indeed, it is through the remembrance of Allah that hearts find peace.
013|029|Those who believe and do righteous deeds—blessedness is theirs and a beautiful return.
013|030|We sent you amongst a nation, as We sent to nations before you, to convey to them what We revealed to you. Yet they deny the Most Merciful. Say, “He is my Lord; there is no god but Him. On Him I have relied, and to Him is my return.”
013|031|And even if there was a Quran that could move mountains, split the earth, or make the dead speak, the ultimate authority would still belong to Allah. Didn’t those who believed give up, realizing that if Allah so willed, He could guide all of humanity? The unbelievers will continue to suffer calamities due to what they did, or they fall near their homes, until Allah’s promise is fulfilled. Allah does not fail in His promise.
013|032|Messengers before you were also ridiculed, but I allowed the unbelievers to carry on, only to seize them—how severe was My retribution!
013|033|Who is He, the One observing over every soul and its actions? And yet they attribute partners to Allah. Say, “Name them! Or are you informing Him of something He doesn’t know on Earth? Or is it mere outward speech?” Their plots seem appealing to the unbelievers, and they are blocked from the path. Whomever Allah leads astray, there is no guide for him.
013|034|They will have suffering in this worldly life, and the suffering of the hereafter is harsher, and they will have no protector from Allah.
013|035|The example of Paradise promised to the righteous is where rivers flow beneath. Its produce and shade are everlasting. Such is the end result for the righteous, while the end result for unbelievers is the Fire.
013|036|Those whom We’ve given the scripture rejoice in what was revealed to You. But some factions deny parts of it. Say, “I am commanded to worship Allah alone and not associate anything with Him. To Him, I call, and to Him, is my return.”
013|037|And thus, We’ve revealed it as a law in Arabic. If you should follow their desires after what has come to you of knowledge, there will be no protector or ally for you against Allah.
013|038|We sent messengers before you, and We assigned to them wives and descendants. It’s not for a messenger to come with a sign except by Allah’s permission. For every era, there is a scripture.
013|039|Allah eliminates what He wills or confirms it, and with Him is the Source Scripture.
013|040|Whether We show you some of what We promised them, or We end your life, you have to convey, and judgment is Ours.
013|041|Don’t they see that We are reducing the land from its borders? Allah decrees. None can overturn His decision. And He is swift in accounting.
013|042|Those before them plotted, but all planning belongs to Allah. He knows what every soul earns. The unbelievers will find out who gets the ultimate Home.
013|043|The unbelievers say, “You are not a Messenger.” Respond, “Allah suffices as a witness between me and you, along with anyone who has knowledge of the Scripture.”
014|001|Alif. Lam. Ra. This is a Scripture that We revealed to you, to guide people from darkness into light, by the permission of their Lord, towards the path of the Almighty, the Praiseworthy.
014|002|Allah, to whom belongs everything in the heavens and on the earth. Woe unto the unbelievers, for a severe punishment awaits them.
014|003|Those who prefer the worldly life over the Hereafter, who deter others from Allah’s path, and seek to bend it. These are far astray.
014|004|We sent every messenger in the language of his people, to clarify things for them. Allah leaves astray whom He wills, and He guides whom He wills. He is the All-Wise, the All-Powerful.
014|005|We sent Moses with Our signs: “Lead your people from darkness into light, and remind them of Allah’s days.” In this are signs for every patient, thankful person.
014|006|Moses told his people, “Remember Allah’s favor upon you, when He saved you from Pharaoh’s people, who imposed terrible suffering upon you, slaughtering your sons and sparing your daughters. That was a grave test from your Lord.”
014|007|Your Lord declared, “If you are grateful, I will surely increase you; but if you are ungrateful, then My punishment is severe.”
014|008|Moses said, ”Even if you, along with everyone on earth, are ungrateful, Allah is still Self-Sufficient, Praiseworthy.”
014|009|Didn’t the stories of those before you reach you—the people of Noah, Aad, Thamud, and those after them? None knows them except Allah. Their messengers came to them with clear signs, but they tried to muzzle them, saying, “We disbelieve in what you’ve been sent with, and we are in serious doubt about what you invite us to.”
014|010|Their messengers responded, “Is there doubt about Allah, the Originator of the heavens and the earth? He invites you to forgive your sins and delay you to a specified time.” They replied, “You are but humans like us, wanting to turn us away from what our ancestors worshiped. So, bring us clear evidence.”
014|011|Their messengers replied, “Indeed, we are only humans like you, yet Allah favors whom He wills of His servants. It’s not up to us to bring you proof except by Allah’s permission. In Allah, should the believers put their trust.”
014|012|“Why shouldn’t we trust Allah when He has guided us along our paths? We will patiently endure what you inflict upon us. Let those who trust place their trust in Allah.”
014|013|The unbelievers told their messengers, “We will expel you from our land, unless you return to our religion.” Then their Lord revealed to them, “Most certainly, We will destroy the wrongdoers.”
014|014|“And after them, We will settle you in the land. This is for those who fear My position and heed My warnings.”
014|015|They sought victory, and every stubborn tyrant was disappointed.
014|016|In front of him is Hell, and he will be given purulent water to drink.
014|017|He will gulp it, yet he won’t swallow it. Death will come at him from every direction, yet he won’t die. And ahead of him, there is unrelenting torment.
014|018|Those who deny their Lord, their works are like ashes, swept away by a fierce wind on a stormy day. They have no control over anything they’ve earned. This is the far straying.
014|019|Don’t you see how Allah created the heavens and the earth in truth? If He wills, He can remove you and produce a new creation.
014|020|And this is not difficult for Allah.
014|021|They will all appear before Allah. The weak will plead with the arrogant, “We were your followers; can you spare us from Allah’s punishment?” They will respond, “Had Allah guided us, we would’ve guided you. Whether we express impatience or endure patiently, there’s no escape for us.”
014|022|When judgment is passed, Satan will say, “Allah gave you a truthful promise, and I made you promises too, but I failed you. I had no authority over you, except that I invited you, and you responded to me. So, don’t blame me, but blame yourselves. I can’t answer your cries, nor can you answer mine. I disavow what you previously associated me with. For the wrongdoers, there is a severe punishment.”
014|023|Those who believed and worked righteousness will be admitted into Gardens beneath which rivers flow, abiding therein by the permission of their Lord, and their greeting therein will be “Peace.”
014|024|Don’t you see how Allah presents a parable? A good word is like a good tree: its roots are firmly anchored, and its branches extend towards the sky.
014|025|It produces its fruit every season by the permission of its Lord. Allah presents such analogies to people so they may reflect.
014|026|The analogy of a wicked word is like a rotten tree, uprooted from the ground, lacking stability.
014|027|Allah anchors the believers with the firm word, in this life and the Hereafter. Allah makes the wrongdoers go astray, for Allah does what He wills.
014|028|Haven’t you considered those who exchanged Allah’s favor for disbelief and brought their people to ruins?
014|029|Hell, where they will burn; a terrible dwelling!
014|030|They set up equals to Allah, intending to mislead others from His path. Say, “Enjoy your brief pleasures; your final destination is the Fire.”
014|031|Tell My servants who have believed to establish their prayers and to give from what We provide for them, secretly and openly, before the arrival of a day in which there will be neither bargaining nor befriending.
014|032|It is Allah who created the heavens and the earth and sends down rain from the sky, thereby producing fruits for your sustenance. And He subjected to you the ships to sail through the sea by His command, and He subjected the rivers to you.
014|033|Also, He subjected to you the sun and the moon, both diligently pursuing their courses, and He subjected the night and the day to you.
014|034|He gave you something of all that you requested. If you were to count Allah’s blessings, you could never enumerate them. Man is given to wrongdoing and ingratitude.
014|035|And when Abraham said, “My Lord, make this city safe, and keep me and my offspring from worshiping idols.”
014|036|“My Lord, they have misled many among the people. So whoever follows me, then he is of me; and whoever disobeys me, then You are Forgiving and Merciful.”
014|037|“Our Lord, I have settled some of my descendants in an uncultivated valley, near Your Sacred House, so they may establish prayer. Our Lord, make people’s hearts incline towards them, and provide them with fruits, so they may be thankful.”

016|061|If Allah were to punish people for their wrongdoings, He wouldn’t leave a living creature on it. However, He defers them to an appointed term. When their time arrives, they can neither delay nor hasten it by an hour.
016|062|They attribute to Allah what they hate, and their tongues falsely claim that all good things are theirs. No doubt, the Fire is their destiny, and they will be left in it.
016|063|By Allah, We sent messengers to communities before you, but Satan made their deeds fair-seeming to them. He is their ally today, and a severe punishment awaits them.
016|064|We revealed the Scripture to you, so you may clarify for them what they dispute, and as guidance and mercy for believers.
016|065|Allah sends down water from the sky, thereby reviving the earth after its demise. In this, there is a sign for those who listen.
016|066|There is a lesson for you in livestock: We give you drink from within them. From what’s in their bellies, between excretions and blood, we produce for you pure milk, pleasant for those who drink it.
016|067|And from the fruits of date palms and grapevines, you obtain sugar and good provision. In this, there is a sign for those who think.
016|068|Your Lord inspired the bee: “Establish your hives in the mountains, the trees, and what they construct.”
016|069|Then, feed on the various fruits, and traverse the paths of your Lord with precision. From within their bodies comes a syrup of varying colors, wherein there is healing for people. In this, there is a sign for those who ponder.
016|070|Allah created you; then He will cause you to die. Some of you will be reduced to the most feeble age, so they don’t know anything after having known. Allah is All-Knowing, Most Capable.
016|071|Allah has favored some of you with more provisions than others. Yet those who are favored wouldn’t hand over their provision to those whom their right hands possess so they become equal to them therein. Do they then deny Allah’s blessings?
016|072|Allah created spouses for you from among yourselves, and through them, He blessed you with children and grandchildren. And He provided you with good things of sustenance. Will they believe in falsehoods and show ingratitude for Allah’s blessings?
016|073|They worship powerless idols instead of Allah, idols that don’t have the power to provide for them from the heavens and the earth.
016|074|So, don’t set up parallels to Allah. Allah knows, and you don’t know.
016|075|Allah presents an example: A slave, powerless and owned by his master, versus a man whom We’ve provided with a good livelihood, which he spends secretly and openly. Can they be considered equal? Praise be to Allah, but most of them don’t know.
016|076|Allah illustrates another example: Two men, one mute, incapable of doing anything useful, is completely dependent on his master; no matter how he directs him, he brings nothing good. Can he be compared to one who promotes justice and follows a straight path?
016|077|To Allah belongs the unseen realms of the heavens and the earth. The coming of the Hour is as swift as the blink of an eye, or even swifter. Allah has power over everything.
016|078|Allah brought you out of your mothers’ wombs, devoid of knowledge. He endowed you with hearing, sight, and intellect, that perhaps you would be grateful.
016|079|Don’t they see the birds suspended in mid-air? None sustains them except Allah. In this, there are signs for those who believe.
016|080|Allah provided you with homes for your comfort, and tents made from the hides of animals for your necessities during your travels and periods of rest. He gave you from their wool, fur, and hair, furnishings and goods for a time.
016|081|Allah has given you shade from what He created, and has provided you with retreats in the mountains. He gave you clothing to protect you from the heat, and armor to protect you from your violence. Thus, He perfects His blessings on you, that you may submit.
016|082|If they turn away, your duty is clear communication.
016|083|They recognize Allah’s blessings, yet they reject them, for the majority of them are ungrateful.
016|084|On the Day when We summon a witness from every community, those who disbelieved won’t be allowed to present excuses, nor will they be pardoned.
016|085|When the wrongdoers witness the punishment, it won’t be lessened for them, nor will they be granted delay.
016|086|When those who associated partners with Allah see their supposed partners, they will cry, “Our Lord, these are our partners whom we invoked besides You.” But they will throw back at them the words, “You are liars!”
016|087|On that Day, they will surrender to Allah, and all their invented claims will desert them.
016|088|For those who disbelieve and obstruct others from Allah’s path, We will add to their punishment because of their misconduct.
016|089|On the Day when We summon a witness from every community against them, We bring you as a witness against these. We revealed to you the Scripture, clarifying all things—a guide, mercy, and good news for those who submit.
016|090|Allah commands justice, kindness, and giving to relatives. He prohibits immorality, injustice, and oppression. He advises you, so you may be mindful.
016|091|Fulfill your commitments to Allah, and don’t violate your oaths after their confirmation, having made Allah your guarantor. Allah knows all that you do.
016|092|Don’t be like the woman who unravels her finely spun thread, making your oaths a means of deceit among yourselves. Allah tests you in this manner. On the Day of Resurrection, He will clarify for you everything you disputed.
016|093|If Allah had willed, He could’ve made you one community, but He misguides whom He wills and guides whom He wills. You’ll be questioned about your actions.
016|094|Don’t make your oaths a means of deception between you, lest your footing slips after being firm, and you suffer distress for hindering others from Allah’s path, and incur a terrible punishment.
016|095|Don’t trade Allah’s covenant for a trivial gain; what Allah prepared for you is far superior, if only you knew.
016|096|What you have will run out, but what Allah has remains. We will reward those who are patient according to their best deeds.
016|097|Whoever acts righteously, male or female, and is a believer, We will grant them a good life and reward them according to their best deeds.
016|098|When you read the Quran, seek refuge in Allah from Satan, the outcast.
016|099|He has no authority over those who believe and trust in their Lord.
016|100|His influence extends only to those who take him as an ally and those who associate partners with Him.
016|101|When We replace one verse with another—and Allah knows best what He reveals—they say, “YYou are just making things up.” Yet, most of them lack knowledge.
016|102|Say, “The Holy Spirit brought it down from your Lord, in truth, to stabilize those who believe, and as guidance and good news for the Submitters.”
016|103|We know they say, “A human is teaching him.” The language of the one they maliciously allude to is foreign, yet this is in clear Arabic.
016|104|Those who don’t believe in Allah’s revelations—Allah won’t guide them, and for them is a painful punishment.
016|105|Those who deny Allah’s revelations are the ones who fabricate falsehoods and are untruthful.
016|106|Anyone who rejects Allah after having faith—except for one who is coerced while his heart remains firm in faith—but anyone who opens their heart to disbelief, upon them descends Allah’s wrath, and a grave punishment awaits them.
016|107|That is because they favor the worldly life over the Hereafter. And Allah doesn’t guide the disbelieving people.
016|108|They are the ones Allah sealed their hearts, their hearing, and their sight. They are the ones who are heedless.
016|109|No doubt, they will be the losers in the Hereafter.
016|110|However, to those who emigrated after being persecuted, and who strived and showed patience, your Lord, in return, is forgiving and merciful.
016|111|On that Day, every soul will come pleading for itself, and every soul will be fully compensated for what it has done, and they won’t be wronged.
016|112|Allah presents an example of a secure and peaceful city, its provisions arriving abundantly from every direction. But it showed ingratitude for Allah’s blessings, so Allah made it taste the cloak of hunger and fear, as a consequence of their deeds.
016|113|A messenger from themselves had come to them, but they denied him. So, the punishment seized them while they were wrongdoers.
016|114|So, eat from what Allah provided for you, lawful and good, and be grateful for Allah’s favor, if you truly worship Him.
016|115|He only forbade you dead animals, blood, the flesh of swine, and what has been consecrated to other than Allah. But if one is compelled by necessity, without willful disobedience or transgression, Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.
016|116|Don’t say, falsely, with your tongues: “This is lawful, and this is unlawful,” in order to invent lies about Allah. Those who fabricate lies against Allah don’t succeed.
016|117|A brief enjoyment, then they will have a severe punishment.
016|118|We’ve detailed to you the prohibitions imposed on the Jews; We didn’t wrong them, but they used to wrong themselves.
016|119|As for those who commit evil deeds inadvertently, but later repent and reform, your Lord, after that, is Forgiving and Merciful.
016|120|Abraham was an exemplary leader, devoutly obedient to Allah, a monotheist, and he wasn’t among the polytheists.
016|121|Being appreciative of His blessings, He chose him and guided him to a straight path.
016|122|We granted him goodness in this life, and in the Hereafter, he will be among the righteous.
016|123|Then, We revealed to you: Follow the religious path of Abraham, the devout monotheist, who was not of the polytheists.”
016|124|The Sabbath was only instituted for those in dispute over it. Your Lord will resolve their disputes on Resurrection Day.
016|125|Invite to the path of your Lord through wisdom and kind advice, and engage in discussions in the most courteous manner. Your Lord knows best who strays from His path, and He knows best those who are rightly guided.
016|126|If you retaliate, then retaliate proportionately to the offense committed against you. However, if you endure, it is indeed better for those who are patient.
016|127|Be patient; your patience is solely through Allah. Don’t grieve over them, and don’t be distressed by their plots.
016|128|Allah is with the righteous, and those who do good deeds.
017|001|Blessed is He who journeyed His servant by night from the Sacred Mosque to the Farthest Mosque, the precincts We’ve blessed, to show him some of Our wonders. He is the All-Hearing, the All-Seeing.
017|002|We gave Moses the Scripture and made it a guide for the Children of Israel: “Take no protector other than Me.”
017|003|The descendants of those We carried with Noah; a thankful servant he was.
017|004|We forewarned the Children of Israel in the Scripture: “Twice you will spread corruption on earth, and you will ascend to a great height.”
017|005|When the first of these prophecies came to pass, We sent against you Our servants of formidable might, they ravaged through the homes, and it was a fulfilled warning.
017|006|Then, We gave you victory over them, reinforced you with wealth and children, and made you more numerous in human resources.
017|007|If you do good, it’s for yourself. If you do evil, it’s against yourselves. Then, when the second warning was fulfilled, they disfigured your faces, entered the temple as they had entered it the first time, and utterly ravaged all that they overran.
017|008|Perhaps your Lord will have mercy on you. If you revert, We will revert. We made Hell a prison for the disbelievers.
017|009|This Quran guides to what’s most upright and gives good news to the believers who do good deeds, that they’ll have a great reward.
017|010|For those who don’t believe in the Hereafter, We prepared a painful punishment.
017|011|Man prays for harm as he prays for good; man has always been hasty.
017|012|We made the night and the day two marvels. We erased the marvel of the night, and made the marvel of the day illuminating, so that you may seek bounty from your Lord, and may know the number of years and calculations. We explained everything in detail.
017|013|We’ve tied every person’s fate to his neck, and on the Day of Resurrection, We will bring out for him a record, which he will find spread open.
017|014|“Read your record! Today, your soul is enough to account against yourself.”
017|015|Whoever is guided, is guided for his benefit, and whoever strays, does so to his detriment. No bearer of burdens can bear the burdens of another, and We never punish until We have sent a messenger.
017|016|When We decide to destroy a town, We command its affluent ones, who then commit transgressions therein, thus justifying the sentence against it, and We destroy it completely.
017|017|How many generations did We annihilate after Noah? Your Lord is sufficient as an observer and knower of His beings’ sins.
017|018|Whoever desires the fleeting life, We readily grant whatever We will to whomever We choose. We then designate him for Hell, where he will burn, condemned and forsaken.
017|019|But whoever desires the Hereafter, and strives for it with due effort, while being a believer—it is those whose striving is appreciated.
017|020|To all—these and those—We extend from the bounty of your Lord. Your Lord’s giving is not restricted.
017|021|Consider how We’ve preferred some over others, yet the Hereafter offers greater ranks and greater in preference.
017|022|Don’t set up with Allah any other god, lest you find yourself despised and forsaken.
017|023|Your Lord has decreed that you worship none but Him, and that you extend kindness to your parents. If one or both of them attain old age in your presence, don’t say ‘uff’ to them, nor scold them, but address them with respectful words.
017|024|Lower the wing of humility out of compassion for them, and pray, “My Lord, have mercy on them, as they have brought me up when I was small.”
017|025|Your Lord is well aware of what’s within yourselves. If you maintain righteousness, then He is Ever Forgiving to those who are repentant.
017|026|Give due to your relatives, the needy, and the traveler. And don’t squander your wealth.
017|027|The extravagant are brethren of the devils, and Satan has always been ungrateful to his Lord.
017|028|But if you turn away from them, seeking mercy from your Lord for which you hope, then speak to them a gentle word.
017|029|Don’t keep your hand tied to your neck, nor extend it fully, lest you end up blamed and regretful.
017|030|Your Lord dispenses abundantly to whom He wills, and He measures out. He is always All-Knowing, All-Seeing of His beings.
017|031|Don’t kill your children for fear of poverty; We provide for them and for you. Killing them is a grave sin.
017|032|And don’t approach adultery, for it’s an immoral act and an evil way.
017|033|Don’t take a life that Allah deemed sacred, except in the course of justice. If someone is killed unjustly, We’ve given his heir authority, but he must not take life excessively; he will be assisted.
017|034|Don’t approach the orphan’s property, except in the best way, until he reaches maturity. Fulfill your commitments; the commitment is going to be questioned.
017|035|Give full measure when you measure, and weigh with an even balance. That is better and best in interpretation.
017|036|Don’t follow what you have no knowledge of. Hearing, sight, and reasoning—all of those will be questioned.
017|037|Don’t walk arrogantly on earth, for you can’t pierce the ground, nor can you reach the mountains in height.
017|038|All of this—the evil of it—is hated by your Lord.
017|039|This is some of the wisdom your Lord revealed to you. Don’t set up another deity with Allah, lest you be thrown into Hell, blamed and banished.
017|040|Did your Lord favor you with sons while taking for Himself daughters from among the angels? Indeed, you’ve made a grave statement.
017|041|We’ve explained variously in this Quran so that they may remember, but it only increases their rebellion.
017|042|Say, “If there were other gods along with Him, as they claim, they would’ve sought a way to the Lord of the Throne.”
017|043|Far exalted is He above what they say, in His grandeur and supremacy.
017|044|The seven heavens, the earth, and everything within them praise His glory. There is not a thing that does not glorify Him with praise, but you do not understand their glorification. He is Ever-Forbearing, Most Forgiving.
017|045|When you read the Quran, We place an invisible barrier between you and those who don’t believe in the Hereafter.
017|046|We placed covers on their hearts, preventing them from understanding it, and deafness in their ears. When you mention your Lord’s singularity in the Quran, they recoil in repulsion.
017|047|We know what they listen to, when they listen to you, when they conspire, when the wrongdoers say, “You are merely following a man under a spell.”
017|048|Look at the comparisons they make for you; they are astray and can’t find a way.
017|049|And they say, “When we are bones and crumbled particles, will we truly be resurrected in a new creation?”
017|050|Respond, “Be you stones or iron.
017|051|Or any creation you deem more even formidable.” Then they will question, “Who will restore us?” Respond, “The One who created you in the first place.” Then they’ll shake their heads at you and ask, “When will this happen?” Say, “It could be quite soon.”
017|052|On the Day He calls you, you will respond praising Him, realizing that you lingered only briefly.
017|053|Tell My servants to speak in a most kindly manner, for Satan sows discord among them. Satan is a clear enemy of man.
017|054|Your Lord knows you best. If He wills, He will have mercy on you. And if He wills, He will punish you. We didn’t send you as their overseer.
017|055|Your Lord knows everyone in the heavens and on earth. We’ve favored some prophets over others. To David, We gave the Psalms.
017|056|Say, “Invoke those you presume besides Him; they lack the power to alleviate your suffering or change your condition.”
017|057|Those whom they call upon are themselves seeking a way to their Lord, vying for His proximity, hoping for His mercy, and dreading His punishment. Your Lord’s punishment is to be avoided.
017|058|There is no community that We won’t obliterate or severely chastise before Resurrection Day. This is inscribed in the Book.
017|059|Nothing prevents Us from sending miracles, except that the previous generations rejected them. We gave Thamud the she-camel as a clear sign, but they maltreated her. We send signs only to instill fear.
017|060|We’ve informed you that your Lord encompasses all people. The vision We showed you and the cursed tree mentioned in the Quran are trials for people. We frighten them, but it only increases their defiance.
017|061|We commanded the angels, “Prostrate before Adam.” They all did, except for Iblis. He said, “Should I prostrate to one You created from mud?”
017|062|He added, “Do you see this one whom You honored over me? If You defer me until Resurrection Day, I will dominate his descendants, except for a few.”
017|063|He replied, “Go away! Whoever among them follows you, then Hell is your recompensation, an ample recompensation.”
017|064|“And entice whomever you can from among them with your voice. Muster against them your cavalry and your infantry, share the promises of wealth and children, and make promises to them.” However, Satan promises them nothing except deceit.
017|065|“As for My devotees, you have no power over them. Your Lord is sufficient as a Protector.”
017|066|It is your Lord who causes the ship to move for you through the sea, so you may seek His bounty. Indeed, He is Most Merciful to you.
017|067|When danger befalls you at sea, all those you call upon vanish, except for Him. Yet, when He brings you safely to land, you turn away. Man is ever ungrateful.
017|068|Are you confident that He won’t collapse a tract of land beneath you, or unleash a hailstorm upon you? Then, you would find no protector.
017|069|Or are you confident that He won’t return you to it again, unleash a hurricane against you, and drown you due to your ingratitude? Then, you would find no avenger against Us.
017|070|We honored the Children of Adam, transported them on land and sea, provided them with good things, and gave them preference over many of those We created.
017|071|On the Day when We summon every people with their leader, whoever is given his record in his right hand will read his record, and not a thread will be wronged.
017|072|But whoever is blind in this life, will be blind in the Hereafter, and further astray from the path.
017|073|They were about to entice you away from what We have revealed to you, in the hope that you would invent something else about Us; and then they would’ve taken you as a friend.
017|074|Had We not fortified you, you might have leaned towards them a little.
017|075|In that case, We would’ve made you taste double in life, and double at death, and then you would’ve found no helper with respect to Us.
017|076|They almost provoked you, to expel you from the land. But then they wouldn’t have remained after you, except for a short while.
017|077|That is the established way with the messengers We sent before you, and you won’t find any change in Our ways.
017|078|Perform the prayer at the sun’s decline until the darkness of the night, and the Quran at daybreak. The recitation at daybreak is witnessed.
017|079|Spend part of the night in vigil, as a supplementary prayer, so that your Lord may elevate you to a commendable station.
017|080|And pray, “My Lord, let my entry be truthful, and my exit be truthful; and grant me, from You, a supporting authority.”
017|081|And say, “The truth has come, and falsehood has dissipated. Falsehood is bound to dissipate.”
017|082|We reveal in the Quran healing and mercy for believers, but it increases the wrongdoers in nothing but loss.
017|083|When We bestow favor upon a person, he withdraws and turns aside; but when adversity touches him, he is in despair.
017|084|Say, “Each person acts according to his character, and your Lord knows best who is rightly guided.”
017|085|They ask you about the spirit. Respond, “The spirit is by the command of my Lord, and you’ve been given only a little knowledge.”
017|086|If We willed, We could take away what We revealed to you. Then, you would find no one to defend you against Us.
017|087|This is only by the mercy of your Lord. His grace unto you is immense.
017|088|Say, “Even if all humans and jinn were to collaborate to produce something akin to this Quran, they would not succeed, despite their collective efforts.”
017|089|In this Quran, We provide diverse parables for people, yet the majority persist in disbelief.
017|090|They say, “We won’t believe in you unless you make a spring gush out from the ground for us.
017|091|Or unless you own a garden of date palms and grapevines and you make rivers burst forth within it.
017|092|Or unless you cause the sky to fall upon us in pieces, as you claim, or bring Allah and the angels before us.
017|093|Or unless you have a house of gold. Or unless you ascend into the sky. Even then, we won’t believe in your ascension, until you bring down a book for us to read.” Say, “Glory be to my Lord! Am I anything more than a human messenger?”
017|094|What prevents people from believing when guidance has come to them, is their saying, “Allah sent a human as a messenger?”
017|095|Say, “If there were angels on earth walking peacefully, We’d certainly send an angel from heaven as a messenger to them.”
017|096|Say, “Allah is sufficient as a witness between you and me. He is fully aware and observant of His beings.”
017|097|Whomever Allah guides is guided, and whomever He misguides, you will find no helpers for him other than Him. We will gather them on the Day of Resurrection, on their faces—blind, dumb and deaf. Their destination is Hell; whenever it subsides, We will intensify the flames for them.
017|098|That is their retribution for rejecting Our revelations and questioning, “When we are reduced to bones and fragments, will we truly be resurrected as a new creation?”
017|099|Don’t they realize that Allah, who created the heavens and the earth, is able to create their likes? He appointed for them a term, of which there is no doubt. But the wrongdoers refuse anything except disbelief.
017|100|Say, “If you possessed the treasures of the mercy of my Lord, then you would withhold out of fear of spending.” Man is ever reluctant to give.
017|101|We gave Moses nine clear signs. Ask the Children of Israel, when he came to them, Pharaoh said to him, “O Moses, I suspect you are under a spell.”
017|102|He replied, “You’ve certainly known that none sent these down except the Lord of the heavens and the earth, as eye-openers. It seems to me, O Pharaoh, that you are perishing.”
017|103|So he intended to drive them out from the land, but We drowned him and those with him all together.
017|104|Subsequently, We told the Children of Israel, “Settle in the land, and when the promise of the final time comes to pass, We will gather you all together.”
017|105|We revealed it with the truth, and in truth, it descended. We sent you only to give good news and to issue warnings.
017|106|A Quran that We unfolded gradually, for you to read to people over time. We revealed it in stages.
017|107|Say, “Believe in it, or don’t believe. Those who were given knowledge before it, when it is recited to them, fall down on their faces, in humility.
017|108|And they exclaim, “Praise be to our Lord! The promise of our Lord has been fulfilled.”
017|109|And they will fall down, crying, and it would increase them in humility.
017|110|Say, “Call upon Allah, or call upon the Most Merciful. Whichever you call upon Him with, for Him are the most beautiful names.” And don’t be loud in your prayer nor quiet in it, but seek a way in between.
017|111|And say, “Praise be to Allah, who has not begotten a child, who has no partner in sovereignty, who has no ally out of weakness, and magnify Him with all the magnificence.”
018|001|Praise be to Allah, who revealed to His servant the Scripture, free from any distortions.
018|002|It is invaluable—to warn of severe punishment from Him, and as good news to the believers who do righteous deeds, that for them is a good reward.
018|003|Remaining in it forever.
018|004|And to warn those who say, “Allah has begotten a son.”
018|005|They have no knowledge of this, nor did their ancestors. A monstrous utterance comes out of their mouths. They speak nothing but lies.
018|006|Perhaps, you may destroy yourself with grief, chasing after them, if they don’t believe in this narrative.
018|007|We’ve made everything on earth an adornment for it, to test them, and ascertain who performs the best deeds among them.
018|008|But ultimately, We will reduce everything on it into a barren wasteland.
018|009|Do you consider the people of the Cave and the Inscription as among Our extraordinary miracles?
018|010|When they sought sanctuary in the cave, they prayed, “Our Lord, shower us with Your mercy, and arrange our affairs with wisdom.”
018|011|Then We sealed their ears in the cave for some years.
018|012|Then We awakened them, to determine which of the two groups could best estimate the duration of their stay.
018|013|We tell you their story with truth. They were young men who had faith in their Lord, and We augmented them in guidance.
018|014|We strengthened their hearts when they stood up and said, “Our Lord is the Lord of the heavens and the earth. We will never call upon any deity other than Him, for then we would be uttering a colossal falsehood.”
018|015|“These, our people, have taken gods besides Him, without producing clear evidence for them. Who is more unjust than one who fabricates lies against Allah?”
018|016|“Now that you have isolated yourself from them and from what they worship other than Allah, retreat to the cave. Your Lord will extend His mercy upon you and arrange your affairs with ease.”
018|017|You would have seen the sun, as it rose, veering away from their cave to the right, and as it set, bypassing them to the left, while they lay within the spacious area of the cave. This was one of Allah’s signs. Whomever Allah guides is guided, and whomever He leaves to stray, you will find no guiding mentor for him.
018|018|You would have thought they were awake, yet they were asleep. We turned them over, to the right and to the left, with their dog stretching its forelegs at the entrance. If you had observed them, you would’ve turned away from them in fear, and terror-filled.
018|019|We then awakened them, prompting them to question each other. One of them asked, “How long did you stay?” They answered, “We stayed a day or part of a day.” They concluded, “Only your Lord knows the duration of your stay.” “Send one of you with your money to the city, and let him find the best sustenance and bring it back to us. He must be discreet and not draw any attention to you.”
018|020|“If they discover you, they may stone you or force you to revert to their religion, and then you will never succeed.”
018|021|We made their story known to mankind, to demonstrate that Allah’s promise is true, and that there is no doubt about the Hour. When they disputed among themselves their affair, they proposed, “Let us build a structure over them.” Their Lord knows them best. Those who prevailed in the argument said, “We will erect a place of worship over them.”
018|022|Some say, “They were three, their dog being the fourth.” Others will say, “They were five, their dog being the sixth,” guessing at the unseen. Yet, others will say, “They were seven, their dog being the eighth.” Say, “My Lord is more knowledgeable of their number; only a few truly know.” Therefore, don’t argue about them without solid evidence, and don’t seek anyone’s opinion about them.
018|023|And don’t say about anything, “I will do this tomorrow.”
018|024|Without adding, “If Allah wills.” And remember your Lord when you forget, and say, “Perhaps my Lord will guide me towards better conduct than this.”
018|025|They remained in their cave for three hundred years, and nine more.
018|026|Say, “Allah knows best how long they stayed.” His are the mysteries of the heavens and the earth. His sight is perfect, His hearing is perfect. They have no protector against Him, and He shares His rule with no one.
018|027|Communicate what was revealed to you from your Lord’s Scripture. None can alter His words, and you won’t find any refuge besides Him.
018|028|Be content with those who call upon their Lord morning and evening, seeking His countenance. Don’t turn your eyes away from them, desiring the splendors of this worldly life. And don’t obey him whose heart We made heedless of Our remembrance, who follows his desires, and whose affairs are in disarray.
018|029|Say, “The truth is from your Lord; let whoever wishes believe, and whoever wishes disbelieve.” We’ve prepared for the wrongdoers a fire, whose walls will enclose them. When they plead for help, they will be helped with water like molten brass, which scalds the faces. Wretched is the drink, and terrible is the resting place.
018|030|As for those who believe and perform righteous deeds—We never let the reward of any such person, who does good, be wasted.
018|031|They will have gardens of eternal bliss, through which rivers flow. They will be adorned with golden bracelets and wear green garments of fine silk and heavy brocade, reclining on plush couches. Excellent is the reward, and what a splendid resting place.
018|032|Present to them the parable of two men: We blessed one with two vineyards, surrounded by date palms, with crops in the middle.
018|033|Both gardens produced their full yield and never failed, and We caused a river to gush through them.
018|034|And he had fruit. In a conversation with his friend, he boasted, “I have more wealth and have a larger following than you.”
018|035|And he entered his garden, while he wronged himself, saying, “I don’t think this will ever perish.”
018|036|“And I don’t think the Hour will ever come. And even if I’m returned to my Lord, I will surely find something better in place of it.”
018|037|His companion said to him while conversing with him, “Do you deny the One who created you from dust, then from a drop, and then developed you into a man?
018|038|But He, Allah, is my Lord, and I don’t associate anyone with my Lord.
018|039|Why didn’t you say, when you entered into your garden, Whatever Allah wills, there is no strength except in Allah, though you see me lesser than you in wealth and children.’
018|040|Perhaps my Lord will give me something better than your garden, and He may send upon it a calamity from the sky, reducing it to a smooth, slippery plain.
018|041|Or its water might sink so deep into the ground—that you won’t be able to seek it.”
018|042|And his fruits were encircled, and he started wringing his hands in regret over all that he had invested in it, while it lay in ruins on its trellises. He said, “I wish I had not associated anyone with my Lord.”
018|043|There was no party to assist him against Allah, nor was he capable of helping himself.
018|044|All sovereignty belongs only to Allah, the Truth. He is the best at rewarding and the best at determining outcomes.
018|045|And give them an example of the life of this world: it’s like water that We send down from the sky, absorbed by the earth’s plants, and it becomes debris that the winds scatter. Allah has the power over all things.
018|046|Wealth and children are the embellishments of worldly life. But the enduring righteous deeds hold more outstanding merit with your Lord, both in reward and hope.
018|047|On the Day when We set the mountains in motion, and you see the earth laid bare, We will gather them all, not leaving any of them behind.
018|048|They will be presented before your Lord: “You’ve come to Us as We created you the first time. Yet you assumed that We wouldn’t set a date for you.”
018|049|The document will be placed, and you’ll see the guilty fearful of its contents. They will lament, “Woe to us! What kind of document is this that omits nothing, small or large, but takes it into account?” They will find everything they did present. Your Lord doesn’t wrong anyone.
018|050|When We commanded the angels to prostrate themselves before Adam, they all did, except for Iblis. He belonged to jinn and deviated from his Lord’s command. Will you then take him and his offspring as allies, even though they are your enemies? Terrible is the exchange for the wrong-doers!
018|051|I didn’t make them witness the creation of the heavens and the earth, nor their own creation. I don’t take misleaders as helpers.
018|052|On that Day, He will say, “Call upon those you claimed were My partners.” They will call upon them, but they won’t answer them. We put a gap between them.
018|053|The wrongdoers will see the Fire, and realize they are about to fall into it. They will find no deliverance from it.
018|054|In this Quran, We present various parables for people, yet man is the most argumentative being.
018|055|What prevents people from believing and seeking their Lord’s forgiveness when the guidance comes to them? Unless the precedent of the ancients comes to them, or the torment comes to them face to face?
018|056|We send messengers only as bearers of good news and as warners. Yet, those who disbelieve argue with falsehood to defeat the truth, and they treat My signs and warnings as a joke.
018|057|Who is more unjust than the one who, when reminded of his Lord’s verses, turns away from them, and forgets what his hands have put forth? We place covers over their hearts, so they don’t understand it, and deafness in their ears. Even if you call them to guidance, they will never be guided at all.
018|058|Your Lord is All-Forgiving, Full of Mercy. If He were to call them to account for what they’ve earned, He would accelerate their punishment. But they have an appointed time from which they will find no escape.
018|059|And those cities—We destroyed them when they wronged, and We set a fixed time for their destruction.
018|060|When Moses said to his young servant, “I won’t give up until I reach the junction of the two seas, even if it takes me a long time.”
018|061|But when they reached the junction between them, they forgot their fish, which took its course into the sea, slipping away.
018|062|As they journeyed, he told his companion, “Bring us our lunch; we’ve experienced hardship on this journey.”
018|063|He replied, “Do you see when we rested by the rock? I forgot about the fish. Only Satan made me forget to remember it. Amazingly, it made its way into the sea.”
018|064|He said, “That’s what we were seeking!” So they returned following their footsteps.
018|065|Then they came across one of Our servants, to whom We had given mercy from Us and taught knowledge from Us.
018|066|Moses asked him, “May I follow you, so that you may teach me some of the righteousness you were taught?”
018|067|He answered, “You won’t be able to endure with me patiently.
018|068|How could you endure things that you don’t understand?”
018|069|He responded, “If Allah wills, you’ll find me patient, and I won’t disobey any of your instructions.”
018|070|He said, “If you follow me, then don’t question me about anything until I choose to explain it to you.”
018|071|They set out, until, when they boarded the boat, he made a hole in it. He exclaimed, “Did you make a hole in it to drown its passengers? You did a strange thing!”
018|072|He replied, “Didn’t I tell you that you couldn’t be patient with me?”
018|073|He responded, “Don’t reprimand me for forgetting, and don’t be harsh with me.”
018|074|They journeyed on. Upon encountering a boy, he killed him. He questioned, “Did you kill an innocent soul who hadn’t taken another’s life? You did a terrible thing!”
018|075|He replied, “Didn’t I tell you that you couldn’t be patient with me?”
018|076|He said, “If I ask you about anything after this, don’t keep me in your company. You’ve already received enough excuses from me.”
018|077|They journeyed on. Upon reaching a town, they asked its residents for food, but they denied them hospitality. There, they found a wall that was about to collapse, and he repaired it. He commented, “If you had wished, you could’ve demanded a wage for it.”
018|078|He said, “This is where we part ways. I am going to make known to you the interpretation of those things over which you couldn’t hold patience.
018|079|As for the boat, it belonged to poor people who worked at sea. I intended to damage it because a king was approaching who was seizing every boat by force.
018|080|As for the boy, his parents were believers, and we feared he would overburden them with transgression and disbelief.
018|081|So we desired that their Lord would give them in exchange someone better in purity and closer in mercy.
018|082|As for the wall, it belonged to two orphan boys in the city, and beneath it was a treasure that was theirs. Their father was righteous, and your Lord intended for them to reach maturity and retrieve their treasure. I didn’t act of my own accord. This is the interpretation of that over which you couldn’t be patient.”
018|083|They ask you about Dhul-Qarnayn. Say, “I will narrate a portion of his story to you.”
018|084|We established him on earth, and We provided him with a means to do all things.
018|085|He then continued his journey.
018|086|Upon reaching the setting of the sun, he found it setting in a vast muddy spring, and he found people there. We said, “O Dhul-Qarnayn, you can either punish or treat them with kindness.”
018|087|He answered, “As for those who commit wrongdoings, we will punish them. Then, they will be returned to their Lord, subjecting them to an even more severe punishment.
018|088|However, those who believe and perform righteous deeds will receive the finest rewards, we will command them in an easy way.”
018|089|He then continued on his way.
018|090|Upon reaching the rising point of the sun, he found it rising over a people for whom We had not provided any form of protection against it.
018|091|We had full knowledge of what he encountered during his journey.
018|092|Subsequently, he embarked on another expedition.
018|093|Upon reaching a pass between two mountains, he encountered people who could hardly understand any language.
018|094|They implored, “O Dhul-Qarnayn, Gog, and Magog are wreaking havoc in the land; could we possibly compensate you to build a barrier between us and them?’
018|095|He replied, “The strength my Lord has granted me is sufficient. Assist me, and I will erect a fortification between you and them.”
018|096|“Bring me blocks of iron.” Once he had filled the space between the two sides, he said, “Light it up!” Once it was red-hot, he directed, “Bring me molten copper to pour over it.”
018|097|As a result, they were unable to climb it or to tunnel through it.
018|098|He declared, “This is a mercy from my Lord. However, when my Lord’s promise is fulfilled, He will reduce it to rubble. The promise of my Lord is always true.”
018|099|On that Day, We will let them surge like waves into each other. Then the Trumpet will be blown, and We will gather them all together.
018|100|On that Day, We will expose Hell in full view for the unbelievers.
018|101|Those whose eyes were covered from My remembrance, and were unable to hear.
018|102|Do those who disbelieve presume they can take My servants as protectors instead of Me? We prepared Hell as a reception for the unbelievers.
018|103|Say, “Shall we inform you of who will be the greatest losers in respect to their deeds?”
018|104|“Those whose efforts in this worldly life are misguided, while they assume themselves to be doing well in work.”
018|105|These are the ones who denied their Lord’s signs and the meeting with Him. Therefore, their deeds are worthless, and We won’t assign any weight to them on Resurrection Day.
018|106|Their compensation will be Hell, because of their disbelief and mockery of My verses and messengers.
018|107|As for those who believe and perform righteous deeds, they will have the Gardens of Paradise as their place of hospitality.
018|108|There, they will reside eternally, with no desire for relocation.
018|109|Say, “If the ocean were ink for my Lord’s words, the ocean would run out, before my Lord’s words run out,” even if we replenished it with another like it.
018|110|Say, “I am only a human like you, revealed to me that your God is One God. Whoever is hopeful for the meeting with his Lord, let him act righteously, and not associate anyone in the worship of his Lord.”
019|001|Kaf. Ha. Ya. Ayn. Saad.
019|002|This is a mention of your Lord’s mercy towards His servant Zechariah.
019|003|When he silently invoked his Lord in a private prayer.
019|004|He said, “My Lord, my bones have grown frail, and my head is aflame with white hair. Yet, my Lord, I have never been unhappy in my prayer to You.
019|005|And I fear the successors after me, and my wife is barren, so grant me from Yourself an heir.
019|006|Who will inherit from me and the family of Jacob. And make him, my Lord, pleasing.”
019|007|“O Zechariah, We give you good news of a son, named John, a name We’ve never given before.”
019|008|He asked, “My Lord, how can I have a son when my wife is barren, and I have reached an advanced age?”
019|009|He replied, “So it will be; your Lord says, ‘It is easy for Me, just as I created you before, when you were nothing.’”
019|010|He asked, “My Lord, give me a sign.” He replied, “Your sign is that you won’t speak to people for three consecutive nights.”

019|012|“O John, adhere firmly to the Scripture.” We gave him wisdom while still a boy.
019|013|And affection from Us, and purity, and he was deeply devout.
019|014|And he was benevolent to his parents, and he was neither arrogant nor disobedient.
019|015|And peace be upon him the day he was born, the day he dies, and the day he is raised alive.

019|018|She exclaimed, “I seek refuge in the Most Merciful from you, if you are Allah-fearing.”
019|019|He replied, “I am the messenger of your Lord, to announce to you the gift of a pure son.”
019|020|She questioned, “How can I have a son, when no man has touched me, and I have not been immoral?”
019|021|He responded, “So it will be; your Lord says, ‘It is easy for Me. And We will make him a symbol for humanity, and mercy from Us. It is a matter already decided.’”
019|022|So she conceived him, and she withdrew with him to a remote place.
019|023|The pains of childbirth drove her to the trunk of a palm tree. She cried, “I wish I had died before this, and was completely forgotten!”
019|024|Then he called her from beneath her, “Grieve not; your Lord has placed a stream beneath you.
019|025|And shake the trunk of the palm-tree towards you, and it will drop upon you fresh, ripe dates.
019|026|So eat, drink, and find comfort. If you see any human, say, ‘I have vowed a fast to the Most Merciful, so I won’t speak to any person today.’”
019|027|Upon her return to her people, carrying him, they exclaimed, “O Mary, you’ve done something unthinkable!
019|028|O sister of Aaron, your father was not a man of disgrace, nor was your mother a woman of dishonor.”

019|030|He said, “I am the servant of Allah. He has given me the Scripture, and He made me a prophet.
019|031|He made me a blessing wherever I may be, and He enjoined upon me prayer and charity as long as I remain alive.
019|032|And kind to my mother, and He didn’t make me an arrogant oppressor.
019|033|Peace is upon me the day I was born, the day I will die, and the day I will be resurrected alive.”

019|036|“Allah is my Lord and your Lord, so worship Him. This is a straight path.”
019|037|However, the factions disagreed among themselves. Woe to those who disbelieve—from the scene of a tremendous Day.
019|038|How keen their hearing, how sharp their sight, the Day they come to Us. But the wrongdoers today are in clear error.

019|040|It is We who will inherit the earth and all who are on it, and to Us, they will be returned.

019|042|When he said to his father, “O my father, why do you worship what can neither hear nor see and can’t benefit you in any way?
019|043|O my father, a specific knowledge that didn’t come to you has come to me. So follow me, and I will guide you to a straight path.
019|044|O my father, don’t worship Satan. Satan has been rebellious against the Most Merciful.
019|045|My dear father, I fear that a punishment from the Compassionate may afflict you, and you become an ally to Satan.”
019|046|He replied, “Are you renouncing my gods, O Abraham? If you don’t desist, I will surely stone you. Now leave me for a long while.”
019|047|He responded, “Peace be upon you. I will ask forgiveness for you from my Lord. He is always gracious to me.
019|048|And I will distance myself from you and what you invoke besides Allah, and I will pray to my Lord. Perhaps I won’t be unhappy in my supplication to my Lord.”
019|049|When he had distanced himself from them and from what they worship besides Allah, We gave him Isaac and Jacob, and each We made a prophet.
019|050|And We showered them with Our mercy, and We made for them a lofty reputation of truth.

019|054|Furthermore, mention in the Scripture, Ishmael. He was faithful to his promise, and was a messenger, a prophet.
019|055|He used to command his family to pray and to give charity, and he was pleasing to his Lord.
019|056|And mention in the Scripture, Enoch. He was a man of integrity, a prophet.
019|057|We elevated him to an esteemed status.
019|058|These are some of the prophets whom Allah blessed; from the progeny of Adam, and those We carried with Noah, and from the offspring of Abraham and Israel, and from those We guided and selected. When the verses of the Most Gracious were recited to them, they collapsed bowing and weeping.
019|059|Yet there succeeded them successors who neglected the prayers and pursued their desires. They will face devastation.
019|060|Except for those who repent, believe, and act righteously, these will enter Paradise, and they won’t be wronged in the slightest.

019|062|No idle talk will they hear therein, only words of peace. They will receive their sustenance therein, morning and evening.
019|063|This is the Paradise that We will grant to Our righteous servants.
019|064|“We descend only by the command of our Lord. To Him belongs what’s ahead of us, what’s behind us, and what lies in between. Your Lord is never forgetful.”
019|065|Lord of the heavens, the earth, and what’s between them. So worship Him, and remain steadfast in His worship. Do you know of any counterpart for Him?
019|066|Man asks, “When I am dead, will I then be raised up alive?”
019|067|Doesn’t man remember that We created him before, when he was nothing?

019|069|Then, We will extract from each group those who were most defiant towards the Most Merciful.

019|071|Every single one of you will traverse it; this is an irrevocable decree from your Lord.
019|072|Then, We will rescue the righteous and leave the wrongdoers within it, on their knees.
019|073|When Our clear verses are presented to them, those who disbelieve say to those who believe, “Which of the two parties is better in position and better in association?”
019|074|And how many a generation have We destroyed before them who were better in possessions and outward appearance?

019|079|Absolutely not! We will write what he says, and We will prolong his agony for him.
