020|001|Ta-Ha.
020|002|We didn’t reveal the Quran upon you to cause you distress.
020|003|Rather, it’s a reminder for those who hold reverence.
020|004|A revelation from He who created the earth and the high heavens.
020|005|The Most Merciful, who is established on the Throne.
020|006|To Him belongs everything in the heavens, everything on earth, everything between them, and everything beneath the soil.
020|007|Whether you speak aloud—He knows the secret and what’s more hidden.
020|008|Allah—there is no god except Him. His are the best names.
020|009|Did you hear the story of Moses?
020|010|When he saw a fire, he told his family, “Stay here, I have noticed a fire. Perhaps I can bring you a torch from it, or find guidance at the fire.”
020|011|As he approached it, he was called, “O Moses!
020|012|I. I am your Lord. Remove your shoes; you are in the sacred valley of Tuwa.
020|013|I have chosen you, so listen to what’s being revealed.
020|014|Surely, it is I. I am Allah. There is no deity except Me. So, worship Me and establish prayer for My remembrance.
020|015|The Hour is coming; I keep it almost hidden, so that every soul may be recompensed for its endeavors.
020|016|Therefore, let not those who don’t believe in it and follow their lusts hinder you from it, else you be ruined.
020|017|And what’s that in your right hand, O Moses?”
020|018|He replied, “It is my staff. I lean on it, herd my sheep with it, and I have other uses for it.”
020|019|He instructed, “Throw it down, O Moses.”
020|020|When he threw it down, it instantly became a moving serpent.
020|021|He said, “Pick it up, and fear not; We will restore it to its original state.
020|022|Now, put your hand under your arm; it will come out white, without any harm—another sign.
020|023|That We may show you some of Our greater signs.
020|024|Go to Pharaoh, for he became tyrannical.”
020|025|He said, “My Lord, calm my heart for me.
020|026|And ease my task for me.
020|027|And remove the knot from my tongue.
020|028|So they may understand my speech.
020|029|Grant me a helper from my family.
020|030|Aaron, my brother.
020|031|Strengthen me through him.
020|032|And let him share in my mission.
020|033|In order to frequently glorify Your praises.
020|034|And remember You frequently.
020|035|You are always watchful over us.”
020|036|He replied, “You have been granted your request, O Moses!
020|037|We’ve favored you before.
020|038|When We inspired your mother with Our message:
020|039|“Put him in a chest and cast it into the river. The river will wash him ashore, where an enemy of Mine and his will take him.” I bestowed upon you love from Me, so that you would be nurtured under My watchful eye.
020|040|Then your sister stepped forward, suggesting, ‘May I direct you to someone who could assist in his upbringing?’ Thus, We returned you to your mother to soothe her heart and relieve her grief. After you had killed a man, We saved you from anxiety and tested you thoroughly. You resided among the people of Midian for several years, until you reached your predestined term, O Moses.
020|041|I prepared you for Myself.
020|042|Go, you and your brother, with My signs, And don’t slacken in My Remembrance.
020|043|Approach Pharaoh, for he transgressed.
020|044|But speak to him mildly; perhaps he may remember or fear.”
020|045|They responded, “Our Lord, we fear that he might lash out against us or become even more tyrannical.”
020|046|He reassured, “Fear not, for I am with you both. I hear, and I see.
020|047|Go to him and say, ‘We are the messengers of your Lord, so send with us the Children of Israel and don’t torment them. We’ve come to you with a sign from your Lord, and peace is upon those who follow the guidance.
020|048|It has been revealed to us that the punishment is upon whoever denies and turns away.’”
020|049|He asked, “Who is your Lord, O Moses?”
020|050|He answered, “Our Lord is the One who gave everything its creation, then guided.”
020|051|He asked, “What was the condition of the earlier generations?”
020|052|He answered, “knowledge about them is with my Lord, documented in a record. My Lord neither errs nor forgets.”
020|053|He who made the earth a habitat for you, and He traced out routes within it. And He sends down water from the sky, with which We produce diverse pairs of plants.
020|054|Eat and let your livestock graze. In this, there are signs for those with discernment.
020|055|From it, We created you, and into it, We will return you. And from it, We will extract you once again.
020|056|We showed him all Our signs, but he denied and refused.
020|057|He said, “Did you come to evict us from our land with your magic, O Moses?
020|058|We will bring you magic like it. So, set a date between us and you, in a neutral place, which neither we nor you will fail to attend.”
020|059|He replied, “Your appointment is on Festival Day, and let the people gather in the morning.”
020|060|Pharaoh turned his back, formulated his plan, and then came back.
020|061|Moses cautioned them, “Woe to you! Don’t forge lies against Allah, lest He destroys you with a punishment; and whoever fabricates lies is bound to fail.”
020|062|They discussed their matter amongst themselves and kept their counsel secret.
020|063|They declared, “These two are magicians who intend to expel you from your land with their magic and abolish your exemplary tradition.
020|064|So, formulate your strategy and come forward as a united front. And indeed, he will succeed this day who is superior.”
020|065|They challenged, “O Moses, either you throw, or we will be the first to throw.”
020|066|He replied, “Rather, you throw.” And suddenly, their ropes and staffs seemed to him from their magic that they were moving.
020|067|And Moses felt fear within himself.
020|068|We said, “Don’t be scared; you have the upper hand.
020|069|Throw that which is in your right hand; it will swallow what they’ve crafted, mere illusions of a magician’s trickery. A magician won’t succeed, wherever he may turn.”
020|070|So the magicians fell down prostrating. They said, “We have believed in the Lord of Aaron and Moses.”
020|071|He threatened, “You dare to believe in Him without my permission? He must be your superior who taught you magic. I will sever your hands and feet on opposite sides, and I will crucify you on the trunks of palm trees. Then you’ll know whose punishment is harsher and more lasting.”
020|072|They responded, “We will never prefer you over the clear proofs that have come to us, nor over Him who created us. So issue whatever decree you wish; your jurisdiction extends only to the life of this world.
020|073|We have put our trust in our Lord, hoping He may forgive our sins and the magic you compelled us to practice. Allah is far superior and everlasting.”
020|074|Whoever comes before his Lord as guilty, for him is hell, where he neither dies nor lives.
020|075|But whoever comes before Him as a believer, having performed righteous deeds—those will attain the highest stages.
020|076|The eternal Gardens of Eternity, through which rivers flow, where they will reside forever—this is the reward for those who purify themselves.
020|077|We revealed to Moses: “Set out at night with My servants, and strike a dry path for them through the sea, without fear of being overtaken or dread.”
020|078|Pharaoh pursued them with his forces, but the sea overwhelmed them, completely submerging them.
020|079|Pharaoh misled his people; he didn’t guide them.
020|080|O Children of Israel, We saved you from your enemy, covenanted with you on the right side of the Mount, and We sent down to you Manna and Quail.
020|081|Eat from the good provisions We provided you, but don’t be excessive in it, lest My wrath descends upon you. Whoever upon whom My wrath descends has fallen.
020|082|I am forgiving to whoever repents, believes, acts righteously, then becomes guided.
020|083|“Why did you rush ahead of your people, O Moses?”
020|084|He replied, “They are on my tracks. I rushed to You, my Lord, so that You might be pleased.”
020|085|He said, “We’ve tested your people in your absence, and the Samarian led them astray.”
020|086|Moses returned to his people, angry and grieved. He said, “O my people, didn’t your Lord make a good promise to you? Did the promise appear too distant to you, or did you wish that wrath from your Lord descends upon you, that you broke your promise to me?”
020|087|They replied, “We didn’t break our promise to you intentionally, but we were made to carry burdens of the people’s ornaments, and we cast them in, as the Samarian suggested.”
020|088|Then he produced for them a statue of a calf which made a mooing sound. They said, “This is your god and the god of Moses, but he forgot.”
020|089|Didn’t they see that it could neither respond to them nor bring them harm or benefit?
020|090|Aaron had already pleaded with them, “O my people, you are being tested by this. Your Lord is the Most Gracious, so follow me and obey my order.”
020|091|They replied, “We won’t cease our devotion to it until Moses returns to us.”
020|092|He said, “O Aaron, what prevented you when you saw them straying?
020|093|From following me? Did you disobey my command?”
020|094|He replied, “O son of my mother, don’t seize me by my beard or head. I feared you would accuse me of causing division among the Children of Israel and not adhering to your words.”
020|095|He then asked, “What’s your explanation, O Samarian?”
020|096|He answered, “I saw what they didn’t see, so I grabbed a handful of the messenger’s trace, and I threw it. That’s what my inner self prompted me to do.”
020|097|Moses declared, “Go away! In this life, you must say, ‘No contact!’ And you have an appointment you can’t evade. Now, look at your god to which you remained devoted. We will burn it and then scatter it into the sea as dust.”
020|098|Your God is the only God, besides whom there is no other god. He encompasses everything in knowledge.
020|099|Thus, We narrate to you some of the stories of what happened before, and We’ve given you from us a Reminder.
020|100|Whoever turns away from it will carry a burden on Resurrection Day.
020|101|They will remain under it forever, an evil for them to bear on Resurrection Day.
020|102|On that Day, the Trumpet is blown, and We will gather the criminals on that Day, blue.
020|103|Whispering among themselves, “You didn’t remain except for ten.”
020|104|We know well what they will say, when the most exemplary among them will say, “You stayed no more than a day.”
020|105|They ask you about the mountains, so say, “My Lord will crumble them into dust.
020|106|He will leave them as a level plain.
020|107|You will see neither elevation or depression in them.”
020|108|On that Day, they will follow the caller without deviation. Voices will be lowered for the Most Merciful, so you will not hear but a whisper.
020|109|On that Day, intercession won’t benefit at all, except for those to whom the Most Merciful has granted permission and whose words He has approved.
020|110|He knows their past and their future, and they can’t comprehend His knowledge.
020|111|All faces will humbly submit to the Ever-Living, the Sustainer. Whoever carries injustice will despair.
020|112|However, those who performed righteous deeds and are believers won’t fear injustice or deprivation.
020|113|We revealed this Quran in Arabic, and We diversified the warnings in it, to foster righteousness or serve as a reminder for them.
020|114|Exalted is Allah, the True King. Don’t hasten with the Quran before its revelation is completed to you, and say, “My Lord, increase me in knowledge.”
020|115|We had previously covenanted with Adam, but he forgot, and We found no resolve in him.
020|116|When We commanded the angels, “Prostrate yourselves before Adam,” they all complied, except for Iblis, who refused.
020|117|We said, “O Adam, this is an enemy to you and your wife. Don’t let him drive you out of Paradise, or you will be miserable.
020|118|In it, you will never experience hunger or nakedness.
020|119|And you won’t be thirsty or suffer from the sun’s heat.”
020|120|Then Satan whispered to him, saying, “O Adam, Shall I lead you to the tree of eternity and a kingdom that never decays?”
020|121|So they ate from it, and their nakedness was revealed to them. Consequently, they started covering themselves with leaves from the Garden. Adam disobeyed his Lord and strayed.
020|122|But then, his Lord selected him, accepted his repentance, and provided guidance.
020|123|He commanded, “Descend from it, all of you, some of you enemies to others. However, when guidance from Me comes to you, those who follow My guidance will neither go astray nor be miserable.
020|124|However, those who disregard My reminder will have a life of hardship, and on the Day of Resurrection, We will resurrect them blind.”
020|125|He will protest, “My Lord, why did You resurrect me blind, though I was sighted?”
020|126|He will reply, “Just as Our revelations came to you, and you dismissed them, so today, you are dismissed.”
020|127|This is how We recompense those who transgress and deny their Lord’s revelations. The punishment of the Hereafter is harsher and more lasting.
020|128|Didn’t they consider how many generations We annihilated before them, in whose dwellings they now roam? There are signs in this for those who possess insight.
020|129|Without a predetermined decree from your Lord and a set term, their doom would’ve been inevitable.
020|130|Therefore, patiently endure their words, and glorify and praise your Lord before sunrise and sunset. And praise Him during the night, and at the day’s extremities, so you may be content.
020|131|Don’t extend your eyes toward what We granted categories among them to enjoy—the splendor of the life of this world—through which We test them. The provision of your Lord is better and more lasting.
020|132|Command your family to establish prayer, and steadfastly maintain it. We don’t ask you for provision; We provide for you. The outcome is for righteousness.
020|133|They say, “Why doesn’t he bring us a sign from his Lord?” Didn’t they receive sufficient evidence in the previous Scriptures?
020|134|If We had annihilated them with a punishment before this, they would have said, “Our Lord, why didn’t You send us a messenger, so we could follow Your verses before we were humiliated and disgraced.”
020|135|Say, “Everyone is waiting; so wait. You will soon know who are the followers of the straight path, and who is guided.”
021|001|The reckoning of humanity is drawing near, yet they remain in heedless disregard.
021|002|Whenever a revelation comes to them from their Lord, fresh, they listen to it while they play.
021|003|With their hearts preoccupied, the wrongdoers confide in private: “Isn’t he just a man like you? Are you going to yield to magic while you can clearly see?”
021|004|He responded, “My Lord knows every word spoken in the heavens and on earth. He is the All-Hearing, the All-Knowing.”
021|005|They even say, “A jumble of dreams,” or “He made it up,” or “He is just a poet.” “Let him bring us a sign, just as the ancients received.”
021|006|Not even one of the cities that we destroyed before them believed; will they then believe?
021|007|We sent before you only men to whom we revealed. Ask the people of the message, if you don’t know.
021|008|We didn’t make them bodies that didn’t eat food, nor were they immortal.
021|009|Then, We fulfilled Our promise to them, rescuing them and those We willed while obliterating the transgressors.
021|010|We revealed to you a Scripture that mentions you explicitly. Don’t you understand?
021|011|How many sinful communities We shatter, and after them, raised other people?
021|012|When they sensed Our power approaching, they tried to flee from it.
021|013|“Don’t run. Return to your luxuries and your homes, so you may be questioned.”
021|014|They cried out, “Alas to us! We were indeed wrongdoers.”
021|015|This cry of theirs continued until We made them like harvested crops, extinguished.
021|016|We didn’t create the heavens, the earth, and everything in between for a pastime.
021|017|If we had wanted to take a pastime, We could have taken it from with Us—if We were to do so.
021|018|Instead, We hurl the truth against falsehood, and it crushes it, leaving it utterly vanquished. Woe unto you, for what you described!
021|019|Everything in the heavens and on earth is His. Those in His presence aren’t too proud to worship Him, nor do they tire.
021|020|They glorify night and day, without ceasing.
021|021|Did they choose gods from the earth who can resurrect?
021|022|If there were gods besides Allah in either of them, they would’ve gone to ruin. Praise be to Allah, the Lord of the Throne, exalted above what they describe.
021|023|He is not questioned about what He does, but they will be questioned.
021|024|Have they chosen other gods besides Him? Say, “Bring your proof. This is a reminder for those with me and a reminder for those before me.” Yet, most of them don’t know the truth and turn away.
021|025|We revealed to every messenger before you, “There is no god but I; so worship me.”
021|026|And they say, “The Most Merciful has begotten a child.” Glorified be He! Rather, they are honored servants.
021|027|They don’t precede Him in speech, and they act only upon His command.
021|028|He knows their past and their future. They can’t intercede except for those He approves of. They stand in awe and reverence of Him.
021|029|Should any among them dare to say, “I am a god besides Him,” We will recompense him with Hell; this is the recompense of transgressors.
021|030|Do the disbelievers not see that the heavens and the earth were a joined entity, which We then separated? And from water, We brought forth all living things. Will they not then believe?
021|031|We placed upon it firm mountains, lest it should shake with them, and We made therein passageways, so they may be guided.
021|032|We made the sky a protected ceiling, yet they turn away from its signs.
021|033|It is He who created the night, the day, the sun, and the moon, each gliding in an orbit.
021|034|We didn’t grant any human before you immortality. So, if you were to die, would they then live forever?
021|035|Every soul will taste death. We burden you with bad and good—a test. And to Us, you will be returned.
021|036|When the unbelievers see you, they take you for mockery: “Is this the one who speaks about your gods?” Yet they deny the mention of the Most Merciful.
021|037|Man was created hasty. I will show you My signs, so don’t rush.
021|038|And they ask, “When will this promise be fulfilled, if you are truthful?”
021|039|If those who disbelieved only knew, when they won’t be able to fend off the fire from their faces or their backs, and they won’t be aided.
021|040|It will come upon them suddenly, and they will become startled. They won’t be able to repel it nor will they be granted respite.
021|041|Messengers before you were also ridiculed, but those who mocked were then engulfed by what they used to mock.
021|042|Say, “Who is there to protect you, night and day, from the Merciful?” Yet, they turn away from the remembrance of their Lord.
021|043|Do they have gods who can protect them from Us? They can’t help themselves, and they won’t be protected from Us.
021|044|We allowed them and their ancestors to enjoy extended periods of comfort and luxury. Don’t they see how We gradually reduce the land from its borders? Are they then the victors?
021|045|Say, “I only warn you by revelation.” However, the deaf won’t hear the call when they are warned.
021|046|Yet if a breath of your Lord’s punishment were to touch them, they would cry out, “Woe to us, we were indeed wrongdoers.”
021|047|On the Day of Resurrection, We will establish the scales of justice. No soul will be wronged in the slightest. Even if it’s the weight of a mustard seed, We will bring it in. And sufficient are We as accountants.
021|048|We gave Moses and Aaron the Criterion, a light, and a reminder for the righteous.
021|049|Those who fear their Lord in private and dread the Hour.
021|050|This, too, is a blessed message that We revealed. Will you then deny it?
021|051|We had previously given Abraham wisdom, and We were well aware of him.
021|052|He questioned his father and his people, “What are these idols to which you are so devoted?”
021|053|They replied, “We found our ancestors worshiping them.”
021|054|He stated, “You and your ancestors have been in manifest error.”
021|055|They asked, “Did you bring us the truth, or are you merely playing?”
021|056|He responded, “Indeed, your Lord is the Lord of the heavens and the earth, He who originated them, and I am to this a witness.
021|057|And by Allah, I will plan against your idols after you have gone away.”
021|058|So he reduced them to fragments, except their largest, so they might return to it.
021|059|They exclaimed, “Who did this to our gods? He must be a villain.”
021|060|They said, “We heard a young man mention them; his name is Abraham.”
021|061|They demanded, “Bring him before the eyes of the people, that they may testify.”
021|062|They interrogated, “Was it you who did this to our gods, O Abraham?”
021|063|He responded, “No, this, their biggest one did it. Ask them, if they can speak.”
021|064|So they turned to themselves and said, “You yourselves are the wrongdoers.”
021|065|But then they were reverted to their former notion: “You know well that these can’t speak.”
021|066|He countered, “Do you then worship, instead of Allah, things that can neither benefit you at all nor harm you?
021|067|Shame on you and what you worship besides Allah! Do you have any sense?”
021|068|They demanded, “Burn him and support your gods, if you are to act.”
021|069|We said, “O fire, be cool and safe for Abraham.”
021|070|They plotted to harm him, but We made them the greatest losers.
021|071|We saved him and Lot, bringing them to the land We had blessed for all the worlds.
021|072|We granted him Isaac and Jacob additionally, and we made each of them righteous.
021|073|We made them leaders who guided by Our command, and We inspired them to do good deeds, establish prayer, and give alms. They were worshippers of Us.
021|074|And to Lot, We gave wisdom and knowledge, and We saved him from the city that practiced the abominations. They were wicked and sinful people.
021|075|We brought him into Our mercy; he was among the righteous.
021|076|And Noah, when he called out to Us before, We responded to him and saved him and his family from the great distress.
021|077|And We supported him against the people who denied Our signs. They were evil people, so We drowned them all.
021|078|And David and Solomon, when they judged concerning the field, when some people’s sheep strayed and grazed therein. We were witnesses to their judgment.
021|079|We granted Solomon understanding of it, and We bestowed on them wisdom and knowledge. We made the mountains and birds join David in Our praises. This was Our doing.
021|080|And We taught him the craft of making coats of armor for you, to protect you in your wars. Will you then be grateful?
021|081|To Solomon, We subjected the wind, blowing forcefully at his command towards the land that We had blessed. We are aware of all things.
021|082|To him, we assigned some devils who dived and performed various minor tasks, but We kept them under strict control.
021|083|And Job, when he implored his Lord, “Adversity has afflicted me, yet You are the Most Merciful of the merciful.”
021|084|We responded to him, alleviated his suffering, and restored his family to him, along with others like them, as a mercy from Us, and a reminder for the worshippers.
021|085|And Ishmael, Enoch, and Ezekiel—each of them was among the patient.
021|086|We embraced them in Our mercy, for they were among the righteous.
021|087|And Jonah, when he stormed out in fury, thinking We had no power over him. Then he called out in the darkness, “There is no god but You! Glory be to You! Indeed, I was among the wrongdoers!”
021|088|So We answered him and saved him from the distress. Thus We save the believers.
021|089|And Zechariah, when he implored his Lord, “My Lord, don’t leave me alone, while You are the best of inheritors.”
021|090|So We answered him and gave him John, and remedied his wife for him. They were always quick to perform good deeds, and they called upon Us with fervor and humility; they were devout to us.
021|091|And she who guarded her chastity, so We breathed into her from Our spirit, and We made her and her son a sign for all peoples.
021|092|This community of yours is a single community, and I am your Lord, so worship Me alone.
021|093|Yet they fragmented their religion among themselves, but all will return to Us.
021|094|Whoever acts righteously, while a believer, his efforts won’t be denied. We write it down for him.
021|095|There is a ban upon any city We’ve destroyed; they may not return.
021|096|Until when Gog and Magog are let loose, and they swoop down from every height.
021|097|And when the true promise draws near, then behold, the eyes of those who disbelieved will be staring in horror: “Alas for us! We were oblivious to this; indeed, we were wrongdoers.”

021|099|Had these been gods, they wouldn’t have been entered into it. All will remain therein eternally.
021|100|There, they will groan; there, they won’t be heard.
021|101|Those for whom We decreed the best will be kept far removed from it.

021|106|In this there is a message for a people who worship.

022|001|O people, beware of your Lord, for the quake of the Hour is something tremendous.
022|002|On the Day you witness it, every nursing mother will forget her nursling, and every pregnant woman will miscarry. You will see people drunk, yet they are not drunk. The punishment of Allah is severe.
022|003|Some people argue about Allah without knowledge, guided by every rebellious devil.
022|004|It has been decreed about him, that whoever turns to him, he will mislead him and guide him to the suffering of the Blaze.
022|005|O people, if you doubt the Resurrection, We created you from dust, then from a drop, then from a clinging clot, and then from a lump, formed and unformed, to show you. We settle in the wombs whom We will for a preordained term, then We bring you out as infants, until you reach your full strength. Some of you may pass away, while others are returned to the feeblest old age, so they know nothing after knowing much. You see the earth barren, but when We send down rain upon it, it stirs, swells, and produces every delightful pair.
022|006|This is because Allah is the Ultimate Truth, revives the dead, and has power over all things.
022|007|The Hour is to come—there is no doubt about it—Allah will resurrect those who are in the graves.
022|008|Some people argue about Allah without knowledge, guidance, or an enlightening Scripture.
022|009|They bend it to mislead others from Allah’s path. For them is humiliation in this world, and on Resurrection Day, We will make them taste the punishment of the Burning Fire.
022|010|This is what your hands sent ahead, and Allah is never unjust to the servants.
022|011|Among people, there is one who worships Allah on edge. If good touches him, he is content, but if a trial strikes him, he reverts, losing both this world and the Hereafter. This is the clear loss.
022|012|He prays to, instead of Allah, what neither harms nor benefits him. That is straying far.
022|013|He invokes one whose harm is closer than his benefit—what an evil patron and what an evil companion!
022|014|Allah will admit those who believe and act righteously into Gardens through which rivers flow. Allah does whatever He wills.
022|015|Whoever thinks that Allah won’t help him in this life and the Hereafter, let him extend to the sky, cut, and see if his strategy eliminates what enrages him.
022|016|And thus, We sent it down as clear signs, and surely, Allah guides whom He wills.
022|017|Those who believe, the Jews, the Sabeans, the Christians, the Zoroastrians, and those who associate—Allah will judge between them on Resurrection Day. Allah is a Witness over all things.
022|018|Don’t you see that everything in the heavens and the earth bows down to Allah—the sun, the moon, the stars, the mountains, the trees, the animals, and many people? Yet, many are deserving of suffering. Whomsoever Allah humiliates, none can honor. Allah does what He wills.
022|019|These are two opponents who dispute concerning their Lord. For those who disbelieve, garments of fire will be tailored, and scalding water will be poured over their heads.
022|020|Melting their insides and their skins.
022|021|For them are iron maces.
022|022|Every time they seek to escape their torment, they are returned to it: “Taste the punishment of the blazing Fire!”
022|023|However, Allah will admit those who believe and act righteously into Gardens beneath which rivers flow, where they’ll be adorned with bracelets of gold and pearls, and their clothing will be of silk.
022|024|They’ve been guided to good speech and to the path of the Praiseworthy.
022|025|Those who disbelieve and obstruct Allah’s path and the Sacred Mosque—which We’ve designated for all people, whether they reside nearby or are from afar—anyone who seeks to desecrate it with wickedness, We will make them taste a severe punishment.
022|026|We showed Abraham the site of the House: “Don’t associate anything with Me, and purify My House for those who circumambulate it, stand in prayer, bow down, and prostrate.”
022|027|Announce the pilgrimage to humanity. They will come to you on foot and every mode of transport, coming from every distant pass.
022|028|To witness benefits, and to commemorate Allah’s name during the known days, for providing them with livestock. So, eat from them and feed the destitute poor.
022|029|Then, let them complete their rites, fulfill their vows, and circumambulate the Ancient House.
022|030|That is the command. Whoever respects the sanctities of Allah, it’s best for him with his Lord. Livestock is permissible for you, except for those explicitly prohibited. Shun the filth of idols, and avoid false speech.
022|031|Being devoted to Allah, not associating anything with Him. Whoever associates partners with Allah, it is as though he has fallen from the sky and is either snatched by birds or carried away by the wind to a distant place.
022|032|So it is. Whoever venerates Allah’s symbols is from the purity of the hearts.
022|033|There are benefits for you in them for a specified term; their final destination is the Ancient House.
022|034|We instituted a rite for every community so they may mention Allah’s name over the livestock He provided for them. Your God is One God, so surrender to Him, and give good news to the humble.
022|035|Those whose hearts tremble at the mention of Allah, those who persevere in patience in whatever afflicts them, who establish prayer, and who spend out of what We’ve provided them.
022|036|We designated the sacrificial animals among Allah’s symbols for you. They hold benefits for you. When they are lined up, pronounce Allah’s name over them. Once they have fallen on their sides, eat from them and feed those in need, whether they ask or not. Thus, We tamed them to you, so you may give thanks.
022|037|Neither their flesh nor their blood reaches Allah, but your piety does. He tamed them to you, to extol Allah’s greatness for guiding you. Give good news to the doers of good.
022|038|Allah defends the believers. Allah has no love for any ungrateful traitor.
022|039|Permission is given to those who were fought against because they were wronged; indeed, Allah can grant them victory.
022|040|Those who were unjustly evicted from their homes, simply for saying, “Our Lord is Allah.” Had Allah not repelled some people by means of others, numerous monasteries, churches, synagogues, and mosques, where Allah’s name is frequently invoked, would’ve been demolished. Allah will support those who support His cause. Allah is Powerful and Mighty.
022|041|Those who, when We empower them on earth, establish prayer, give charity, promote what’s right, and forbid what’s wrong. The final decision in all matters belongs to Allah.
022|042|If they reject you, so before them, the people of Noah and Aad and Thamud had rejected.
022|043|And the people of Abraham, and the people of Lot.
022|044|And the inhabitants of Midian. Moses, too, was accused of lying. I granted delay to the unbelievers, then I seized them. So how terrible was My condemnation?
022|045|How many a town did We destroy while it was committing wrong? They now lie in ruins, with abandoned wells and lofty mansions.
022|046|Didn’t they travel through the earth and use their intellect to understand, and their ears to listen? It’s not the eyes that go blind, but it’s the hearts in the chests that do.
022|047|They challenge you to hasten the punishment, but Allah will never fail in His promise. A day with your Lord is like a thousand years by your calculations.
022|048|And how many a town did I prolong while it was committing wrong? To Me is the ultimate return.
022|049|Say, “O people, I am only a clear warner to you.”
022|050|Those who believe and perform righteous deeds will receive forgiveness and a generous reward.
022|051|But those who strive to frustrate Our revelations will be inhabitants of Hell.
022|052|We never sent a messenger or a prophet before you without Satan attempting to interfere with his desires. Yet, Allah nullifies what Satan insinuates, and Allah reinforces His revelations. Allah is All-Knowing, All-Wise.
022|053|Satan’s insinuations are a trial for those with diseased and hardened hearts. The wrongdoers are in profound discord.
022|054|Those endowed with knowledge recognize the truth from your Lord; they believe in it, and their hearts humble to it. Allah guides those who believe to a straight path.
022|055|But the unbelievers will remain in doubt until the Hour suddenly overtakes them—or the punishment of a barren day befalls them.
022|056|On that Day, the dominion will belong exclusively to Allah; He will judge between them. Those who believed and did righteous deeds will be in the Gardens of Bliss.
022|057|But those who disbelieved and denied Our signs—for those there will be a humiliating punishment.
022|058|Those who emigrated for Allah’s cause and were then killed or died, Allah will provide for them a good provision. Allah is the best of providers.
022|059|He will admit them to an entrance they will find pleasing. Allah is All-Knowing, Most Forbearing.
022|060|That is so. If anyone retaliates in equivalence to the harm inflicted upon him, and is transgressed upon, Allah will assist him. Allah is Pardoning and forgiving.
022|061|That is because Allah merges night into day and day into night; Allah is Hearing and Seeing.
022|062|That is because Allah is the Reality, while what they call upon besides Him is falsehood; and because Allah is the Most High, the Grand.
022|063|Didn’t you see how Allah sends down water from the sky, causing the earth to become green? Allah is Subtle and Aware.
022|064|To Him belongs everything in the heavens and the earth. Allah is the Self-Sufficient, the Praiseworthy.
022|065|Didn’t you see how Allah made everything on earth subservient to you? Ships sail the sea by His laws. He holds the sky from falling on earth, unless by His permission. Allah is Compassionate and Merciful to humankind.
022|066|It is He who gave you life, will cause you to die, and will then revive you. Yet, man is ungrateful.
022|067|For every community, We established certain rites which they follow, so don’t let their disputes entangle you. Instead, invite to your Lord. You are on a straight path.
022|068|If they argue with you, say, “Allah knows best about what you’re doing.”
022|069|On the Day of Resurrection, Allah will judge between you, resolving all your disputes.
022|070|Don’t you know that Allah is aware of everything in the heavens and the earth? All of this is recorded in a book; this is easy for Allah.
022|071|They worship, besides Allah, what He didn’t authorize, which they have no knowledge of. The wrongdoers will have no supporter.
022|072|When Our clear verses are conveyed to them, you will notice disdain on the faces of the unbelievers. They nearly assault those who convey Our verses to them. Say, “Shall I inform you of something worse than that? The Fire which Allah has promised those who disbelieve, and wretched is the destination!”
022|073|O people, a parable is presented; listen to it attentively: those you call upon besides Allah can’t even create a fly, even if they combined their efforts. And if a fly were to snatch something away from them, they would be unable to retrieve it. Both the seeker and the sought are weak.

022|076|He knows their past and their future. All matters will return to Allah.
022|077|O you who believe, bow and prostrate yourselves, and worship your Lord, and do good, so that you may succeed.
022|078|Strive for Allah with the striving due to Him. He has chosen you and imposed no difficulty upon you in religion—the way of your forefather Abraham. He named you ‘Submitters’ from before, and in this, so that the Messenger may bear witness over you, and you may bear witness over the people. Therefore, establish prayers, give charity, and hold fast to Allah. He is your Protector—a splendid Guardian and a superb Helper.
023|001|The believers have attained success.
023|002|Those who are humble in their prayers.
023|003|Those who avoid vain talk.
023|004|Those who are active in charitable deeds.
023|005|Those who protect their chastity.
023|006|Except from their wives or what their right hands possess, for they aren’t to be blamed.
023|007|However, those who seek beyond that are the transgressors.
023|008|Those who faithfully uphold their trusts and promises.
023|009|And those who guard their prayers.
023|010|These are the inheritors.
023|011|Who will inherit Paradise, therein to dwell forever.
023|012|We created man from an extract of clay.
023|013|Then, We placed him as a drop in a secure dwelling place.
023|014|Then, We transformed the drop into a clot, then developed the clot into a lump, then shaped the lump into bones, then clothed the bones with flesh. Then, We brought him forth as another creation. So, blessed is Allah, the Best of Creators.
023|015|Afterward, you will surely die.
023|016|Then, on the Day of Resurrection, you will be resurrected.
023|017|We created above you seven pathways, and We are never unmindful of creation.
023|018|We send down water from the sky in due measure, storing it within the earth, and We can take it away.
023|019|Through it, We produce for you gardens of date palms and vineyards, yielding abundant fruits from which you eat.
023|020|Also, a tree that springs forth from Mount Sinai, producing oil and relish for the eaters.
023|021|In livestock, too, there is a lesson for you: We provide you with a drink from what’s in their bellies, and there are numerous other benefits for you in them, and of them, you eat.
023|022|And on them, as well as on ships, you are transported.
023|023|We sent Noah to his people, and he pleaded, “O my people, worship Allah; you have no god but Him. Will you not then be righteous?”
023|024|However, the leaders of his people who disbelieved said, “This is nothing but a man like yourselves, seeking to assert dominance over you. If Allah had willed, He could’ve sent down angels. We’ve never heard of this from our forefathers.
023|025|He is only a man with delusions. Just ignore him for a while.”
023|026|He prayed, “My Lord, assist me, because they have rejected me.”
023|027|We revealed to him: “Construct the Ark under Our observation and by Our inspiration. When Our command comes, and the oven overflows, take on board a pair of every kind, and your family, excluding those upon whom the sentence has been pronounced. And don’t plead with Me on behalf of those who did wrong; they are to be drowned.”
023|028|When you and those with you are settled in the Ark, say, “Praise be to Allah who has delivered us from the wrong-doing people.”
023|029|And pray, “My Lord, make me land with a blessed landing, for You are the best to ensure a safe landing.”
023|030|In this, there are lessons, and We are constantly testing.
023|031|Then, after them, We established another generation.
023|032|We sent a messenger from among them, proclaiming, “Worship Allah; you have no deity other than Him. Won’t you protect yourselves?”
023|033|The leaders of his people who disbelieved and denied the meeting in the Hereafter, and We had given them affluence in the worldly life, countered, “This is merely a man like you, who eats what you eat and drinks what you drink.
023|034|If you obey a man like yourselves, you will surely be at a loss.
023|035|Does he promise you that, when you die and become dust and bones, you will be resurrected?
023|036|Far-fetched, far-fetched is what you’re promised.
023|037|Our life is only this present existence; we live, die, and won’t be resurrected.
023|038|He is just a man inventing lies about Allah, and we’re not going to believe in him.”
023|039|He pleaded, “My Lord, assist me, because they have denied me.”
023|040|He replied, “In a little while, they will be regretful.”
023|041|The blast justly overtook them, reducing them to ruins. Thus, the wrongdoers were no more.
023|042|Then, after them, We raised up other generations.
023|043|No nation can advance its term, nor delay it.
023|044|We sent Our messengers in succession. Whenever a messenger came to his people, they denied him, branding him a liar. So, We made them follow each other, turning them into tales of the past. So, away with those who refuse to believe!
023|045|Then, We sent Moses and his brother Aaron with Our signs and a clear authority.
023|046|To Pharaoh and his aristocracy, they reacted with arrogance and superiority.
023|047|They said, “Are we to believe in two men like us, while their people serve us as slaves?”
023|048|Thus, they rejected them both and were consequently doomed to destruction.
023|049|We gave Moses the Scripture, so they may be guided.
023|050|And We made the son of Mary and his mother a sign, and We sheltered them on a plateau with security and flowing springs.
023|051|O Messengers, eat from the pure and good foods, and do good deeds. I am fully aware of everything you do.
023|052|This community of yours is one community, and I am your Lord, so fear Me.
023|053|Yet they fragmented into denominations, each rejoicing in its doctrines.
023|054|So leave them in their bewilderment until a time.
023|055|Do they assume that by granting them wealth and children.
023|056|We are racing to give them good things? They don’t perceive.
023|057|And those who, due to the fear of their Lord, are apprehensive.
023|058|And those who believe in the signs of their Lord.
023|059|And those who don’t associate anything with their Lord.
023|060|And those who give what they give with hearts trembling, because they will return to their Lord.
023|061|These are the ones who compete in goodness and are foremost in doing so.
023|062|We don’t burden a soul beyond its capacity. With Us is a record that speaks with truth, and they won’t be wronged.
023|063|But rather, their hearts are in confusion over this, and they engage in deeds that contradict it.
023|064|Until, when We seize their elite with torment, they begin to groan.
023|065|Don’t groan today; you will receive no assistance from Us.
023|066|My verses were conveyed to you, yet you backed away from them.
023|067|You reacted arrogantly towards them, debated against them baselessly, and outright rejected them.
023|068|Don’t they ponder over the Word? Or did news come to them that didn’t come to their ancestors?
023|069|Or did they fail to recognize their Messenger, and thus, they deny him?
023|070|Or do they say, “He is possessed”? In fact, he brought them the truth, and most of them hate the truth.
023|071|If the truth were to follow their desires, the heavens, the earth, and everything within them would surely be in chaos. We gave them their reminder, yet they disregard their reminder.
023|072|Are you demanding a fee from them? The reward from your Lord is far better, for He is the best of providers.
023|073|You are inviting them to a straight path.
023|074|Yet, those who don’t believe in the Hereafter veer away from the path.
023|075|Even if We were to show them mercy and alleviate their troubles, they would stubbornly persist in their transgression, wandering blindly.
023|076|We had afflicted them, yet they didn’t turn to their Lord or humble themselves.
023|077|Until, when We opened upon them a gate of intense pain, they were left in utter despair.
023|078|It is He who endowed you with hearing, sight, and hearts, yet you rarely give thanks.
023|079|It is He who scattered you throughout the earth, and to Him, you will be gathered.
023|080|It is He who gives life and causes death, and His is the alternation of night and day. Don’t you comprehend?
023|081|They merely repeat what was said by those before them.
023|082|They question, “After we have died and become dust and bones, will we be resurrected?
023|083|We and our forefathers were promised this before—these are nothing but legends of the ancients.”
023|084|Ask them, “To whom does the earth and everything on it belong, if you truly know?”
023|085|They will respond, “To Allah.” Say, “Then why don’t you reflect?”
023|086|Ask them, “Who is the Lord of the seven heavens and the Lord of the Majestic Throne?”
023|087|They will answer, “Allah.” Say, “Won’t you be righteous?”
023|088|Say, “In whose hands is sovereignty over everything, and He provides protection but requires none, if you truly possess knowledge?”
023|089|They will say, “Allah.” Say, “Then how are you bewitched?”
023|090|We brought them the truth, yet they persist in denial.
023|091|Allah has never begotten a child, nor is there any god besides Him. If there were, each god would have claimed what it created, and some would’ve sought supremacy over others. Glory be to Allah, far beyond what they describe.
023|092|He is the Knower of the unseen and the seen, far above having a partner.
023|093|Say, “My Lord! If You should show me what they’ve been promised.
023|094|My Lord, place me not among the wrongdoers.”
023|095|We can show you what We’ve promised them.
023|096|Repel evil with what’s better. We know best what they describe.
023|097|And say, “My Lord, I seek refuge in You from the whispers of the devils.
023|098|And I seek Your protection, my Lord, lest they become present.”
023|099|Until, when death comes to one of them, he pleads, “My Lord, let me return.
023|100|So that I may rectify what I left undone.” By no means! It is merely a word he says; a barrier stands behind them until the Day they are resurrected.
023|101|When the Trumpet is blown, on that Day, all familial ties among them will be severed, and they won’t have the means to inquire after one another.
023|102|Those whose scales are heavy will be the successful ones.
023|103|However, those with light scales will have lost their souls, remaining in Hell forever.
023|104|The Flames will scorch their faces, disfiguring them beyond recognition.
023|105|“Were My verses not conveyed to you, yet you denied them?”
023|106|They will respond, “Our Lord, our wretchedness overcame us, and we were led astray.
023|107|Our Lord, remove us from this. If we were to revert, we would indeed be wrongdoers.”
023|108|He will say, “Remain despised therein, and don’t speak to Me.
023|109|A group of My servants used to say, ‘Our Lord, we have believed, so forgive us, and have mercy on us, You are the Best of the Merciful.’
023|110|But you made fun of them, to the extent that it made you forget My remembrance, and you used to laugh at them.
023|111|“Today, I have rewarded them for their patience; truly, they are the ones who have triumphed.”
023|112|He will ask, “How long did you stay on Earth in terms of years?”
023|113|They will answer, “We stayed a day or part of a day; ask those who count.”
023|114|He will say, “In fact, you stayed only a little—if only you had known.
023|115|Did you think that We created you without purpose, and that you wouldn’t be returned to Us?”
023|116|So exalted is Allah, the True King. There is no deity except Him, the Lord of the Noble Throne.
023|117|Whoever invokes, beside Allah, another god for which he has no proof, then his account rests with his Lord. The unbelievers won’t succeed.
023|118|Say, “My Lord, forgive and have mercy, for You are the Best of the merciful.”
024|001|A chapter that We revealed and made obligatory, containing clear verses, so that you may remember.
024|002|Regarding the adulteress and the adulterer, administer one hundred lashes to each. Let not pity for them prevent you from implementing Allah’s Law—if you believe in Allah and the Last Day. Let a group of believers witness their punishment.
024|003|An adulterer may only marry an adulteress or a polytheistic woman, and an adulteress may only marry an adulterer or a polytheistic man. This is prohibited for the believers.
024|004|Those who falsely accuse chaste women, yet fail to produce four witnesses, whip them with eighty lashes, and reject their testimony after that. These are the sinful ones.
024|005|However, those who repent and reform afterwards—Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.
024|006|If a man accuses his wife, but has no witnesses except himself, he must swear by Allah four times that he is truthful.
024|007|On the fifth instance, he must invoke Allah’s curse upon himself if he’s lying.
024|008|Her punishment will be averted if she swears four times by Allah that he’s lying.
024|009|On the fifth occasion, she must invoke Allah’s wrath upon herself, if he is truthful.
024|010|But for Allah’s grace and mercy upon you, and that Allah is Accepting of Repentance, Wise.
024|011|Those who initiated the slander are a group among you. Don’t consider it harmful for you; it is beneficial for you. Each person involved will bear a portion of the sin, but the one who played the major role will face harsh punishment.
024|012|When you heard it, the believing men and women should’ve thought positively of one another and said, “This is obviously a lie.”
024|013|Why didn’t they produce four witnesses for it? If they don’t produce the witnesses, then in the sight of Allah, they are the liars.
024|014|Were it not for Allah’s grace and mercy upon you, in this world and the Hereafter, a tremendous punishment would’ve befallen you for what you engaged in.
024|015|You propagated it with your tongues and spoke with your mouths what you had no knowledge of, considering it trivial, while it was, in the sight of Allah, significant.
024|016|Upon hearing it, you should’ve said, “It is not for us to speak of this. Glory be to You, this is a serious slander.”
024|017|Allah admonishes you never to return to such a thing, if you are believers.
024|018|Allah clarifies the verses for you. Allah is All-Knowing, All-Wise.
024|019|Those who love to see immorality among the believers will face severe punishment in this life and the Hereafter. Allah knows, and you don’t know.
024|020|Allah extends His grace and mercy upon you. Allah is Kind and Merciful.
024|021|O you who believe, don’t follow Satan’s footsteps. Whoever follows Satan’s footsteps—he orders immorality and what’s objectionable. If not for Allah’s grace and mercy upon you, none of you would ever be purified. But Allah purifies whom He wills. Allah is All-Hearing, All-Knowing.
024|022|And let those of abundance and ample means among you not swear to withhold their help from their relatives, the needy, and the emigrants in the cause of Allah. Let them forgive and overlook. Don’t you wish for Allah to forgive you? Allah is All-Forgiving, Most Merciful.
024|023|Those who falsely accuse innocent, unsuspecting, believing women are cursed in this world and in the Hereafter, and for them is a terrible punishment.
024|024|On the Day when their own tongues, hands, and feet will testify against them as to what they used to do.
024|025|On that Day, Allah will settle their accounts in full, and they will know that Allah is the Evident Truth.
024|026|Wicked women are for wicked men, and evil men are for evil women. And good women are for good men, and virtuous men are for virtuous women. These are clear of what people say. For them, there is forgiveness and a generous provision.
024|027|O you who believe, don’t enter homes other than your own until you have sought permission and greeted its inhabitants. This is better for you, that you may be mindful.
024|028|If you find no one therein, don’t enter until your permission has been granted. If you’re asked to leave, then turn back. Allah is fully aware of what you do.
024|029|There is no fault in you for entering houses not inhabited, where there is convenience for you. Allah knows what you disclose and what you conceal.
024|030|Tell the believing men to lower their gaze and guard their privates. That is purer for them, and Allah fully knows what they do.
024|031|And tell the believing women to lower their gaze, to guard their chastity, and not to display their beauty beyond what appears thereof. They should draw their veils over their chests and not display their beauty except to their husbands, fathers, fathers-in-law, sons, stepsons, brothers, the sons of their sisters, female relatives, their dependents, male servants devoid of sexual desires, and children who are unaware of women’s nakedness. They shouldn’t stamp their feet to draw attention to their hidden beauty. O believers, turn to Allah in repentance, so you may succeed.
024|032|Marry off the singles among you, and the righteous among your male and female servants. If they are poor, Allah will enrich them from His bounty. Allah is Bountiful, All-Knowing.
024|033|Let those who don’t find marriage abstain, until Allah enriches them from His grace. If any of your servants desire literacy, provide it, if you recognize any good in them. Give them from the wealth that Allah has given you. Don’t compel your maids into prostitution for worldly gains if they wish to remain virtuous. However, if anyone compels them, then after their compulsion, Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.
024|034|We’ve sent down to you clear signs, narratives of those who preceded you, and an admonition for the righteous.
024|035|Allah is the Light of the heavens and the earth. His light is like a niche in which there is a lamp. The lamp is encased in a crystal, glowing like a brilliant star, fueled by a blessed olive tree, neither of the East nor the West. Its oil would almost glow, even without fire touching it—light upon light. Allah guides to His Light whom He wills. Allah presents parables for humankind.
024|036|In houses that Allah authorized to be raised His name is mentioned, and His praises are proclaimed, morning and evening.
024|037|Men, whom neither trade nor sale distracts from the remembrance of Allah, from performing prayers and giving charity. They fear a day when hearts and eyes will be overturned.
024|038|Allah will reward them for their best deeds and give them more from His grace. Allah provides without account for whom He wills.
024|039|But as for those who disbelieve, their deeds are like a mirage in a desert. The thirsty thinks it to be water, until, upon reaching it, finds nothing. Instead, he finds Allah there, to settle his account in full. Allah is swift in reckoning.
024|040|Or like darkness within a vast, deep sea, covered by wave upon wave, topped by clouds—layers upon layers of darkness. If one extends his hand, he can barely see it. For those whom Allah doesn’t grant light, there is no illumination.
024|041|Don’t you see that everything in the heavens and on earth glorifies Allah, including the birds, as they soar? Each knows its mode of prayer and praise. Allah is fully aware of what they do.
024|042|The sovereignty of the heavens and the earth belongs to Allah, and to Allah is the final return.
024|043|Didn’t you see how Allah drives the clouds, gathers them, then stacks them up? From within their midst, you see raindrops emerge. He sends down abundant hail from the sky, striking with it whom He wills and averting it from whom He wills. The flash of its lightning almost snatches away the sight.
024|044|Allah alternates the night and the day. In this, there is a lesson for those who have insight.
024|045|Allah created every living creature from water—some crawl on their bellies, some walk on two legs, and others on four. Allah creates whatever He wills, for He is capable of all things.
024|046|We revealed enlightening revelations, and Allah guides whom He wills to a straight path.
024|047|They say, “We believe in Allah and the Messenger, and we obey.” But after that, some of them turn away; these are not believers.
024|048|When they are called to Allah and His Messenger to judge among them, some of them hesitate.
024|049|However, if the judgment is in their favor, they come to it willingly.
024|050|Is there illness in their hearts? Or are they plagued with doubt? Or do they fear that Allah and His Messenger will mistreat them? In reality, it is they who are the wrongdoers.
024|051|When called upon by Allah and His Messenger to settle their disputes, the believers respond, saying, “We heard, and we obeyed.” These are the ones who will prosper.
024|052|Those who obey Allah and His Messenger, who fear Allah and are mindful of Him, are the successful ones.
024|053|They swear solemnly by Allah that they would mobilize if you were to command them. Say, “Don’t swear; true obedience will be recognized. Allah is fully aware of what you do.”
024|054|Say, “Obey Allah and obey the Messenger.” But if they turn away, he is accountable for his duty, and you are accountable for yours. If you obey, you will be guided. It is only incumbent upon the Messenger to deliver the clear message.
024|055|Allah promises those among you who believe and do good deeds that He will grant them sovereignty on earth, as He did to those before them. And He will establish for them their religion, which He has preferred for them, and replace their fear with security. They will worship Me alone, not associating anything with Me. However, those who disbelieve after this—these are the sinful.
024|056|Establish prayer, give charity, and obey the Messenger, so that you may receive mercy.
024|057|Don’t think that those who disbelieve can escape on earth. Their final abode is the Fire—a terrible destination.
024|058|O you who believe, let your dependents and those who haven’t reached puberty ask for permission in three instances: before the dawn prayer, when you undress at noon, and after the evening prayer. These are three occasions of privacy for you. At other times, it’s not improper for you or them to move about freely, mingling with each other. Thus, Allah clarifies His verses for you. Allah is All-Knowing, Most Wise.
024|059|When your children reach puberty, they must also ask for permission, as those before them did. Thus, Allah makes His commandments clear to you. Allah is All-Knowing, Most Wise.
024|060|Elderly women who are past the prospect of marriage can relax their dress code, provided they don’t flaunt their beauty. However, it’s better for them to maintain modesty. Allah is All-Hearing, All-Knowing.
024|061|There is no blame on the blind, the disabled, the sick, nor upon yourselves if you eat in your own houses, or the houses of your fathers, mothers, brothers, sisters, paternal uncles and aunts, maternal uncles and aunts, or in houses whose keys you possess, or in your friends’ houses. There is no blame upon you whether you eat together or separately. When you enter houses, greet each other with a greeting blessed and pure from Allah. Thus, Allah clarifies His revelations to you, so you may understand.
024|062|True believers are those who have faith in Allah and His Messenger, and when they are with him on a matter of common interest, they don’t leave without seeking his permission. Those who ask your permission are the ones who believe in Allah and His Messenger. If they request your permission for some of their affairs, grant permission to whomever you wish among them, and ask Allah for forgiveness for them. Allah is Ever Forgiving, Most Merciful.
024|063|Don’t address the Messenger as you address each other. Allah surely knows those of you who slip away hiding themselves. Let those who defy His commands beware, lest a trial befall them or a grievous penalty be inflicted on them.
024|064|Surely, to Allah belongs whatever is in the heavens and the earth. He knows what you’re upon. On the Day they are returned to Him, He will make them aware of what they did. And Allah is fully aware of everything.
025|001|Blessed is He who revealed the Criterion upon His servant, serving as a Warner to the worlds.
025|002|He to whom belongs the sovereignty of the heavens and the earth, who has not begotten a son, who has no partner in His dominion, and who created everything and ordained its destiny.
025|003|Yet, they choose gods other than Him that create nothing but are themselves created, possess no power to harm or benefit themselves, and cannot control death, life, or resurrection.
025|004|The unbelievers say, “This is nothing but a lie he lied, and others have helped him with it.” They committed an injustice and a falsehood.
025|005|They also say, “Legends of the ancients, which he wrote down, and they are being dictated to him morning and evening.”
025|006|Respond, “It was revealed by He who knows the secrets of the heavens and the earth. Indeed, He is Forgiving, Merciful.”
025|007|They ask, “What sort of messenger is this, who eats food and walks in the markets? Why wasn’t an angel sent down to be a co-warner with him?”
025|008|Or they ask, “Why wasn’t a treasure dropped on him?” Or, “Why doesn’t he have a garden from which he eats?” The wrongdoers also say, “You are only following a man who is bewitched.”
025|009|See how they make comparisons for you; they are astray and can’t find a way.
025|010|Blessed is He, who, if He wills, can give you better than that: Gardens through which rivers flow, and He will give you palaces.
025|011|They deny the Hour, and for those who deny the Hour, We prepared a scorching fire.
025|012|When it sees them from a distant place, they will hear its fury and roaring.
025|013|When they are thrown into a narrow place, bound in chains, they will plead for annihilation there and then.
025|014|“Don’t plead for a single annihilation today, but plead for many annihilations.”
025|015|Say, “Is that better, or the Eternal Garden, which is promised to the righteous?” It will be their reward and final destination.
025|016|There, they will have all they desire, forever. This is a promise binding upon your Lord.
025|017|On the Day He gathers them and whatever they worshiped besides Allah, He will ask, “Was it you who misled these servants of Mine, or did they stray from the path themselves?”
025|018|They will respond, “Glory be to You! It wasn’t for us to take any allies besides You. You gave them and their ancestors pleasures, until they forgot the Remembrance and became a ruined people.”
025|019|Thus, they will deny you because of what you say, and you won’t be able to avert or help. Whoever among you commits wrongdoing, We will make him taste a severe punishment.
025|020|We never sent messengers before you who didn’t eat food and walk in the markets. We test you through each other—will you have patience? Your Lord is ever Watchful.
025|021|Those who don’t anticipate Our meeting say, “If only the angels were sent down to us, or we could see our Lord.” They’ve grown inwardly arrogant, and have come with great arrogance.
025|022|On the Day they see the angels, there will be no joy for the transgressors, and they will exclaim, “This is an insurmountable barrier!”
025|023|We will then turn to the deeds they’ve committed and reduce them to scattered dust.
025|024|On that Day, the inhabitants of Paradise will have the best residence, and the finest place of rest.
025|025|On the Day when the sky and its clouds are ripped apart, the angels descend in continuous streams.
025|026|On that Day, sovereignty will belong to the Most Merciful. It will be a difficult Day for the disbelievers.
025|027|On that Day, the wrongdoer will bite on his hands in despair, he will say, “I wish I had taken a path with the Messenger.
025|028|Alas, for me! I wish I had never taken so-and-so as a friend.
025|029|He led me away from the Reminder after it had reached me. Satan has always been a betrayer of man.”
025|030|The Messenger will say, “O my Lord, my people have treated this Quran as something to be disregarded.”
025|031|For every prophet, We assigned adversaries from among the guilty. Yet, your Lord is sufficient as a Guide and Helper.
025|032|The disbelievers question, “Why wasn’t the Quran revealed to him all at once?” It was thus, to strengthen your heart, that We revealed it in stages.
025|033|They can’t bring you any argument, but We bring you the truth and the best explanation.
025|034|Those who are dragged face down to Hell, are in the worst position, and are most astray from the path.
025|035|We gave Moses the Scripture and appointed his brother Aaron as his assistant.
025|036|We instructed, “Go to the people who denied Our signs.” Then, We destroyed them utterly.
025|037|And the people of Noah—when they rejected the messengers, We drowned them, and made them a sign for all people. For the wrongdoers, We prepared a severe punishment.
025|038|And Aad, Thamud, the inhabitants of Rass, and many generations in between.
025|039|We presented each of them with parables, and then We obliterated them completely.
025|040|They passed by the town that was drenched by the terrible downpour. Didn’t they see it? Yet, they don’t expect resurrection.
025|041|When they see you, they mock, “Is this the one whom Allah has sent as a messenger?”
025|042|“He almost led us away from our gods, had we not firmly adhered to them.” They will realize, when they witness the punishment, who strayed further.
025|043|Have you considered the one who makes his own desire his god? Can you be responsible for him?
025|044|Do you think that most of them hear or understand? They are like cattle; in fact, they are even further astray from the path.
025|045|Didn’t you see how your Lord causes the shadow to extend? Had He willed, He could’ve made it still. And We made the sun its indicator.
025|046|Then We retract it towards Us in gradual stages.
025|047|It is He who made the night a covering for you, sleep for rest, and the day a revival.
025|048|It is He who sends the winds as heralds ahead of His mercy, and We send down from the sky pure water.
025|049|To revive dead lands thereby and to provide drink for the multitude of creatures and humans We created.
025|050|We distribute it among them for reflection, yet most people persist in ingratitude and disbelief.
025|051|Had We willed, We could’ve sent a warner to every community.
025|052|So don’t obey the unbelievers, but strive against them vigorously.
025|053|He is the one who has released two bodies of water, one sweet and fresh, the other salty and bitter. He set a barrier and a prohibitive partition between them.
025|054|It is He who created man from water, then made him relation by lineage and marriage. Your Lord is always Capable.
025|055|Yet, they worship entities other than Allah, which can neither benefit nor harm them. The disbeliever is in open defiance of his Lord.
