027|087|On the Day when the Trumpet will be blown, and everyone in the heavens and everyone on earth will be terrified, except those whom Allah wills. Everyone will come humbly submissive before Him.
027|088|You see the mountains, and you think they are fixed, but they pass, as the passing of the clouds. The making of Allah, who perfected everything; He is fully aware of everything you do.
027|089|Whoever brings a good deed, he will have better than it, and they will be secure from terror on that day.
027|090|But those who commit evil deeds, their faces will be thrown into the Fire. Are you recompensed except for what you used to do?
027|091|“I have been commanded only to worship the Lord of this town, Who has declared it sacred, and to Whom all things belong. And I am commanded to be of those who submit.
027|092|And to convey the Quran.” Whoever is guided, is only guided for his soul. As for those who go astray, then say, “I am only a warner.”
027|093|And say, “Praise be to Allah, He will show you His signs, and you will recognize them. Your Lord is not unaware of what you do.”
028|001|Ta. Seen. Meem.
028|002|These are the verses of the Enlightening Book.
028|003|We narrate to you the story of Moses and Pharaoh, with truth, for a people who believe.
028|004|Pharaoh exalted himself in the land, dividing its people into sects. He oppressed a group among them, slaughtering their sons while sparing their women. He was among the corruptors.
028|005|Yet, We intended to show favor upon those oppressed in the land, and make them leaders, and make them the inheritors.
028|006|And to establish them in the land. And to show Pharaoh, Haman, and their troops from them what they were fearing.
028|007|We inspired Moses’ mother: “Suckle him, and if you fear for him, cast him into the river, and don’t fear nor grieve. We will return him to you and make him one of the messengers.”
028|008|Pharaoh’s family picked him up, unaware he would become their adversary and bring them sorrow. Pharaoh, Haman, and their troops were sinful.
028|009|Pharaoh’s wife said, “He is a delight to my eyes and yours. Don’t kill him; perhaps he may benefit us, or we may adopt him as a son.” However, they didn’t foresee.
028|010|The heart of Moses’ mother was filled with anxiety—she almost disclosed his identity, if We had not strengthened her heart, so that she could be among the believers.
028|011|And she said to his sister, “Follow him.” So she watched him from a distance while they perceived not.
028|012|And We had forbidden foster-mothers for him. She said, “Shall I point out to you a household that could look after him for you?”
028|013|And so, We returned him to his mother, to bring her joy, alleviate her sorrow, and reassure her that Allah’s promise is true. Yet, most of them don’t understand.
028|014|When he reached his full strength and was mature, We endowed him with wisdom and knowledge. This is how We reward the righteous.
028|015|One day, he entered the city unnoticed by its inhabitants. There, he found two men fighting—one from his sect and the other from his enemies. The man from his sect sought his help against the adversary, and Moses struck him, ending his life. He said, “This is the work of Satan; he is a clear enemy, leading astray.”
028|016|He prayed, “My Lord, I have wronged myself. Please forgive me.” And He forgave him. He is the Forgiving, the Merciful.
028|017|He pledged, “My Lord, by the favors You’ve bestowed upon me, I will never be a helper to the criminals.”
028|018|Afterward, he was vigilant in the city. The man who had sought his help the previous day was again crying out for his assistance. Moses said to him, ”You are clearly a troublemaker.”
028|019|And when he intended to strike the one from their enemy faction, he said, “O Moses, do you intend to kill me, as you killed a man yesterday? You only aim to become a tyrant in the land and not a peacemaker.”
028|020|A man came rushing from the city’s farthest part, exclaiming, “O Moses, the authorities are consulting to kill you. Leave immediately; I am advising you in good faith.”
028|021|So he departed from there, fearful and vigilant, saying, “My Lord, save me from the wrongdoing people.”
028|022|When he was heading towards Midian, he said, “Hopefully, my Lord will guide me to the right path.”
028|023|Upon reaching the water of Midian, he found a crowd of people watering. And he found, apart from them, two women keeping back. He asked, “What troubles you?” They replied, “We can’t water until the shepherds have finished, and our father is an elderly man.”
028|024|Then, he watered for them, then withdrew to the shade and said, “My Lord, I am in desperate need of whatever good You might send down to me.”
028|025|Later, one of the two women approached him, walking modestly. She said, “My father invites you so he may reward you for drawing water for us.” When he arrived and told him the story, he said, “Don’t fear. You’ve escaped from the unjust people.”
028|026|One of the women said, “My father, hire him! The best one to hire is the strong and trustworthy.”
028|027|He said, “I intend to wed you to one of my daughters, provided you serve me for eight years. If you complete ten, it is up to you. And I don’t intend to impose any hardship on you, and Allah willing, you’ll find me righteous.”
028|028|He responded, “That’s an agreement between us. Whichever of the two terms I fulfill, let there be no injustice towards me, and Allah is the guardian over what we say.”
028|029|After Moses had completed the term and was journeying with his family, he noticed a fire in the direction of the Mount. He told his family, “Stay here; I have noticed a fire. Perhaps I can bring back some news from it, or a burning ember to warm you.”
028|030|As he approached, he was called out from the right side of the valley, from the Blessed Spot, from within the tree, “O Moses, it is I, Allah, Lord of the worlds.”
028|031|“Drop your staff.” And when he saw it writhing, as if it were a serpent, he turned to flee and didn’t look back. “O Moses, approach and fear not—you are safe.
028|032|Insert your hand into your robe; it will come out white, without any blemish. And draw your arm toward yourself to ward off fear. These are two proofs from your Lord for Pharaoh and his chiefs; they are sinful people.”
028|033|He said, “My Lord, I have killed a man among them, so I fear that they will kill me.
028|034|And my brother Aaron; he is more fluent in speech than me. So send him with me as a helper to affirm my truth; I fear they will reject me.
028|035|He replied, “We will strengthen you with your brother, and We will grant both of you authority, so they can’t harm you. With Our signs, you and those who follow you will be victorious.”
028|036|But when Moses came to them with Our clear signs, they said, “This is nothing but fabricated magic; we’ve never heard of such from our forefathers.”
028|037|Moses responded, “My Lord knows best who brought guidance from Him, and to whom the ultimate home will belong. The wrongdoers won’t succeed.”
028|038|Pharaoh declared, “O my chiefs, I know of no other god for you than myself. Therefore, O Haman, fire up the clay for me, and build me a tower, that I may climb up to the God of Moses; though I am convinced he is lying.”
028|039|He and his troops behaved arrogantly in the land, without right, and they thought that they wouldn’t be returned to Us.
028|040|So, We seized him and his troops, throwing them into the sea. Observe the end of the wrongdoers!
028|041|And We appointed them leaders who call to the Fire, and on Resurrection Day, they won’t be helped.
028|042|And We followed them in this world with a curse, and they will be among the despised on Resurrection Day.
028|043|And We gave Moses the Scripture, after We had destroyed the former generations, as a beacon of light for humanity, offering guidance and mercy, so they might reflect.
028|044|You weren’t on the western side when We decreed the commandment to Moses, nor were you among the witnesses.
028|045|Yet, We raised numerous generations and extended their lifespans. You were not among the people of Midian, delivering Our verses to them. But, We have always sent messengers.
028|046|You weren’t at the base of the Mount when We called out. However, it’s an act of mercy from your Lord, to warn a people to whom no warner had come before, so they may become aware.
028|047|Thus, if a calamity befalls them due to their actions, they can’t say, “Our Lord, if only You had sent us a messenger, we would’ve followed Your guidance and been among the believers.”
028|048|Now, when the truth has come to them from Us, they argue, “Why wasn’t he given something similar to what Moses received?” Didn’t they reject what was previously given to Moses? And they say, “These two are mixed-up magic spells, and we reject both.”
028|049|Say, “Then produce a scripture from Allah that offers superior guidance than these two, and I will follow it, if you are truthful.”
028|050|If they fail to respond to you, know that they are merely following their desires. And who is more astray than one who follows his desires without guidance from Allah? Allah does not guide the wrongdoers.
028|051|We’ve conveyed the Word to them, so they may remember.
028|052|Those to whom We’ve given the Scripture before this, are believers in it.
028|053|When it’s conveyed to them, they assert, “We believe in it; it’s the truth from our Lord. Even before its revelation, we were already Submitters.”
028|054|These will be given their reward twice over, because they persevered. They fend off evil with good, and they spend out of what We’ve provided for them.
028|055|When they hear idle talk, they turn away from it, saying, “To us our deeds, and to you your deeds. Peace be upon you; we don’t engage with the ignorant.”
028|056|You can’t guide whom you love, but Allah guides whom He wills. He knows best those who are guided.
028|057|They argue, “If we follow the guidance with you, we will be displaced from our land.” Didn’t We establish for them a secure sanctuary, to which all kinds of fruits are brought, as sustenance from Us? Yet, most of them don’t understand.
028|058|How many a city did We destroy while they were arrogant in their luxury? These are their dwellings, uninhabited after them except a little; We are the Inheritor.
028|059|Your Lord never destroyed the towns until He has raised a messenger within them to relay to them Our revelations. We would never destroy a community unless its people were wrongdoers.
028|060|What you’ve been given is merely for the enjoyment and decoration of this worldly life. What Allah possesses, however, is superior and more lasting. Don’t you understand?
028|061|Is the one to whom We’ve promised a good promise—which he will attain—comparable to the one to whom We granted worldly pleasures, but who, on Resurrection Day, will be among the arraigned?
028|062|On that Day, He will call out to them, “Where are those ‘partners’ of Mine you claimed?”
028|063|Those against whom the word will come into effect, will say, “Our Lord, these are the ones we misled. We misled them as we ourselves were misled. We disassociate ourselves from them before You. It was not us whom they worshiped.”
028|064|Then it will be said, “Call upon your associates.” They will call upon them, but they won’t answer them. They will witness the suffering and wish they had followed guidance.
028|065|On that Day, He will question them, “What was your reply to the messengers?”
028|066|On that day, they will be blind to the news, and they won’t ask one another.
028|067|However, those who repent, believe, and perform righteous deeds may indeed be among the successful.
028|068|Your Lord creates what He wills, and He chooses. The choice isn’t theirs. Glory be to Allah, and High above what they associate with Him.
028|069|Your Lord knows what their hearts conceal and what they disclose.
028|070|He is Allah; there is no god except He. All praise is His in this life and the Hereafter. His is the judgment, and to Him you will be returned.
028|071|Say, “Have you considered: if Allah were to make the night continuous over you until Resurrection Day, which god, other than Allah, could bring you illumination? Don’t you listen?”
028|072|Say, “Have you considered: if Allah were to make the day continuous over you until Resurrection Day, which god, other than Allah, could bring you night for rest? Don’t you see?”
028|073|Out of His mercy, He made for you the night and the day, so you may rest therein, seek His bounty, and perhaps express gratitude.
028|074|On the Day He will summon them, He will question, “Where are those you alleged were My ‘partners’?”
028|075|We will extract from every nation a witness and say, “Present your evidence.” Then they will realize that the truth is Allah’s alone, and the lies they fabricated will abandon them.
028|076|Korah was of Moses’ people, but he oppressed them. We had given him such treasures, that their keys would burden a group of strong men. When his people said to him, “Don’t exult; Allah does not love the exultant.
028|077|Seek the Hereafter with what Allah has given you, and don’t neglect your share of this world. Do good, as Allah has done good to you, and refrain from causing corruption in the land. Allah doesn’t favor the corrupt.”
028|078|He replied, “I acquired all this through my knowledge.” Didn’t he know that Allah had destroyed before him generations that were mightier and wealthier than he was? But the sinful won’t be asked about their sins.
028|079|And he paraded before his people in his splendor. Those who seek this worldly life said, “If only we had the like of what Korah was given. Indeed, he is one of great fortune.”
028|080|But those who had been given knowledge said, “Woe to you! The reward from Allah is better for those who believe and act righteously, but only the patient will receive it.”
028|081|So, We made the earth swallow him and his mansion. There was no group to help him against Allah, nor could he defend himself.
028|082|Those who wished they were in his place the day before began to say, “Oh, how Allah extends provision to whom He wills of His servants and restricts it. Had Allah not been gracious to us, He would’ve caused the earth to swallow us. Oh, how the unbelievers don’t succeed.”
028|083|That Home of the Hereafter, We assign it to those who don’t seek superiority on earth, nor corruption. And the outcome is for the righteous.
028|084|Whoever comes with good will have what’s better. But whoever comes with evil—the evildoers will be recompensed only for what they’ve done.
028|085|He who ordained the Quran upon you, will bring you back to the place of return. Say, “My Lord knows best who comes with guidance and who is in manifest error.”
028|086|You didn’t expect the Scripture to be transmitted to you, but it is a mercy from your Lord. So, don’t be a supporter of unbelievers.
028|087|And let them not turn you away from Allah’s verses after they’ve been revealed to you. And invite to your Lord, and never be one of the idolaters.
028|088|And call not, besides Allah, unto any other god. There is no deity except Him. Everything will perish, except His presence. To Him is judgment, and to Him, you will be returned.
029|001|Alif. Lam. Meem.
029|002|Do people think they will be left alone, just stating, “We believe,” without being tested?
029|003|We tested those before them. And Allah will certainly know those who are true from those who are false.
029|004|Do those who commit evil think they can outmaneuver Us? How delusional they are!
029|005|Whoever hopes to meet Allah, the appointed time of Allah is surely coming. He is the All-Hearing, the All-Knowing.
029|006|Whoever strives, strives for his own soul. Allah is free of all needs from all creation.
029|007|As for those who believe and lead righteous lives, We will erase their sins and reward them according to the best of their actions.
029|008|We’ve instructed man to honor his parents. However, if they pressure you to associate something with Me, about which you have no knowledge, don’t obey them. To Me is your return, and I will inform you of everything you did.
029|009|Those who believe and do righteous deeds will be among the righteous.
029|010|Some people profess, “We believe in Allah.” But when they suffer for Allah’s sake, they equate human persecution with Allah’s punishment. Yet, when help comes to them from your Lord, they say, “We were always with you.” Doesn’t Allah know what resides in the hearts of all beings?
029|011|Allah will certainly ascertain those who believe, and He will surely expose the hypocrites.
029|012|Those who disbelieve say to the believers, “Follow our path, and we will carry your sins.” Yet they can’t carry any of their sins. They are liars.
029|013|They will carry their own burdens, and other burdens along with their own. And on Resurrection Day, they will be questioned about their false assertions.
029|014|We sent Noah to his people, and he dwelt among them for a millennium, less fifty years. Then the flood overtook them while they were wrongdoers.
029|015|But We rescued him and those with him in the Ark, and We made it a symbol for all people.
029|016|Consider Abraham, who said to his people, “Worship Allah and revere Him; this is better for you, if only you understood.
029|017|You worship idols besides Allah and invent lies. The idols you worship apart from Allah don’t possess provision for you. Therefore, seek sustenance from Allah, worship Him, and give thanks to Him. To Him, you will be returned.”
029|018|If you deny the truth, nations before you have also denied. The Messenger’s only duty is to deliver the message clearly.
029|019|Didn’t they see how Allah originates creation and then repeats it? This is easy for Allah.
029|020|Say, “Travel through the earth and observe how He initiated creation.” Then, Allah will produce the next existence. Allah has power over everything.
029|021|He punishes whom He wills, and He shows mercy to whom He wills. And to Him, you will be restored.
029|022|You can’t escape from Him on Earth or in the heavens, and you have neither protector nor helper besides Allah.
029|023|Those who reject Allah’s revelations and the meeting with Him have despaired of My mercy and will face severe punishment.
029|024|The only response of his people was that they said, “Kill him or burn him!” Yet, Allah saved him from the Fire. In this are signs for people who believe.
029|025|He said, “Instead of Allah, you’ve taken to worshiping idols; your mutual love will last only in the life of this world; then on the Day of Resurrection, you will deny each other and curse each other; and your refuge shall be the fire, and you will have no helpers.”
029|026|Lot believed in him. He said, “I am migrating to my Lord. He is the Almighty, the Wise.”
029|027|And We gave him Isaac and Jacob, and in his lineage, We established prophethood and the Scripture. We gave him his reward in this life, and in the Hereafter, he will be among the righteous.
029|028|Lot told his people, “You commit such indecency as no other community has ever committed.
029|029|You approach men with desire, cut off roads, and commit indecency in your gatherings.” But his people only responded, “Bring upon us Allah’s punishment, if you are truthful.”
029|030|He prayed, “My Lord, give me victory against these corrupt people.”
029|031|When Our messengers brought the good news to Abraham, they also announced, “We are about to destroy the inhabitants of this town, for they are immersed in sin.”
029|032|He protested, “But Lot resides there!” They replied, “We are well aware of who resides there. We will rescue him and his family, except for his wife, destined to be among those left behind.”
029|033|When Our messengers arrived at Lot’s home, they were mistreated, and he was distressed on their account. They reassured him, saying, “Fear not, nor grieve, We will save you and your family, except for your wife, destined to be among the doomed.”
029|034|“We are going to bring down on the people of this town a punishment from the sky due to their transgressions.”
029|035|We left of it an evident sign, for people endowed with intelligence.
029|036|And to Midian, their brother Shuaib. He implored, “O my people, worship Allah, have hope in the Last Day and don’t create disorder in the land.”
029|037|But they rejected him, and the tremor seized them, leaving them lifeless in their homes.
029|038|And Aad, and Thamud—it became clear to you from their dwellings. Satan made their deeds appear pleasing to them, leading them astray from the path, even though they could see.
029|039|And Korah, Pharaoh, and Haman—Moses came to them with clear signs, but they behaved arrogantly in the land. Yet, they weren’t out of reach.
029|040|We seized each of them for their wrongdoings. Some We swept away in a sandstorm; a blast struck others; some We caused the earth to swallow; and others We drowned. It was not Allah who wronged them, but they wronged themselves.
029|041|The example of those who take allies other than Allah is like that of the spider who builds a house. Yet, the weakest of houses is the house of the spider—if they only knew.
029|042|Allah knows whatever they invoke besides Him. He is the Mighty, the Wise.
029|043|We present such parables to people, but only those with knowledge can comprehend them.
029|044|Allah created the heavens and the earth with truth. In this, there is a sign for believers.
029|045|Communicate what has been revealed to you from the Scripture, and establish prayer. Prayer repels immorality and wrongdoing, and the remembrance of Allah is greater. Allah is fully aware of what you do.
029|046|Debate with the People of the Scripture only in the kindest manner, except with those who do wrong among them. And say, “We believe in what was revealed to us, and in what was revealed to you. Our God and your God is One, and to Him we submit.”
029|047|Thus, We revealed the Scripture to you. Those to whom We gave the Scripture, as well as some of these, believe in it. None renounce our verses except the unbelievers.
029|048|You didn’t recite any scripture before this or write one with your right hand. If you had, the fabricators of falsehood would have doubted.
029|049|Rather, these are clear signs in the hearts of those endowed with knowledge. None reject Our verses except the unjust.
029|050|They question, “Why are no miracles sent down to him from his Lord?” Respond, “The miracles are solely with Allah, and I am simply a plain warner.”
029|051|Isn’t it sufficient for them that We revealed to you the Scripture, which is conveyed to them? In this are mercy and reminders for people who believe.
029|052|Say, “Allah is sufficient as a witness between me and you. He knows everything in the heavens and on earth. Those who believe in falsehood and reject Allah—they are the ones who will be the losers.”
029|053|They urge you to hasten the punishment. If not for a set term, the punishment would’ve already come upon them. Yet, it will come upon them suddenly while they are unaware.
029|054|They urge you to hasten the punishment. Hell will undoubtedly envelop the unbelievers.
029|055|On the Day when the punishment will envelop them from above them and from below their feet, He will say, “Taste what you used to do!”
029|056|O My servants who have believed, My earth is vast, so worship only Me.
029|057|Every soul will taste death. Then, you will be returned to Us.
029|058|Those who believe and lead righteous lives, We will settle them in Paradise, in dwellings beneath which rivers flow, where they will stay forever. What an excellent reward for the workers.
029|059|Those who exercise patience and put their trust in their Lord.
029|060|How many living creatures don’t carry their provisions? Allah provides for them and for you. He is the All-Hearing, the All-Knowing.
029|061|If you were to ask them, “Who created the heavens and the earth? Who governs the sun and the moon?” They would surely answer, “Allah.” How then are they deluded?
029|062|Allah extends the provision for whom He wills of His beings and restricts it. Allah is fully aware of all things.
029|063|If you were to ask them, “Who sends down rain from the sky, thereby reviving the lifeless earth?” They would surely answer, “Allah.” Then say, “Praise be to Allah!” Yet, most of them don’t apply their intellect.
029|064|This worldly life is nothing more than diversion and entertainment. And indeed, the home of the Hereafter—that’s the life, if only they knew.
029|065|When they board a vessel, they call upon Allah, devoting their prayer sincerely to Him. However, once He delivers them safely to land, they attribute partners to Him.
029|066|In doing so, they show ingratitude for what We’ve given them. Let them indulge in it. Soon, they will realize.
029|067|Can’t they see that We’ve established a secure sanctuary, while people are being snatched away all around them? Do they believe in falsehood and deny Allah’s favors?
029|068|Who could be more unjust than the one who invents lies against Allah or denies the truth when it comes to him? Isn’t there a place in Hell reserved for the unbelievers?
029|069|Those who strive for Us, We will guide them along Our way. Allah is with the doers of good.
030|001|Alif. Lam. Meem.
030|002|The Romans have been defeated.
030|003|In the nearest region of the land, and yet, after their defeat, they will be victorious.
030|004|Within a few years—to Allah belongs the command, before and after. And on that day, the believers will rejoice.
030|005|In the victory of Allah. He grants victory to whom He wills. He is the Almighty, the Merciful.
030|006|The promise of Allah—Allah never breaks His promise, but most people don’t know.
030|007|They know the superficial aspects of this worldly life, but they are oblivious to the Hereafter.
030|008|Don’t they reflect within themselves? Allah didn’t create the heavens, the earth, and what’s between them, except with the truth and for a determined term. Yet, many among humankind deny the meeting with their Lord.
030|009|Didn’t they travel through the earth and see how was the end of those before them? They were stronger than them. They tilled the ground and developed it more than they have developed it. Their messengers came to them with clear proofs. Surely, Allah was not to wrong them; they wronged themselves.
030|010|The outcome for those who did evil was the worst, because they denied Allah’s signs and they used to ridicule them.
030|011|Allah begins creation; then He will repeat it; then you will be returned to Him.
030|012|On the Day the Hour sets in, the guilty will be struck with despair.
030|013|None of their associates will intercede for them, and they will reject their partners.
030|014|On the Day when the Hour appears—on that Day, they will be separated.
030|015|As for those who believed and did righteous deeds, they will be made happy in a Garden.
030|016|However, those who disbelieved, denied Our revelations and the meeting of the Hereafter—those will be ushered into punishment.
030|017|So exalted is Allah when you reach the evening and when you reach the morning.
030|018|To Him belongs all praise in the heavens and the earth, and in the late afternoon, and when the day begins to decline.
030|019|He brings the living from the dead, and He brings the dead from the living, and He revives the earth after its death. Likewise, you will be resurrected.
030|020|Among His signs is that He created you from dust—and behold—you are humans spreading.
030|021|And among His signs is that He created for you, of yourselves, mates, so that you may find tranquility in them, and He placed between you love and mercy. In that are signs for those who reflect.
030|022|And among His signs is the creation of the heavens and the earth, and the variations of your languages and your colors. In that are signs for the knowledgeable.
030|023|And among His signs is your sleep, during both night and day, and your pursuit of His bounty. In that are signs for people who would hear.
030|024|And among His signs is that He shows you the lightning, causing fear and aspiration, and He sends rain down from the sky, reviving the earth after its death. In that are lessons for those who understand.
030|025|And among His signs is that heaven and earth stand by His command. Then, when He calls you out from the earth, you will emerge at once.
030|026|Every being in the heavens and on earth belongs to Him; all are obedient to Him.
030|027|He is the One who begins creation, then repeats it, and it is easier for Him. To Him pertains the highest example in the heavens and on earth. He is the Mighty, the Wise.
030|028|He offers you a comparison from your own selves: would you make your servants equal partners in your wealth, you fear them as you fear each other? Thus, We make the revelations clear for those who reflect.
030|029|The wrongdoers follow their desires without knowledge. Who can guide those whom Allah has led astray? They have no helpers.
030|030|Embrace the faith of monotheism—the inclination Allah has instilled in humans. There is no altering of Allah’s creation. This is the upright religion, yet most people are unaware.
030|031|Turn to Him, be conscious of Him, and establish prayer. And don’t be of those who associate others with Him.
030|032|Those who divided their religion and became denominations, each faction rejoicing in what they possess.
030|033|When adversity touches people, they call upon their Lord, turning sincerely to Him. Yet when He gives them a taste of His mercy, some of them ascribe partners to their Lord.
030|034|In this way, they are ungrateful for what We’ve given them. Enjoy the fleeting pleasure; you will find out.
030|035|Did We grant them any authority that justifies their association of partners with Him?
030|036|When We let people taste mercy, they rejoice in it. But when adversity strikes them as a result of their actions, they fall into despair.
030|037|Don’t they realize that Allah expands the provision for whom He wills, and He restricts it? Therein lie signs for a people who believe.
030|038|So give the near kin his due right, and also the needy and the displaced. This is best for those who seek Allah’s favor; these are the ones who will prosper.
030|039|The interest you charge to increase people’s wealth doesn’t grow with Allah. But the charity you give, seeking Allah’s presence, these are the ones that will multiply.
030|040|Allah is the One who created you, provides for you, causes you to die, and then revives you. Can any of your ’partners’ do any of that? Glorified is He, and exalted above what they associate with Him.
030|041|Corruption has appeared on land and sea, because of what people’s hands have done, causing them to experience some of the effects of their deeds, so they may return.
030|042|Say, “Roam the earth, and see the outcome of those who came before. Most of them were polytheists.”
030|043|Dedicate yourself to the authentic, ever-true religion, before a Day comes from Allah that can’t be averted. On that Day, they will be divided.
030|044|The disbelief of the unbelievers only serves to burden them; meanwhile, those who act righteously are preparing for their own selves.
030|045|He rewards those who believe and do good works from His bounty. He doesn’t love the unbelievers.
030|046|Among His signs are the winds, heralds of good news, enabling you to experience His mercy. Ships sail by His command, for you to seek from His bounty, so you may give thanks.
030|047|We sent before you messengers to their own peoples and they came to them with clear proofs. Then, We exacted retribution from those who sinned. It is incumbent upon Us to help the believers.
030|048|Allah is the One who releases the winds, stirring up clouds. He spreads them across the sky as He wills, and He breaks them up. You see raindrops issuing from within them. Then, when He makes it fall upon whom He will of His beings, behold, they rejoice.
030|049|Though before it was sent down upon them—just before that—they were in despair.
030|050|Look at the traces of Allah’s mercy, how He revives the earth after its death. He is the One who will revive the dead, and He has power over all things.
030|051|But if We send a wind, and they see it turning things yellow, they would, after that, persist in their disbelief.
030|052|You can’t make the dead hear, nor can you make the deaf hear the call when they’ve turned their backs and retreated.
030|053|And you can’t guide the blind out of their misguidance. You can make hear only those who believe in Our messages and have submitted.
030|054|Allah is the One who created you weak, then made you strong after weakness, then decreed after strength, weakness and old age. He creates as He wills. He is the All-Knowing, the All-Powerful.
030|055|On the Day when the Hour arrives, the criminals will swear they remained only an hour; thus are they deluded.
030|056|Those given knowledge and faith will say, “According to Allah’s decree, you remained until Resurrection Day. This is the Day of Resurrection, but you were unaware.”
030|057|On that Day, the excuses of those who did wrong won’t benefit them, nor will they be permitted to make amends.
030|058|In this Quran, We present various parables for people. Yet, regardless of what verse you offer them, the unbelievers will say, “You are just making things up.”
030|059|Thus Allah seals the hearts of those who don’t know.
030|060|So be patient; the promise of Allah is truth. And let not those who lack certainty discourage you.
031|001|Alif. Lam. Meem.
031|002|These are the verses of the Book of Wisdom.
031|003|Guidance and mercy for the doers of good.
031|004|Those who perform prayer, give purifying charity, and are certain of the Hereafter.
031|005|These are guided by their Lord. These are the successful.
031|006|Some people purchase vain talk to mislead others from Allah’s path without knowledge, and they treat it with ridicule. For them, a humiliating punishment awaits.
031|007|When Our verses are recited to him, he turns away arrogantly, as if he didn’t hear them, as if his ears are blocked. So, inform him of a severe punishment.
031|008|Those who believe and do righteous deeds—for them are Gardens of Delight.
031|009|Where they will dwell eternally. The promise of Allah is truth. He is the Mighty, the Wise.
031|010|He created the heavens with no visible pillars, and He placed firm mountains on the earth, lest it shakes with you. He spread throughout it a variety of living creatures. We send down rain from the sky, causing all types of fine plants to grow.
031|011|This is the creation of Allah. Now, show Me what those other than Him have created. The wrongdoers are in clear error.
031|012|We granted Luqman wisdom: “Give thanks to Allah. Whoever is grateful, it is for his own good. And whoever is ungrateful—Allah is Self-Sufficient and Praiseworthy.”
031|013|Luqman said to his son while counseling him, “O my son, don’t associate anything with Allah, for polytheism is a tremendous injustice.”
031|014|We instructed the human being to honor his parents. His mother carried him with hardship and gave birth to him in pain, and his weaning takes two years. Be grateful to Me and your parents; to Me is the final destination.
031|015|But if they endeavor to make you associate others with Me, of which you don’t know, don’t obey them. However, treat them kindly in this world, and follow the path of those who turn to Me. Then, to Me is your return, and I will inform you of everything you did.
031|016|“O my son, even the weight of a mustard seed, whether hidden in a rock, the heavens, or on earth, Allah will bring it forth. Allah is Subtle, All-Aware.
031|017|O my son, establish prayer, advocate for righteousness, forbid what’s wrong, and be patient with whatever happens to you. These are matters of determination.
031|018|And don’t turn your cheek in scorn towards people, and don’t strut around exultantly on earth. Allah doesn’t like any arrogant boaster.
031|019|And walk modestly and lower your voice; the most unpleasant of sounds is the braying of donkeys.”
031|020|Don’t you see that Allah subjected everything in the heavens and on earth to you, and He showered upon you His visible and hidden blessings? Yet some argue about Allah without knowledge, guidance, and an enlightening scripture.
031|021|When they’re advised, “Follow what Allah revealed,” they respond, “No, we follow what we found our ancestors doing.” Even if Satan is leading them towards the torment of the Inferno?
031|022|Whoever submits completely to Allah and leads a righteous life has grasped the most secure handhold. The ultimate outcome of all matters is to Allah.
031|023|As for those who disbelieve, don’t let their disbelief sadden you. They will return to Us, and We will inform them of their deeds. Allah is fully aware of the contents of the hearts.
031|024|We give them little enjoyment, but ultimately, We will drive them to a harsh punishment.
031|025|If you ask them, “Who created the heavens and the earth?” They would answer, “Allah.” Say, “Praise be to Allah.” But most of them don’t understand.
031|026|To Allah belongs everything in the heavens and the earth. Allah is the Rich, the Praiseworthy.
031|027|Even if all the trees on earth were made into pens, and the ocean, supplemented by seven additional oceans, were turned into ink, Allah’s words wouldn’t be depleted. Allah is Exalted in Might and Wisdom.
031|028|Your creation and resurrection are akin to that of a single soul. Allah is All-Hearing, All-Seeing.
031|029|Don’t you see how Allah merges night into day and day into night? How He subjected the sun and the moon, each running for a specified period, and that Allah is fully aware of your deeds?
031|030|This is because Allah is the Absolute Truth, and anything that they invoke beside Him is false. Allah is the Exalted, the Great.
031|031|Don’t you see how ships sail across the sea by Allah’s grace, to show you some of His signs? In this, there are signs for every patient, grateful person.
031|032|When engulfed by towering waves, they call upon Allah, sincerely devoted to Him. Yet, once he brings them safely to land, some of them waver. Only the ungrateful, treacherous denies Our signs.
031|033|O people! Be mindful of your Lord, and fear a Day when no parent can avail their child, nor can a child avail their parent. Indeed, the promise of Allah is true. Therefore, let not the transient life deceive you, and let not the arch-deceiver deceive you about Allah.
031|034|The knowledge of the Hour is with Allah. He sends down the rain, and He knows what’s in the wombs. No soul knows what it will earn tomorrow, and no soul knows in which land it will die. Allah is All-Knowing, Fully-Aware.
032|001|Alif. Lam. Meem.
032|002|This Book, beyond doubt, is a revelation from the Lord of the worlds.
032|003|Do they say, “He fabricated it”? No, it is the truth from your Lord, to warn a people who received no prior warning, so they may be guided.
032|004|It is Allah who created the heavens and the earth, and whatever is between, in six periods, then He established Himself upon the throne. You have no protector or intercessor apart from Him. Will you not remember?
032|005|He directs the affairs from the heavens to the earth; then it ascends to Him, in a Day the measure of which is a thousand years according to your calculations.
032|006|He is the Knower of the unseen and the seen, the Almighty, the Most Merciful.
032|007|He who perfected everything that He created and began the creation of man from clay.
032|008|Then, He made his reproduction from an extract of a base fluid.
032|009|Then He shaped him and breathed into him from His Spirit, giving you hearing, sight, and intelligence. Yet, you are seldom grateful.
032|010|They question, “After we have disintegrated into the earth, are we to be created anew?” In fact, they deny the meeting with their Lord.
032|011|Say, “The angel of death, assigned to you, will reclaim you, then you will be returned to your Lord.”
032|012|If only you could see when the guilty bow their heads before their Lord: “Our Lord, we’ve seen and heard, so send us back, and we will act righteously. We are now convinced.”
032|013|Had We willed, We could’ve given every soul its guidance, but My decree has been fulfilled: “I will fill Hell with jinn and humans altogether.”
032|014|So taste, because you forgot the meeting of this Day of yours. We’ve forgotten you. Taste the punishment of eternity for what you used to do.
032|015|When reminded of them, those who believe in Our revelations fall prostrate and glorify their Lord with praise, without any pride.
032|016|Their sides shun their beds, calling upon their Lord in fear and hope. And from what We’ve provided for them, they spend.
032|017|No soul knows what delights to the eyes are kept hidden for it—a reward for their deeds.
032|018|Is the believer like the sinner? They are not equal.
032|019|As for those who believe and do righteous deeds, for them are the Gardens of Refuge, as accommodation for what they used to do.
032|020|But for those who defiantly disobey, their dwelling will be the Fire. Every time they wish to get out of it, they will be returned to it, and it will be said to them, “Taste the punishment of the Fire which you used to deny.”
032|021|We will make them taste the lesser suffering, before the greater suffering, so they may return.
032|022|Who is more unjust than the one who, when reminded of his Lord’s verses, turns away from them? We will take revenge on the criminals.
032|023|We gave Moses the Scripture, so don’t be in doubt about His meeting. And We made it a guide for the Children of Israel.
032|024|We selected leaders from among them, who, under Our guidance, directed others, as long as they demonstrated steadfastness and had unwavering belief in Our revelations.
032|025|On the Day of Resurrection, your Lord will adjudicate among them concerning the matters they disputed.
032|026|Isn’t it a lesson for them, how many generations We destroyed before them, in whose dwellings they walk? Indeed in that are signs; do they not hear?
032|027|Don’t they see that We drive water to barren land, and with it, We produce crops that they and their livestock eat? Can’t they see?
032|028|And they say, “When will this judgment come, if you are truthful?”
032|029|Say, “On the day of judgment, the faith of those who disbelieved won’t benefit them, nor will they be reprieved.”
032|030|So turn away from them and wait, they are also waiting.
033|001|O Prophet, be aware of Allah, and don’t obey the unbelievers and the hypocrites. Allah is All-Knowing, Most Wise.
033|002|Follow what has been revealed to you from your Lord, for Allah is fully aware of what you do.
033|003|And trust in Allah; and sufficient is Allah as Disposer of affairs.
033|004|Allah didn’t place two hearts within any man’s body. He didn’t make your wives, whom you equate with your mothers, your actual mothers. Nor did He make your adopted children, your actual children. These are but words from your mouths. Allah speaks the truth, and He guides along the path.
033|005|Name them after their fathers; this is more equitable in Allah’s sight. If you don’t know their fathers, they are your brothers in faith and dependents. There is no blame upon you for the mistakes you make, but only for what your hearts purposely intend. Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.
033|006|The Prophet is closer to the believers than themselves, and his wives are mothers to them. As decreed by Allah, blood relatives have greater rights over each other than the believers and the emigrants. However, you are still obligated to treat your friends kindly. This is inscribed in the Scripture.
033|007|We received a solemn oath from the Prophets, including you, Noah, Abraham, Moses, and Jesus, son of Mary. We received from them a firm covenant.
033|008|He will then question the truthful about their truthfulness, and He prepared a severe punishment for the unbelievers.
033|009|O you who believe, remember Allah’s favor upon you, when armies advanced against you, and We sent upon them a wind and forces you didn’t see. Allah is watchful of all your actions.
033|010|When they advanced upon you from above and below, your vision blurred, your hearts reached the throats, and you began to doubt Allah.
033|011|There, the believers were tested and severely shaken.
033|012|The hypocrites and those with diseased hearts said, “Allah and His Messenger promised us nothing but delusions.”
033|013|Among them, some said, “O people of Yathrib, you can’t withstand, so retreat.” Meanwhile, others sought permission from the Prophet, saying, “Our homes are exposed,” when they were not. They only intended to flee.
033|014|If they had been invaded from all sides, and they were incited to sedition, they would’ve indulged in it.
033|015|They had previously made a covenant with Allah that they wouldn’t turn their backs. The covenant with Allah must be answered for.
033|016|Say, “Fleeing won’t benefit you, if you flee from death or killing. Even then, you would be indulged only a little.”
033|017|Say, “Who can protect you from Allah if He intends harm or mercy for you?” They will find no ally or helper besides Allah.
033|018|Allah knows those among you who discourage others and those who say to their brethren, “Come to us,” yet they seldom engage in battle.
033|019|They are reluctant to support you. When danger looms, you see them staring at you, their eyes rolling, as if they are on the verge of death. Yet, when the threat subsides, they lash you with sharp tongues, greedy for the good. These were never believers, so Allah nullified their deeds, a task effortless for Allah.
033|020|They assumed that the Confederates wouldn’t retreat. If the Confederates were to return, they would wish they were amongst the Bedouins in the desert, seeking news about you. If they were with you, they would hardly engage in battle.
033|021|In Allah’s Messenger, you have an excellent example for those who hope for Allah and the Last Day and remember Allah often.
033|022|Upon seeing the Confederate forces, the believers said, “This is what Allah and His Messenger promised us; truly, Allah and His Messenger spoke the truth.” It only increased them in faith and submission.
033|023|Among the believers are men who have been true to their covenant with Allah. Some of them have met their obligations, and some are still waiting, unwavering in their commitment.
033|024|That Allah may reward the truthful for their truthfulness, and He may punish the hypocrites if He wills or accept their repentance. Allah is Forgiving, Most Merciful.
033|025|And Allah repulsed those who disbelieved, in their rage; they gained no advantage. Allah was sufficient for the believers in battle. Allah is Powerful, Most Dignified.
033|026|He brought down those who supported them among the People of the Scripture from their fortresses, and He cast terror into their hearts. You killed some and took others as captives.
033|027|He let you inherit their lands, their houses, their wealth, and lands you had not trodden. Allah has power over all things.
033|028|O Prophet, tell your wives, “If you desire the worldly life and its glitter, then come; I will provide for you and release you honorably.
033|029|But if you wish for Allah and His Messenger and the Home of the Hereafter, then indeed, Allah has prepared for those who do good among you an immense reward.
033|030|O wives of the Prophet, those who commit a clear immorality among you, doubled will be her suffering, and that is easy for Allah.
033|031|And whoever of you devoutly obeys Allah and His messenger and does good, We will give her her reward twice over, and We have prepared for her a noble provision.
033|032|O wives of the Prophet, you are unlike any other women if you uphold righteousness. Therefore, don’t be seductive in speech, lest he in whose heart is a disease should desire, but speak with appropriate speech.
033|033|Settle in your homes, and don’t flaunt your beauty, as in the former days of ignorance. Establish prayer, give the purifying charity, and obey Allah and His Messenger. Allah intends to remove all impurities from you, O People of the Household, and to purify you thoroughly.
033|034|Be mindful of what’s recited in your homes of Allah’s verses and wisdom. Allah is always Kind and Well-Informed.
033|035|The submissive men and women, the believing men and women, the devout men and women, the honest men and women, the patient men and women, the humble men and women, the charitable men and women, the fasting men and women, the men and women who guard their chastity, and the men and women who frequently remember Allah—for them, Allah has prepared forgiveness and a great reward.
033|036|Believers, both men and women, have no right to question the decisions made by Allah and His Messenger. Those who disobey Allah and His Messenger have deviated into clear error.
033|037|You said to the one whom Allah had favored and you had favored, “Keep your wife and fear Allah,” while concealing within yourself what Allah was going to reveal. You feared people, but it is more appropriate that you fear Allah. Then, when Zaid had dissolved his marriage with her, We wedded her to you, so that there would be no fault in believers marrying the divorced wives of their adopted sons. Allah’s command is always fulfilled.
033|038|The Prophet is not liable for what Allah has ordained for him. This is Allah’s established way with those who came before. The command of Allah is a destiny determined.
033|039|Those who convey Allah’s messages, fear Him, and fear none but Allah. Allah is sufficient as a Reckoner.
033|040|Muhammad is not the father of any man among you, but he is Allah’s Messenger and the Prophets’ seal. Allah has full knowledge of all things.
033|041|O you who believe, remember Allah with much remembrance.
033|042|And praise Him morning and evening.
033|043|It is He who reaches out to you, and His angels, to bring you from darkness into light. He is ever Merciful to the believers.
033|044|Their greeting on the Day they meet Him will be “Peace,” and He prepared for them a generous reward.
033|045|O Prophet, We sent you as a witness, a bearer of good news, and a warner.
033|046|Inviting to Allah by His permission, and as a luminous lamp.
033|047|Give the believers the good news of Allah’s abundant grace.
033|048|Don’t obey the unbelievers and the hypocrites; dismiss their annoyances, and rely on Allah. Allah is sufficient as a Protector.
033|049|O you who believe, when you marry believing women and then divorce them before you have touched them, you have no obligation to observe a waiting period for them. Provide for them, and release them graciously.
033|050|O Prophet, We’ve made lawful for you your wives to whom you’ve given their due compensation, and what your right hand possesses from what Allah has granted you. Also, the daughters of your paternal uncle, and the daughters of your paternal aunts, and the daughters of your maternal uncle, and the daughters of your maternal aunts who migrated with you. Additionally, a believing woman who offered herself to the Prophet, if the Prophet desires to marry her—exclusively for you, not for the other believers. We certainly know what We ordained for them regarding their wives and those their right hands possess, so that there may be no discomfort for you. Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.
033|051|You may postpone any of those you wish, and you may receive anyone you wish. There is no blame on you if you invite one whose turn you had previously set aside. This is more appropriate, so that they may be comforted, not saddened, and may all be pleased with what you give them. Allah knows what’s in your hearts. Allah is All-Knowing, Most Forbearing.
033|052|No women are lawful for you after this, nor can you exchange them for other wives, even if their beauty captivates you, except what your right hand possesses. Allah is watchful over everything.
033|053|O you who believe, don’t enter the Prophet’s homes for a meal, unless you are invited, and don’t wait for its preparation. But if you are invited, then enter. And when you have eaten, then disperse, not lingering for conversation. This behavior may cause the Prophet discomfort, and he would be shy to dismiss you, but Allah is not shy of the truth. When you ask his wives for something, do so from behind a partition. This is purer for your hearts and theirs. It is not suitable for you to offend Allah’s Messenger, nor should you ever marry his wives after him. Indeed, this would be a grave offense in Allah’s sight.
033|054|Whether you reveal something or conceal it, Allah is always aware of everything.
033|055|There is no blame on them regarding their fathers, sons, brothers, brothers’ sons, sisters’ sons, their women, or those under their protection. So let them fear Allah. Allah is a witness to everything.
033|056|Allah and His angels send blessings upon the Prophet. O you who believe, invoke blessings and peace upon him.
033|057|Those who insult Allah and His Messenger, Allah has cursed them in this world and the Hereafter, and He prepared for them a humiliating punishment.
033|058|Those who harm believing men and women undeservedly, bear on themselves the guilt of slander and a manifest sin.
033|059|O Prophet, instruct your wives, daughters, and the believers’ women to lengthen their garments, so they may be recognized and not be harassed. Allah is ever Forgiving, Most Merciful.
033|060|If the hypocrites, those in whose hearts is sickness, and those who spread malicious rumors in the city don’t cease, We will incite you against them; then they won’t be your neighbors therein except for a little while.
033|061|Cursed they are. Wherever they are found, they are to be apprehended and executed promptly.
033|062|This has been Allah’s established way with those who passed before. You will find no alteration in Allah’s way.
033|063|People ask you concerning the Hour. Say, “Knowledge of it is only with Allah. And what will make you know? Perhaps the Hour is near.”
033|064|Allah has cursed the unbelievers and prepared for them a blazing Fire.
033|065|There, they will remain forever, devoid of any protector or helper.
033|066|On the Day when their faces are flipped in the Fire, they will cry out, “Oh, how we wish we had obeyed Allah and the Messenger.”
033|067|And they will say, “Our Lord, we obeyed our leaders and great ones, but they led us astray from the path.
033|068|Our Lord, give them double the punishment and curse them severely.”
033|069|O you who believe, don’t be like those who hurt Moses, yet Allah absolved him of what they said. And he was distinguished in Allah’s sight.
033|070|O you who have faith, revere Allah, and always speak with straightforward words.
033|071|He will correct your actions and forgive your sins. Whoever obeys Allah and His Messenger has achieved a magnificent triumph.
033|072|We presented the trust to the heavens, the earth, and the mountains, but they refused to bear it, fearing its consequences. However, man undertook it, being inherently unjust and ignorant.
033|073|Allah will punish the hypocritical men and women, and the polytheistic men and women. And Allah pardons the believing men and women. Allah is always Forgiving, Most Merciful.
034|001|Praise be to Allah, to whom belongs everything in the heavens and the earth, and praise be to Him in the Hereafter. He is the Wise, the Expert.
034|002|He knows what penetrates the earth and what emerges from it, what descends from the sky, and what ascends to it. He is the Merciful, the Forgiving.
034|003|Those disbelieving say, “The Hour won’t come upon us.” Say, “Yes, by my Lord, it will surely come upon you. He is the Knower of the Unseen.” Not an atom’s weight within the heavens and the earth escapes from His knowledge, nor anything smaller or larger, but it is recorded in a clear book.
034|004|He will reward those who believe and do good deeds. For them is forgiveness and generous provision.
034|005|But for those who strive against Our verses, trying to undermine them, will be a torment of painful wrath.
034|006|Those endowed with knowledge recognize that what’s revealed to you from your Lord is the truth, guiding to the path of the Almighty, the Praiseworthy.
034|007|Those who disbelieved said, “Shall we point out to you a man who will inform you, that when you’ve disintegrated completely, you will be created anew?”
034|008|“Did he invent a lie about Allah, or is he afflicted with madness?” Those who don’t believe in the Hereafter suffer and are far astray.
034|009|Didn’t they consider what’s before them and what’s behind them of the heavens and the earth? If We will, We could let the earth swallow them, or drop pieces of the sky on them. In this, there is a sign for every returning servant.
034|010|We bestowed upon David a grace from Us: “O mountains, sing praises with him, and you birds as well.” And We softened iron for him.
034|011|“Craft coats of armor, and balance the links well. And work righteousness. I am observant of what you do.”
034|012|For Solomon, the wind, its outward journey was one month, and its return journey was one month. We made a spring of tar flow for him. Among Jinns are those who worked for him by his Lord’s permission. Whoever deviated from Our command among them, We made him taste of the punishment of the Blaze.
034|013|They made for him whatever he pleased—sanctuaries, statues, bowls like reservoirs, and firmly fixed cooking pots. “Work gratefully, O house of David.” But few of My servants are grateful.
034|014|When We decreed his death, nothing showed them his death except an earthworm consuming his staff. When he fell, the jinn perceived that if they had known the unseen, they wouldn’t have remained in the shameful torment.
034|015|There was a sign for Sheba in their homeland: two gardens, one on the right and one on the left. “Eat from your Lord’s provisions, and give thanks to Him. A good land and a forgiving Lord.”
034|016|Yet they turned away, so We sent upon them the Flood of Dam, and We replaced their two gardens with gardens yielding bitter fruit, tamarisks, and a few thorny shrubs.
034|017|We penalized them for their ingratitude. Would we penalize any but the ungrateful?
034|018|We placed between them and the towns that We had blessed, prominent towns, and We determined the distances between them: “Travel safely between them, night and day.”
034|019|Yet they said, “Our Lord, extend the distances of our journeys,” and they wronged themselves. As a result, We made them legends and scattered them in every direction. There are signs in this for every patient, grateful individual.
034|020|Satan’s prediction for them proved accurate; they followed him, except for a group of believers.
034|021|He had no authority over them, except to distinguish those who believed in the Hereafter from those who harbored doubts. Your Lord oversees everything.
034|022|Say, “Call upon those you claim besides Allah. They don’t possess even an atom’s weight in the heavens or the earth, nor do they have any share in them. And He has no helpers among them.”
034|023|Intercession with Him avails nothing except those to whom He grants permission. Once fear is dispelled from their hearts, they will ask, “What did your Lord say?” They will answer, “The truth; and He is the Most High, the Great.”
034|024|Say, “Who provides for you from the heavens and the earth?” Say, “Allah,” and “Either us or you are on guidance or clearly in the wrong.”
034|025|Say, “You won’t be held accountable for our sins, nor will we be held accountable for your actions.”
034|026|Say, “Our Lord will gather us together, then He will judge justly between us. He is the All-Knowing Judge.”
034|027|Say, “Show me those you’ve attached to Him as partners. No, indeed! He is Allah, the Mighty, the Wise.”
034|028|We sent you as a messenger to all of humanity, bearing good news and warnings, but most people are unaware.
034|029|They ask, “When is this promise, if you are truthful?”
034|030|Say, “For you, there is a promised Day. You cannot delay it by an hour, nor can you bring it forward.”
034|031|The unbelievers say, “We will never believe in this Quran, nor in what preceded it.” If only you could see the wrongdoers, held captive before their Lord, casting blame on one another. Those who were oppressed will say to those who were arrogant, “If not for you, we would’ve been believers.”
034|032|The arrogant will answer the oppressed, “Did we deter you from guidance after it had reached you? No, indeed, you were the ones who transgressed.”
034|033|The oppressed will say to the arrogant, “Rather, it was your constant scheming, day and night, urging us to disbelieve in Allah and set up rivals to Him.” And they will hide their regret when they see the punishment. We will place iron collars around the necks of the unbelievers. Won’t they be recompensed for what they did?
034|034|Every time We sent a warner to a city, its affluent inhabitants responded by saying, “We reject the message you’ve been sent with.”
034|035|They say, “We have more wealth and children, and we won’t be punished.”
034|036|Say, “My Lord expands and restricts provision for whom He wills, yet most people don’t know.”
034|037|It is not your wealth or your children that will bring you closer to Us. But those who believe and perform righteous deeds—their rewards will be multiplied, and they will reside in secure homes.
034|038|Those who strive to invalidate Our verses will be subject to punishment.
034|039|Say, “My Lord provides for whom He wills among His servants and restricts for him. Whatever you spend of anything, He will replace it; and He is the best of providers.”
034|040|On the Day He will gather them all together, then say to the angels, “Was it you these people used to worship?”
034|041|They will respond, “Glory to You! Our loyalty is to You, not to them. Rather, they were worshiping the jinn; most of them were believers in them.”
034|042|“Today, you have no power to benefit or harm one another.” And We will say to those who acted unjustly, “Taste the punishment of the Fire, which you used to deny.”
034|043|When Our clear verses are recited to them, they say, “This is nothing but a man who wants to deviate you from what your fathers worshiped.” And they say, “This is nothing but fabricated fiction.” When truth reaches those who disbelieve, they dismiss it as nothing but an obvious sorcery.
