038|022|They startled David when they entered upon him. They said, “Fear not. We are two litigants; one has wronged the other. Judge justly between us, show no bias, and guide us to the right way.”
038|023|“My brother has ninety-nine ewes, while I have only one. Yet he insisted, ‘Entrust it to me,’ and he overpowered me in speech.”
038|024|He responded, “He wronged you by demanding your single ewe be added to his flock. Indeed, many associates wrong one another, except for those who believe and do righteous deeds, and they are few.” Then David realized that We were testing him, so he asked forgiveness from his Lord, fell prostrate, and he turned in repentance.
038|025|We forgave him for that. He holds a position of closeness to Us and a beautiful destination.
038|026|“O David, We made you a successor on earth, so judge between people with justice, and don’t follow desire, lest it diverts you from Allah’s way. Those who stray from Allah’s way will face a severe punishment for forgetting the Day of Account.”
038|027|We didn’t create the heavens, the earth, and everything between them in vain. That’s the misconception of those who disbelieve—woe to the unbelievers from the Fire.
038|028|Shall We treat those who believe and perform righteous deeds the same as those who spread corruption on earth? Or should We treat the devout as the wicked?
038|029|We revealed to you a blessed Book, so they may ponder its verses, and those with discernment may reflect.
038|030|To David, We granted Solomon—a good servant, deeply devoted.
038|031|One evening, fine horses were paraded before him.
038|032|He said, “I have loved material wealth over the remembrance of my Lord—until they disappeared from sight.
038|033|Bring them back to me.” And he began to stroke their legs and necks.
038|034|We tested Solomon, and We placed a figure on his throne. Then he turned back.
038|035|He prayed, “My Lord, forgive me, and grant me a kingdom that none after me can attain; You are the Bestower.”
038|036|So, We subjected the wind to his command, flowing gently at his discretion.
038|037|And also the demons—every builder and diver.
038|038|And others shackled in chains.
038|039|“This is Our gift, so dispense or withhold, without account.”
038|040|He holds a position of proximity to Us, and a beautiful final destination.
038|041|And remember Our servant Job, who appealed to his Lord: “Satan afflicted me with hardship and suffering.”
038|042|“Strike with your foot. Here is cool water for washing and drinking.”
038|043|We restored his family to him, and the same with them, as a mercy from Us, and a lesson for those with understanding.
038|044|“And take in your hand a bundle and strike with it, and don’t break your oath.” We found him patient. What an excellent servant he was, always returning.
038|045|And mention Our servants Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob, possessors of strength and insight.
038|046|We granted them a unique favor—the remembrance of the Home.
038|047|They are among Our chosen ones, the outstanding.
038|048|Also remember Ishmael, Elisha, and Ezekiel. Each of them was among the excellent.
038|049|This is a reminder. For the virtuous, there is a beautiful place of return.
038|050|Gardens of Eternity, the gates of which will be open to them.
038|051|Reclining therein, they will call for ample fruit and drink.
038|052|Along with them will be chaste women with modest gaze, of equal age.
038|053|This is what you are promised for the Day of Reckoning.
038|054|This is Our provision, which has no end.
038|055|But for the transgressors, there will be a dreadful place of return.
038|056|Hell—where they will burn, a horrific resting place.
038|057|Let them taste it—boiling water and bitter cold.
038|058|And other torments of a similar kind.
038|059|Here is a group rushing headlong with you. They shall roast in the Fire.
038|060|They will cry out, “No, you are not welcome! It is you who prepared this for us. What a terrible destination!”
038|061|Then they will plead, “Our Lord, whoever led us to this, increase his suffering in the Fire.”
038|062|They will ask, “Why don’t we see those we considered evil?
038|063|Were we mistaken in mocking them, or did our eyes fail to recognize them?”
038|064|This is the quarrel among the dwellers of the Fire.
038|065|Say, “I am only a warner, and there is no god except Allah, the Singular, the Prevailing.
038|066|The Lord of the heavens and the earth, and whatever is between them, the Mighty, the Forgiving.”
038|067|Say, “This is a significant message.
038|068|From which you are turning away.
038|069|I have no knowledge of the Exalted Assembly when they argue.
038|070|It has only been revealed to me that I am a clear warner.”
038|071|When your Lord told the angels, “I am creating a human being from clay.
038|072|Once I have shaped him and breathed into him of My Spirit, prostrate before him.”
038|073|So the angels prostrated all of them together.
038|074|Except for Iblis—he was arrogant and became one of the unbelievers.
038|075|He questioned, “O Iblis, what prevented you from prostrating before the one I created with My hands? Are you too proud, or are you of high rank?”
038|076|He answered, “I am better than him. You created me from fire, while You created him from clay.”
038|077|He commanded, “Then get out of here, for you are an outcast, banished.
038|078|And My curse will be upon you until Judgement Day.”
038|079|He said, “My Lord, allow me to remain until the Day they’re resurrected.”
038|080|He responded, “You are allowed to remain.
038|081|Until the day of the well-known time.”
038|082|He vowed, “By Your might, I will surely seduce them all.
038|083|Except for Your devoted servants among them.”
038|084|He said, “The truth and only the truth I speak.
038|085|I will fill Hell with you and with those of them who follow you—all together.”
038|086|Say, “I ask no reward from you for this, nor am I a pretender.
038|087|It is but a reminder for the world.
038|088|And you will know its news after a while.”
039|001|This Book is a divine revelation from Allah, the Almighty, the Wise.
039|002|We revealed to you the Book of Truth. Therefore, worship Allah, dedicating your religion to Him alone.
039|003|Isn’t exclusive devotion due to Allah? Those who take protectors besides Him say, “We worship them only to bring us closer to Allah.” Allah will judge their differences. Allah doesn’t guide the lying disbeliever.
039|004|If Allah had intended to take a child, He could’ve chosen what He willed from His creation. Glory be to Him! He is Allah, the One, the Overpowering.
039|005|He created the heavens and the earth with purpose. He wraps the night over the day, and He wraps the day over the night. He subjected the sun and the moon, each running for a predetermined period. He is the Almighty, the Forgiving.
039|006|He created you from a single soul. Then, from it, He formed its mate. He sent down eight pairs of livestock for you. He formed you within your mothers’ wombs in successive stages, within a triple darkness. Such is Allah, your Lord; His is the sovereignty. There is no god but Him, so why do you deviate?
039|007|If you are ungrateful, Allah doesn’t need you. Yet, He doesn’t approve of ingratitude from His beings. If you are grateful, He is pleased with you. No bearer of burdens can bear the burdens of another. Ultimately, your return is to your Lord, who will inform you of everything you did. He knows the secrets within the hearts.
039|008|When adversity befalls a person, he earnestly prays to his Lord. Yet, when He bestows a favor upon him from Himself, he forgets his previous appeal, attributing rivals to Allah, leading others astray from His path. Say, “Enjoy your denial for a little while; you are among the inmates of the Fire.”
039|009|Can he who worships devoutly in the watches of the night, prostrating himself and standing in prayer, fearing the Hereafter and hoping for the mercy of his Lord, be like the one who does not? Say, “Could those who know be equal to those who don’t know?” Only those endowed with understanding will take heed.
039|010|Tell My faithful servants always to be mindful of their Lord. For those who do good in this world, there is goodness. Allah’s earth is vast, and the patient will be given their rewards without account.
039|011|Say, “I am commanded to worship Allah, dedicating my faith entirely to Him.
039|012|And I am also commanded to be the first of the Submitters.”
039|013|Say, “I fear the punishment of a formidable Day should I disobey my Lord.”
039|014|Say, “I worship Allah, dedicating my religion purely to Him.”
039|015|“So, worship whatever you want besides Him.” Say, “The losers are those who lose themselves and their families on Resurrection Day.” Most certainly, that’s the most significant loss.
039|016|Upon them are layers of fire, and beneath them are layers. This is how Allah instills fear into His beings. “O My beings, be mindful of Me.”
039|017|As for those who shun false worship and turn in repentance to Allah, for them are glad tidings. So, give good news to My servants.
039|018|Those who listen to the word and follow the best of it are the ones whom Allah has guided, and they are the ones blessed with discernment.
039|019|As for those who deserve the punishment—can you save those who are in the Fire?
039|020|Yet, those who revere their Lord will have lofts, constructed one above another, beneath which rivers flow. This is the promise of Allah, Allah does not fail in His promise.
039|021|Don’t you see how Allah sends down water from the sky, seeping into the earth to form springs? Through them, He produces crops of different colors. Then they wither, and you see them turn yellow, before He reduces them to chaff. In that is a reminder for those who have understanding.
039|022|Consider the one whose heart Allah has opened to Submission, thus receiving enlightenment from his Lord. Woe to those whose hearts have hardened against Allah’s remembrance—those are in obvious error.
039|023|Allah revealed the most excellent message: a book consistent in its teachings, offering repeated reinforcement and serving as a reminder. The skins of those who revere their Lord shiver due to it. Then, their skins and hearts soften to Allah’s remembrance. This is Allah’s guidance, through which He guides whom He wills. But he whom Allah leaves to stray has no guide.
039|024|What about the person who shields his face from the terrible suffering on Resurrection Day? To the evildoers, it will be said, “Taste what you’ve earned.”
039|025|Those before them also denied, so the punishment befell them from where they were unaware.
039|026|Thus, Allah made them taste disgrace in this worldly life, but the punishment of the Hereafter is indeed greater—if only they knew.
039|027|In this Quran, We present various parables for people to ponder.
039|028|A Quran in Arabic, without any discrepancy, so they may become cautious.
039|029|Allah presents an example of a man having quarreling partners and another man entirely belonging to one man. Can they be considered equal? Praise be to Allah! Yet, most of them don’t understand.
039|030|You will surely die, and they, too, will die.
039|031|Then, on Resurrection Day, you will dispute in the presence of your Lord.
039|032|Who could be more unjust than the one who fabricates lies about Allah and denies the truth when it reaches him? Isn’t there a dwelling in Hell for the unbelievers?
039|033|Yet, those who brought the truth and believed in it—these are the righteous ones.
039|034|They will have all that they desire with their Lord. That’s the reward of the good-doers.
039|035|Allah will absolve them of their worst deeds, and He will reward them according to their best deeds.
039|036|Isn’t Allah sufficient for His servant? They threaten you with those other than Him. Whomever Allah allows to stray has no guide.
039|037|And whomever Allah guides—there is none to lead him astray. Isn’t Allah the Almighty, the Avenger?
039|038|If you were to ask them, “Who created the heavens and the earth?” They would surely answer, “Allah.” Then, ask, “Did you consider those you call upon besides Allah? If Allah intends harm for me, would they lift His harm from me? Or if He intends mercy for me, would they withhold His mercy?” Say, “Allah suffices me; in Him trust those who put their trust.”
039|039|Say, “O my people, continue doing whatever you are doing, just as I am. You will soon come to know.
039|040|To whom a punishment comes that disgraces him, on whom an enduring torment descends.”
039|041|We revealed to you the Book for mankind in truth. Whoever follows guidance does so for his good, and whoever goes astray does so to his own loss. You are not responsible for them.
039|042|Allah takes the souls at the time of their death and those that haven’t died in their sleep. He retains those for whom death was decreed, and He sends the others back until their appointed time. In this are signs for those who reflect.
039|043|Or have they taken besides Allah intercessors? Say, “Even though they don’t possess anything, nor do they reason?”
039|044|Say, “All intercession belongs exclusively to Allah. His is the dominion over the heavens and the earth. To Him, you will be returned.”
039|045|And when Allah is mentioned alone, the hearts of those who don’t believe in the Hereafter shrink with aversion, but when those other than Him are mentioned, immediately they rejoice.
039|046|Say: “O Allah, Originator of the heavens and the earth, Knower of the unseen and the witnessed, You will arbitrate among Your servants regarding their disputes.”
039|047|If the wrongdoers possessed everything on earth, and twice as much, they would surely offer it to ransom themselves from the horrific punishment on Resurrection Day. And there will come to them, from Allah, what they had not been counting on.
039|048|They will be confronted with the bad outcomes of their actions, and what they used to ridicule will come back to haunt them.
039|049|When adversity touches a person, he implores Us. But when We bestow a favor upon him, he says, “I acquired this through my knowledge and skill.” Indeed, it is just a trial, but most of them don’t realize.
039|050|Those who preceded them said the same, but their ill-gotten gains availed them not.
039|051|The repercussions of their evil deeds overwhelmed them, and the wrongdoers of this era will also face the consequences of their actions, from which they can’t escape.
039|052|Don’t they realize that Allah expands the provision for whom He wills and restricts it as well? In this are signs for people of faith.
039|053|Say, “O my servants who have transgressed against yourselves: Don’t despair of Allah’s mercy, Allah forgives all sins. It is He who is the Merciful, the Forgiving.”
039|054|Return with wholehearted repentance to your Lord, and submit yourselves completely to Him, before the suffering befalls you, after which you won’t be helped.
039|055|Adhere to the best of what was revealed to you from your Lord, before the punishment engulfs you unexpectedly.
039|056|Lest a soul should lament, “Alas, I have neglected my duty towards Allah and was among the mockers.”
039|057|Or it may say, “Had Allah guided me, I would’ve been among the righteous.”
039|058|Or, it may say when it sees the penalty: “If only I had another chance, I would be among those who do good.”
039|059|But, indeed, My signs came to you, but you denied them, were arrogant, and became a disbeliever.
039|060|On the Day of Resurrection, you will see those who told lies about Allah, their faces blackened. Is not in Hell a residence for the arrogant?
039|061|Allah will deliver the righteous to their destined haven—no harm will touch them, nor will they grieve.
039|062|Allah is the Creator of all things, and He is, over all things, Disposer of affairs.
039|063|To Him belong the keys of the heavens and the earth. Those who deny Allah’s verses are the losers.
039|064|Say, “Do you instruct me to worship someone other than Allah, O ignorant people?”
039|065|It was revealed to you and those before you that if you associate, your deeds will be nullified, and you will be among the losers.
039|066|Rather, worship Allah alone, and be among the thankful.
039|067|They can’t grasp the full extent of Allah’s greatness. The entire earth will be His handful on the Day of Resurrection, and the heaven will be folded in His right hand. Glorified is He, and High above what they associate with Him.
039|068|The Trumpet will be blown, and whoever is in the heavens and in the earth will be struck with terror, except whom Allah wills. Then it will be sounded again, and at once they will be standing, looking on.
039|069|And the earth will shine with the light of its Lord, and the Record will be placed. The prophets and witnesses will be brought forward, judgment will be passed among them in truth, and they won’t be wronged.
039|070|And every soul will be fully compensated for what it has done. He is well aware of what they do.
039|071|The unbelievers will be driven to Hell in groups, until, when they reach it, its gates are opened, and its keepers will say to them, “Did not messengers come to you from yourselves, reciting to you the verses of your Lord and warning you of the meeting of this Day of yours?” They will say, “Yes, but the decree of punishment has been justified against the unbelievers.”
039|072|It will be said, “Enter the gates of Hell, to dwell therein forever.” Wretched is the dwelling of the arrogant!
039|073|Those who revered their Lord will be led in groups towards Paradise. When they near it, its gates will be opened, and its keepers will greet them: “Peace be upon you, you’ve been good; so enter here, to dwell forever.”
039|074|They will say, “Praise be to Allah, who fulfilled His promise to us and made us inherit this land, allowing us to settle in Paradise wherever we wish. How splendid is the reward of the workers.”
039|075|You will see the angels surrounding the Throne, glorifying their Lord with praises. And it was judged between them in truth, and it will be said, “Praise be to Allah, the Lord of the universes.”
040|001|Ha. Meem.
040|002|The revelation of the Scripture is from Allah, the Almighty, the All-Knowing.
040|003|He is the forgiver of sins, acceptor of repentance, severe in retribution, and of infinite forbearance. There is no god except Him; to Him is the ultimate return.
040|004|None dispute Allah’s revelations except those who disbelieve. Let not their activities in the lands deceive you.
040|005|The people of Noah denied the truth before them, as did the factions after them. Every community plotted against their own messenger, to seize him. They argued with falsehood to invalidate the truth. Yet, I seized them, and how severe was My retribution!
040|006|The decree of your Lord against those who disbelieve is just: “They are the occupants of the Fire.”
040|007|Those who carry the Throne, and those around it, glorify their Lord with praises, believe in Him, and plead for forgiveness for those who believe: “Our Lord, You encompass all things in mercy and knowledge; forgive those who have repented and followed Your path, and shield them from the torment of the Inferno.
040|008|Admit them, Our Lord, into the Gardens of Eternity, which You’ve promised them, along with the righteous among their parents, spouses, and offspring. You are the All-Powerful, the All-Wise.
040|009|And shield them from evil deeds. Whomever You shield from evil deeds on that Day has received Your mercy, and that’s the ultimate triumph.”
040|010|The disbelievers will be told, “Allah’s abhorrence of you is greater than your self-loathing, for when you were invited to faith, you refused.”
040|011|They will plead, “Our Lord, You’ve caused us to die twice, and You’ve given us life twice. Now we admit our sins; is there an escape?”
040|012|This is because when Allah alone was called upon, you disbelieved, but when partners were associated with Him, you believed. Judgment belongs to Allah, the Most High, the Supreme.
040|013|It is He who shows you His marvels and sends down sustenance from the sky for you. Only those who turn to Him will truly understand.
040|014|Invoke Allah, dedicating your devotion to Him, even though the unbelievers may detest it.
040|015|He is of the highest rank, the Master of all sovereignty. He sends down the Spirit by His command to whichever of His servants He wills, to warn of the Day of Encounter.
040|016|On that Day, they will emerge, with nothing about them will be hidden from Allah. To whom does sovereignty belong today? To Allah, the One, the Irresistible.
040|017|On that Day, every soul will be recompensed for what it has earned. There will be no injustice on that Day. Allah is swift in taking account.
040|018|Warn them of the approaching Day, when hearts are at throats, choked with fear. The wrongdoers will have no comforting friend, nor any intercessor who might be obeyed.
040|019|He knows the treachery of the eyes and what the hearts conceal.
040|020|Allah judges with the truth, while those they call upon other than Him can’t judge at all. Allah is the All-Hearing, the All-Seeing.
040|021|Didn’t they journey through the earth and see what was the end of those before them? They were stronger than them, and had more impact on the earth. Yet, Allah seized them for their sins, and they had no protector against Allah.
040|022|Their messengers came to them with clear signs, yet they disbelieved. So, Allah seized them. He is powerful and severe in retribution.
040|023|We sent Moses with Our signs and a manifest authority.
040|024|To Pharaoh, Haman, and Korah, but they said, “A magician, a liar”.
040|025|When he brought them the truth from Us, they said, “Kill the sons of those who believe with him, and spare their women.” Yet, the plots of the unbelievers are destined to fail.
040|026|Pharaoh declared, “Leave me to kill Moses, and let him appeal to his Lord. I fear he may change your religion or spread disorder in the land.”
040|027|Moses responded, “I seek refuge in my Lord and your Lord from every arrogant one who doesn’t believe in the Day of Reckoning.”
040|028|A believing man from Pharaoh’s family, who had concealed his faith, said, “Would you kill a man just because he says, ‘My Lord is Allah,’ and he brought you clear proofs from your Lord? If he is lying, his lie will be upon him, but if he’s truthful, then some of what he promises you will befall you. Surely, Allah doesn’t guide the extravagant liar.
040|029|O my people, you have the kingdom today and you are dominant in the land. But who will save us from Allah’s wrath, if it were to befall us?” Pharaoh said, “I only show you what I see and guide you to the path of right conduct.”
040|030|The believer continued, “O my people, I fear for you a fate like that of the day of the confederates.
040|031|Like the fate of the people of Noah, Aad, Thamud, and those after them. Allah doesn’t intend any injustice for the beings.
040|032|O my people, I fear for you the Day of Calling Out.
040|033|The Day when you will turn around and retreat, having no defender against Allah. Whomever Allah sends astray will have no guide.”
040|034|Joseph had previously come to you with clear proofs, but you remained doubtful about what he brought you. So when he died, you said, “Allah won’t send a messenger after him.” Thus, Allah misguides the transgressors and doubtful.
040|035|Those who dispute Allah’s verses, without any authority given to them, are greatly despised by Allah and those who believe. Thus, Allah seals the heart of every arrogant tyrant.
040|036|Pharaoh commanded, “O Haman, build me a tower, that I may reach the pathways.
040|037|The pathways into the heavens, so I may look at the God of Moses, but I think he’s a liar.” Thus, Pharaoh’s evil deeds were made appealing to him, and he was barred from the path. Pharaoh’s scheming led only to ruin.
040|038|The believer pleaded, “O my people, follow me, and I will guide you to the path of righteousness.”
040|039|“O my people, this worldly life is fleeting enjoyment, while the Hereafter is the home of permanence.”
040|040|He who does an evil deed will only be repaid with its equivalent. However, whoever acts righteously, whether male or female, while being a believer, will enter Paradise, where they will be provided for without measure.
040|041|“O my people! How is it that I invite you to salvation while you invite me to the Fire?
040|042|You urge me to disbelieve in Allah and to associate with Him what I don’t know, while I invite you to the Almighty, the Forgiving.
040|043|No doubt, what you invite me to has no calling in this world, nor in the Hereafter. Our return is to Allah, and the transgressors will be the inhabitants of the Fire.
040|044|You will soon remember what I say to you. I commit my affairs to Allah. Truly, Allah is Seeing of the beings.”
040|045|So Allah protected him from the evil schemes they plotted, while a terrible punishment engulfed Pharaoh’s people.
040|046|The Fire! They will be exposed to it morning and evening, and on the Day when the Hour sets in: “Admit Pharaoh’s family into the severest of punishment.”
040|047|As they quarrel in the Fire, the weak will say to those who were arrogant, “We were your followers; can you then relieve us of a portion of the Fire?”
040|048|The arrogant will reply, “We are all in it —Allah has already judged among the beings.”
040|049|Those in the Fire will beg the keepers of Hell, “Implore your Lord to lessen our suffering for just one day.”
040|050|They will respond, “Didn’t your messengers come to you with clear signs?” They will reply, “Yes.” They will say, “Then pray, but the prayers of the unbelievers are only in vain.”
040|051|We will surely aid Our messengers and those who believe, in the worldly life and on the Day when the witnesses arise.
040|052|The Day when their excuses won’t benefit the wrongdoers. For them is a curse, and they will have the worst dwelling.
040|053|We gave Moses the guidance, and We made the Children of Israel inherit the Scripture.
040|054|A guide and a reminder for people of understanding.
040|055|So be patient, the promise of Allah is truth. So ask forgiveness for your sin, and glorify your Lord with praise, morning and evening.
040|056|Those who dispute Allah’s revelations without any authority given to them, nothing resides in their breasts but vainglory which they will never achieve. So, seek refuge in Allah. He is the All-Hearing, the All-Seeing.
040|057|The creation of the heavens and the earth is greater than the creation of humankind, but most people don’t know.
040|058|Not equal are the blind and the seeing, nor are those who believe and perform good deeds and the wrongdoers. How little you reflect.
040|059|The Hour is coming, there is no doubt about it, yet most people don’t believe.
040|060|Your Lord says, “Pray to Me, and I will respond to you. Those who are too arrogant to worship Me will enter Hell humiliated.”
040|061|It is Allah who made the night for your rest and the day for visibility. Allah is full of Bounty to mankind, but most of them don’t give thanks.
040|062|That is Allah, your Lord, the Creator of all things; there is no deity but Him. So how are you deluded?
040|063|So it is that those who deny Allah’s signs deviate.
040|064|It is Allah who made the earth a dwelling for you, and the sky a structure. He formed you and perfected your forms, and provided you with good things. Such is Allah, your Lord. Blessed is Allah, the Lord of the realms.
040|065|He is the Living; there is no deity except Him. Call upon Him, dedicating your faith exclusively to Him. Praise be to Allah, the Lord of the worlds.
040|066|Say, “I have been forbidden to worship those you invoke apart from Allah, as clear proofs have come to me from my Lord, and I am commanded to submit to the Lord of the universes.”
040|067|It is He who created you from dust, then from a drop, then from a clot, and then He brings you out as infants. Then, you reach your full strength. Then, you become elderly—although some of you die earlier—that you may reach a appointed term and gain understanding.
040|068|It is He who gives life and causes death. When He decrees an affair, He says to it, “Be,” and it becomes.
040|069|Didn’t you see how those who dispute concerning Allah’s verses—how are they averted?
040|070|Those who deny the Scripture and what We sent Our messengers with, will indeed know.
040|071|With shackles around their necks, and dragged by chains.
040|072|In boiling water, then in the Fire they will be burnt.
040|073|Then it will be said to them, “Where are those whom you used to associate?
040|074|Besides Allah?” They will reply, “They have deserted us. Actually, we were not calling upon anything before.” In this way, Allah lets the unbelievers go astray.
040|075|This is because you exulted in the earth baselessly, and because you were frolicking.
040|076|Enter the gates of hell to stay therein forever—what a terrible abode for the arrogant!
040|077|Therefore, be patient; the promise of Allah is true. Whether We show you some of what We’ve promised them, or We cause you to pass away, to Us, they will be returned.
040|078|We sent messengers before you; some of their stories We’ve told you, and some We haven’t. No messenger can bring a sign except by Allah’s permission. When Allah’s decree comes, the matter will be settled in truth, and those who perpetuated falsehood will then lose.
040|079|It is Allah who made for you the livestock, that you may ride some of them and from some you eat.
040|080|And you have in them other benefits too, and you fulfill your diverse needs through them. You are carried upon them, as well as on ships.
040|081|And He shows you His signs: Which then of Allah’s signs will you deny?
040|082|Didn’t they travel through the earth and see the fate of those who preceded them? They were more numerous and powerful, having left more impressive marks on the earth, yet their achievements availed them not.
040|083|So when their messengers came to them with clear evidence, they exulted in the knowledge they already possessed, but what they used to mock encompassed them.
040|084|And when they saw Our wrath, they said, “We believe in Allah alone and reject what we were associating with Him.”
040|085|But their faith didn’t benefit them when they saw Our punishment. Such is Allah’s Law of dealing with His beings. And there, the unbelievers lost utterly.

041|002|A revelation from the Compassionate, the Merciful.
041|003|A Book whose verses have been detailed. An Arabic Quran for people who understand.
041|004|Bringing good news and warning, but most have turned away, so they don’t hear.
041|005|They say, “Our hearts are covered from what you call us towards, in our ears is deafness, and there is a veil between you and us. So act, we too are acting.”
041|006|Say, “I am only a human like you, divinely inspired that your God is One God. Be upright towards Him and ask for His forgiveness.” Woe to those who associate others with Him!
041|007|Those who don’t give purity and deny the Hereafter.
041|008|For those who believe and do good deeds, there is an endless reward.
041|009|Say, “Do you deny the One who created the earth in two periods? And do you attribute equals to Him? He is the Lord of the realms.”
041|010|He placed anchors upon it, blessed it, and proportioned its sustenance in four equal intervals for all who ask.
041|011|Then, He turned to the sky, which was smoke, and He said to it and the earth, “Come, willingly or unwillingly.” They responded, “We come willingly.”
041|012|Thus, He completed them as seven heavens in two periods, and He assigned to each heaven its duty. We adorned the nearest heaven with lamps and protection. Such is the decree of the Almighty, the All-Knowing.
041|013|If they turn away, say, “I have warned you of a thunderbolt, similar to Aad’s and Thamud’s.”
041|014|When the messengers came to them, from in front and behind, saying, “Worship none but Allah,” they responded, “If our Lord had willed, He would’ve sent down angels. Therefore, we disbelieve in your message.”
041|015|As for Aad, they were arrogant on earth, denied the truth, and said, “Who is mightier than us?” Didn’t they see that Allah, who created them, is mightier than them? And they continued to deny Our revelations.
041|016|So We unleashed upon them a roaring wind, for a few unfortunate days, to make them taste the disgraceful punishment in this worldly life. However, the punishment of the Hereafter is more shameful, and they won’t be helped.
041|017|As for Thamud, We offered them guidance, but they preferred blindness over guidance. Thus, the thunderbolt of a humiliating punishment seized them for their deeds.
041|018|And We saved those who believed and were righteous.
041|019|On the Day when Allah’s enemies are gathered and marshaled towards the Fire.
041|020|When they reach it, their hearing, their eyes, and their skin will testify against them regarding what they used to do.
041|021|They will ask their skins, “Why did you testify against us?” They will reply, “Allah, who gave everything the ability to speak, made us speak. He who first created you, and to Him, you will return.
041|022|You could not shield yourselves from your hearing, sight, and skins testifying against you. And you thought that Allah didn’t know much of what you do.
041|023|Your misconception about your Lord caused your ruin, and now you are among the losers.
041|024|If they endure patiently, the Fire is their destination. If they try to justify themselves, they won’t be pardoned.
041|025|We’ve appointed partners for them, who make their past and future actions attractive to them, leading them towards a fate akin to that of previous generations of jinn and humans, all of whom ultimately met their loss.
041|026|The unbelievers say, “Don’t listen to this Quran, and drown it in noise, so you may prevail.”
041|027|We will make those who disbelieve taste the severe punishment and reward them with the worst of what they used to do.
041|028|This is the retribution for Allah’s enemies: the Fire, their eternal dwelling, a recompense because they used to deny Our signs.
041|029|The disbelievers will plead, “Our Lord, show us those who misled us—both jinn and humans—so we may put them beneath our feet, reducing them to the lowest.”
041|030|Those who say, “Our Lord is Allah,” and then go straight, the angels will descend upon them: “Fear not, nor grieve, but rejoice in the Paradise that you’ve been promised.
041|031|We are your allies in this life and in the Hereafter, where you will have everything your hearts could desire and everything you request.
041|032|A hospitality from a Merciful Forgiver.”
041|033|Who speaks better than one who calls to Allah, acts righteously, and says, “I am among those who submit”?
041|034|Good and evil aren’t equal. Repel by what’s better, and your former enemy may become a dear friend.
041|035|Yet, none will attain it except those who are patient. And none will attain it except the very fortunate.
041|036|When a provocation from Satan assails you, seek refuge in Allah. He is the All-Hearing, the All-Knowing.
041|037|Among His signs are the night and the day, and the sun and the moon. Don’t bow down to the sun or the moon, but bow down to Allah, who created them both, if it’s Him that you serve.
041|038|If they display arrogance, those who stand in your Lord’s presence praise Him night and day, and they never tire.
041|039|Among His signs: you see the earth barren, but when We send down water upon it, it quivers and grows. Indeed, He who gave it life, is the Giver of Life to the dead; He has power over everything.
041|040|Those who distort Our verses aren’t hidden from Us. Are those who are hurled into the Fire better, or those who arrive safe and sound on Resurrection Day? Do what you wish; He is Seeing of everything you do.
041|041|Those who reject the Reminder when it comes to them—it’s an invincible Book.
041|042|Falsehood can’t approach it, neither from before it, nor from behind it. It is a revelation from a Wise, Praiseworthy One.
041|043|Nothing is said to you that wasn’t said to the messengers before you: your Lord is the Owner of forgiveness, and the Owner of painful retribution.
041|044|Had We made the Quran in a foreign language, they would have said, “Why are its verses not explained clearly?” A foreign and Arabic?” Say, “It is guidance and healing for those who believe. Yet, those who disbelieve are deaf and blind to it. They are being called from a place far away.”
041|045|We gave Moses the Scripture, but disputes arose regarding it. If it wasn’t for a predetermined decision from your Lord, they would’ve been judged immediately. Yet they are in perplexing doubt about it.
041|046|Whoever acts righteously is for his good, and whoever commits evil is to his detriment. Your Lord does not wrong the servants.
041|047|To Him belongs the knowledge of the Hour. No fruit emerges from its sheath, nor does any female conceive or give birth, except with His knowledge. On the Day when He questions them, “Where are My partners?” They will reply, “We confess to You, not one of us can testify to that.”
041|048|What they used to invoke before will disappear from them, and they will realize that there is no refuge for them.
041|049|Man never tires of praying for good, but if adversity touches him, he becomes despondent and despairing.
041|050|And if we make him taste mercy from Us after harm has touched him, he will surely say, “This is for me, and I don’t think the Hour will come. And even if I’m returned to my Lord, surely, with Him, I will have the ultimate good.” But We will inform those who disbelieve of what they did, and We will make them taste a harsh punishment.
041|051|When We bestow blessings upon a person, he turns away and withdraws. But when adversity touches him, he indulges in extensive prayers.
041|052|Say, “Have you considered: if it is from Allah and you rejected it, who is more astray than one who is in extreme dissension?”
041|053|We will show them Our signs on the horizons and within themselves, until it becomes clear to them that it’s the truth. Does it not suffice that your Lord is a Witness over everything?
041|054|Yes, they are in doubt about meeting their Lord. Yes, He fully encompasses all things.
042|001|Ha. Meem.
042|002|Ayn. Seen. Qaaf.
042|003|Thus does Allah, the Mighty, the Wise, inspire you and those before you.
042|004|Everything in the heavens and on earth belongs to Him. He is the Most High, the Supreme.
042|005|The heavens almost rupture from above them, while the angels praise the glory of their Lord and seek forgiveness for those on earth. Allah is the Forgiving, the Merciful.
042|006|As for those who take protectors other than Him, Allah is watchful over them, and you aren’t a trustee over them.
042|007|Thus, We revealed to you an Arabic Quran, to warn the Mother of Cities and those around it, and to warn of the Day of Gathering, about which there is no doubt. A group will be in paradise, and a group in the Blaze.
042|008|Had Allah willed, He could’ve made them one community, but He admits into His mercy whom He wills. The wrongdoers have no protector or helper.
042|009|Or have they taken protectors other than Him? Allah alone is the Protector. He gives life to the dead, and He is over all things capable.
042|010|In any matter of dispute, the final decision rests with Allah. “This is Allah, my Lord. Upon Him I have relied, and to Him I turn.”
042|011|The Creator of the heavens and the earth, has made for you mates from your own kind, and pairs of livestock, by which He multiplies you. There is nothing like Him. He is the All-Hearer, the All-Seer.
042|012|To Him belong the controls of the heavens and the earth. He extends provision for whomever He wills, and restricts. He is fully aware of everything.
042|013|He ordained for you the same religion He enjoined upon Noah, and what We revealed to you, and what We enjoined upon Abraham, Moses, and Jesus: “Uphold the religion, and don’t be divided within it.” What you call the polytheists to is difficult for them. Allah chooses for Himself whom He wills and guides to Himself whoever turns back.
042|014|They didn’t become divided until after knowledge had come to them, out of mutual envy. If not for a prior decree from your Lord, judgment would’ve been issued between them. Those who were made to inherit the Scripture after them are in troubling doubt concerning it.
042|015|So, invite to this, and be upright as you’re commanded, and don’t follow their desires. And say, “I believe in whatever Scripture Allah revealed. And I am commanded to judge justly among you. Allah is our Lord and your Lord. We have our deeds, and you have yours. There is no contention between us and you. Allah will bring us together, and to Him is the final return.”
042|016|As for those who argue about Allah after his acceptance, their argument is null before their Lord, and upon them is wrath, and for them is severe punishment.
042|017|It is Allah who revealed the Scripture with truth and balance. What would make you realize? Perhaps the Hour is near.
042|018|Those who don’t believe in it seek to hasten it, but those who believe are fearful of it, and they know that it’s the truth. Those who dispute about the Hour are indeed in a far misguidance.
042|019|Allah is kind to His servants. He provides sustenance for whomever He wills. He is the Strong, the Mighty.
042|020|Whoever desires the harvest of the Hereafter, we will increase for him his yield. And whoever desires the harvest of this world, We will give him some of it, but in the Hereafter he will have no share.
042|021|Or do they have associates who have legislated for them a religion not authorized by Allah? If not for a conclusive word, judgment would’ve been passed between them. The wrongdoers will face a grievous punishment.
042|022|You will see the wrongdoers fearful of what they’ve earned, and it will befall them. Yet those who believe and do righteous deeds will be in the meadows of the gardens, receiving whatever they desire from their Lord. This is the greatest bounty.
042|023|Allah gives this good news to His servants who believe and perform righteous deeds. Say, “I ask no reward from you for it, except affection to kin.” Whoever earns a good deed, We will increase its goodness for him. Allah is Forgiving and Appreciative.
042|024|Or do they say, “He invented lies about Allah”? If Allah willed, He could seal your heart. But Allah dispels falsehoods and establishes the truth with His words. He is fully aware of what resides within hearts.
042|025|It is He who accepts repentance from His beings, forgives sins and knows what you do.
042|026|He answers those who believe and perform righteous deeds, and increases them from His bounty. But the unbelievers will suffer a harsh punishment.
042|027|If Allah were to expand the provision for His servants, they would commit excess on earth. But He sends down what He wills in measured amounts. He is All-Seeing and All-Aware of His beings.
042|028|It is He who sends down rain after they have lost hope and spreads His mercy. He is the Protector, the Praiseworthy.
042|029|Among His signs are the creation of the heavens and the earth, and the living creatures He has spread within them. And He is capable of gathering them at will.
042|030|Whatever misfortune befalls you is due to your deeds. Yet, He pardons much.
042|031|You can’t escape on earth, and you have no protector or helper besides Allah.
042|032|Among His signs are ships sailing like mountains in the sea.
042|033|If He willed, He could still the wind, leaving them motionless on its surface. In this, there are signs for every patient, grateful person.
042|034|Or He could destroy them because of what they’ve earned, yet He pardons much.
042|035|Those who dispute Allah’s revelations won’t find any refuge.
042|036|What you’ve been given is merely the enjoyment of the temporal worldly life, but what Allah possesses is better and more enduring for those who believe and rely on their Lord.
042|037|Those who avoid grave sins and indecencies; and when they are angered, they forgive.
042|038|Those who respond to their Lord, perform their prayers, conduct their affairs by mutual consultation, and give from what We provide for them.
042|039|Those who, when tyranny afflicts them, defend themselves.
042|040|The retribution for an evil deed is an equivalent evil. Yet, whoever pardons and reconciles, his reward is with Allah. He doesn’t love the wrongdoers.
042|041|Those who retaliate after being wronged bear no guilt.
042|042|The guilt lies with those who oppress others and instigate aggression on earth without justice. For them, there is a severe punishment.
042|043|Those who patiently endure and forgive demonstrate fortitude.
042|044|Whomever Allah misguides will have no protector besides Him. When they face the punishment, you will witness the wrongdoers pleading, “Is there any way to go back?”
042|045|You will see them exposed to it, humbled by disgrace, looking with a furtive glance. The believers will say, “The losers are those who lost themselves and their families on Resurrection Day.” Surely, the wrongdoers are in lasting punishment.
042|046|They will have no protectors to aid them other than Allah. And for whomever Allah leaves astray, there is no way.
042|047|Respond to your Lord before a Day from Allah arrives that can’t be repelled. On that Day, you will have no shelter, and no possibility of denial.
042|048|If they turn away, We didn’t send you as their keeper. Your responsibility is only to deliver the message. When We bestow Our grace on a person, he rejoices in it. And when adversity touches him due to his deeds, man becomes ungrateful.
042|049|To Allah belongs the sovereignty of the heavens and the earth. He creates whatever He wills. He grants to whom He wills females, and males to whom He wills.
042|050|Or He combines them in pairs, male and female, and He renders whom He wills infertile. He is All-Knowing, Most Capable.
042|051|It is not for any human that Allah should speak to him, except through revelation, or from behind a veil, or by sending a messenger to reveal, by His permission, what He wills. He is Exalted, Wise.
042|052|And thus, We’ve revealed to you an inspiration of Our command. You didn’t know what the Scripture was, nor the faith. But We made it a light, guiding with it whomever We will of Our servants. You are guiding them to a straight path.
042|053|The path of Allah, to Whom belongs whatever is in the heavens and whatever is on earth. Unquestionably, to Allah do all matters evolve.
043|001|Ha. Meem.
043|002|By the clear and enlightening Scripture.
043|003|We’ve made it an Arabic Quran, so you may understand.
043|004|In fact, it is in the Source of the Book with Us, exalted and full of wisdom.
043|005|Should We withdraw the Message from you, since you are a people who transgress?
043|006|How many a Prophet did We send among the ancients?
043|007|Yet, no Prophet came to them but they mocked him.
043|008|We destroyed those far more powerful than them, and the example of the ancients has gone past.
043|009|If you were to ask them, “Who created the heavens and the earth?” They would surely state, “The Almighty, the All-Knowing created them.”
043|010|He who made the earth a cradle for you, and traced routes upon it for you, so you may find your way.
043|011|He who sends down rain from the sky in measured quantities, and with it, We revive a lifeless land. Similarly, you will be resurrected.
043|012|He who created all paired things, and granted for you ships and animals that you may ride.
043|013|So that you may be mounted on their backs, remember your Lord’s favor when seated on them, and say, “Exalted be He who has put this under our control; we couldn’t have done it by ourselves.
043|014|And indeed, to our Lord, we will return.”
043|015|They made some of His servants a part of Him. The human being is openly ungrateful.
043|016|Did He choose daughters for Himself from what He created, and favored you with sons?
043|017|When one of them is informed of what he attributes to the Most Merciful, his face darkens, and he is repressed with grief.
043|018|“An entity nurtured amidst ornaments?” And he suppresses inner conflicts.
043|019|They attribute the angels, who are servants of the Gracious, as females. Did they witness their creation? Their testimony will be recorded, and they will be questioned.
043|020|They assert, “If the Merciful had willed, we wouldn’t have worshiped them.” They don’t know this; they are only speculating.
043|021|Or did We give them a scripture before this one to which they are adhering?
043|022|But they say, “We found our ancestors upon a course, and we are guided by their footsteps.”
043|023|Likewise, whenever We sent a warner before you to any city, its affluent inhabitants said, “We found our forefathers following a path, and we are following in their footsteps.”
043|024|He would say, “Even if I bring you better guidance than what you found your forefathers following?” They would reply, “We reject what you’ve been sent with.”
043|025|So We wreaked vengeance on them. Consider the end of the deniers.
043|026|Abraham told his father and his people, “I am free from what you worship.
043|027|Only He who created me will guide me.”
043|028|He left this a lasting word among his descendants, so they might return.
043|029|I allowed these and their ancestors some enjoyment, until the truth arrived with a transparent messenger.
043|030|However, when the truth came to them, they said, “This is sorcery, and we disbelieve it.”
043|031|They ask, “Why wasn’t this Quran revealed to a notable man from one of the two cities?”
043|032|Is it they who dispense your Lord’s mercy? It is We who distribute their sustenance in this life, elevating some in ranks above others, so that they may take one another in service. Your Lord’s mercy is far better than whatever they amass.
043|033|Were it not that all mankind might become one community, We would have granted the Merciful-deniers houses with ceilings of silver and stairways upon which they could ascend.
043|034|And for their homes, doors, and beds on which they recline.
043|035|And all kinds of ornaments. However, all these are merely transient pleasures of this worldly life. The Hereafter, with your Lord, is for the righteous.
043|036|For those who shun the remembrance of the Most Merciful, We assign for them a devil to be their constant companion.
043|037|They lead them astray from the path, while they think they are guided.
043|038|Until, when he comes before Us, he will say, “I wish you and I were as distant as the two horizons—what a terrible companionship!”
043|039|It won’t benefit you on that Day if you did wrong; you will be sharing in the punishment.
043|040|Can you make the deaf hear; or guide the blind, or those who are in evident error.
043|041|Even if We were to take you away, We will inflict punishment upon them.
043|042|Or We may show you what We promised them, for We have absolute control over them.
043|043|So, adhere to what was revealed to you; you are on a straight path.
043|044|It is a reminder for you and your people, and you’ll be questioned.
043|045|Ask the messengers We sent before you: “Did We ever appoint gods to be worshiped other than the Most Merciful?”
043|046|With Our signs, we sent Moses to Pharaoh and his assembly, proclaiming, “I am the messenger of the Lord of the worlds.”
043|047|But when he presented Our verses to them, they laughed at them.
043|048|Every miracle We showed them was more significant than the one preceding it. And We afflicted them with plagues, so they might return.
043|049|They pleaded, “O magician, pray to your Lord for us, according to the covenant He made with you, and we will be guided.”
043|050|But when We relieved their affliction, they immediately broke their promise.
043|051|Pharaoh proclaimed among his people, “O my people, do I not rule Egypt, with these rivers flowing beneath me? Can’t you see?
043|052|Am I not superior to this pitiful wretch who can barely express himself?
043|053|Why were no gold bracelets dropped on him, or angels accompanying him in procession?”
043|054|He fooled his people, and they obeyed him. They were a people prone to wrongdoing.
043|055|When they provoked Our wrath, We retaliated by drowning them all.
043|056|And We made them a precedent and an example for future generations.
043|057|When the instance of Jesus, son of Mary, was cited, your people immediately jeered.
043|058|They argued, “Are our gods better, or is he?” They posed this question only to argue. They are a quarrelsome lot.
043|059|He was but a servant whom We blessed, and We set him an example for the Children of Israel.
043|060|Had We willed, We could’ve made from you angels to be successors on earth.
043|061|He is knowledge for the Hour. Have no doubt about it, and follow me. This is a straight path.
043|062|And don’t let Satan divert you; he is your clear enemy.
043|063|When Jesus came with the evident miracles, he said, “I’ve come to you with wisdom, and to clarify some of your disagreements. So fear Allah, and obey me.
043|064|Allah is my Lord and your Lord, so worship Him. This is a straight path.”
043|065|But the sects differed among themselves. Woe to those who commit wrong, for they will face severe punishment on a dreadful day.
043|066|Are they merely waiting for the Hour to come upon them suddenly while they are unaware?
043|067|On that Day, close friends will be enemies to each other, except for the righteous.
043|068|O My servants, there will be no fear or sorrow upon you that Day.
043|069|Those who believed in Our verses and submitted themselves.
043|070|Enter Paradise, you and your spouses, in happiness and delight.
043|071|Circulated among them are dishes and goblets of gold, and all that the soul could desire, and the eyes could delight in will be yours. You will reside there forever.
043|072|This is the Paradise which you’ve inherited because of what you used to do.
043|073|Therein for you are plentiful fruits, from which you eat.
043|074|Surely, for the wrongdoers, they will suffer the unending torment of Hell.
043|075|It won’t be lightened for them, and they will despair therein.
043|076|We didn’t wrong them, but they were the wrongdoers.
043|077|They will cry out: “O Malik, let your Lord end us!” He will say, “You are staying.”
043|078|Surely, We brought you the truth, but most of you hate the truth.
043|079|Did they devise a plan? We, too, are planning.
043|080|Or do they think that We don’t hear their secrets and their private conversations? Indeed, Our messengers, with them, are recording.
043|081|Say, “If the Merciful had a child, I would be the first to worship.”
043|082|Glory be to the Lord of the heavens and the earth, the Lord of the Throne, far beyond what they attribute to Him.
043|083|Let them chatter and play until they meet their promised Day.
043|084|He is Allah in the heavens and Allah on earth. He is the All-Wise, the All-Knowing.
043|085|Blessed is He who holds dominion over the heavens, the earth, and all that is between them. With Him is the knowledge of the Hour, and you will be returned to Him.
043|086|None of those they call upon besides Him has any power of intercession, except those who testify to the truth knowingly.
043|087|If you were to ask them, “Who created them?” they would reply, “Allah.” How, then, are they deluded?
043|088|Regarding his statement, “O my Lord, these are people who don’t believe.”
043|089|Pardon them, and say, “Peace.” Soon they will find out.
044|001|Ha, Meem.
044|002|By the clear, enlightening Scripture.
044|003|We revealed it on a blessed night—We’ve been warning.
044|004|On that night, every wise matter is made distinct.
044|005|A command from Us—We’ve been sending messengers.
044|006|As a mercy from your Lord—He is the All-Hearing, the All-Knowing.
044|007|The Lord of the heavens and the earth, and all that’s between them—if you are certain.
044|008|There is no god but He. He gives life and causes death—your Lord and the Lord of your ancestors.
044|009|Still, they are playing in doubt.
044|010|Await the day when the sky will bring visible smoke.
044|011|It will envelop the people: this is a painful punishment.
044|012|“Our Lord, lift from us the punishment; we are believers.”
044|013|How can there be a reminder for them, since a clear Messenger has already come to them?
044|014|Yet they turned away from him and said, “He is tutored, a madman.”
044|015|We will withdraw the punishment a little. But you will surely return.
044|016|The Day We will strike with the greatest assault—We will take revenge.
044|017|Before them, We tested the people of Pharaoh, when a noble messenger came to them.
044|018|“Hand over to me Allah’s servants. I am definitely a reliable messenger to you.
044|019|And don’t exalt yourselves against Allah; I’ve come to you with clear authority.
044|020|I have sought refuge in my Lord and your Lord, lest you stone me.
044|021|If you don’t believe me, then keep your distance from me.”
044|022|Then, he implored his Lord, “These are criminal people.”
044|023|“Depart with My servants by night—you will be pursued.
044|024|And leave the sea in stillness; they are soldiers to be drowned.”
044|025|How many gardens and springs did they leave behind?
044|026|And fields and noble sites.
044|027|And comfort wherein they were amused.
044|028|Thus, and We made it an inheritance for another people.
044|029|Neither heaven nor earth wept for them, nor were they reprieved.
044|030|We rescued the Children of Israel from the degrading torment.
044|031|From Pharaoh. He was a tyrant, an oppressor.
044|032|And We knowingly chose them over the worlds.
044|033|We gave them signs in which there were transparent trials.
044|034|Yet these people say:
044|035|“There is only our first death, and we won’t be resurrected.
044|036|Then bring back our ancestors, if you are truthful.”
044|037|Are they better than the people of Tubba and those before them? We destroyed them because they were criminals.
044|038|We didn’t create the heavens, the earth, and everything in between in play.
044|039|We created them only in truth, but most of them don’t know.
044|040|The Day of Decision is their appointed time, all of them.
044|041|The Day when no relation will avail a relation at all, nor will they be helped.
044|042|Except those on whom Allah has mercy. He is the Mighty, the Merciful.
044|043|The Tree of Bitterness.
044|044|Food of the sinners.
044|045|Like molten brass, it boils in the bellies.
044|046|Like the boiling of seething water.
044|047|“Grab him and drag him into the middle of the Hellfire.
044|048|Then, pour over his head from the suffering of the Inferno.
044|049|Taste! For you are the mighty, the noble one!
044|050|This is what you used to question.”
044|051|As for the righteous, they will be in a safe place.
044|052|Amid gardens and springs.
044|053|Clothed in fine silk and heavy brocade, facing each other.
044|054|Thus. And We will pair them with pure companions with beautiful eyes.
044|055|They will call for fruit therein, in peace and tranquility.
044|056|Therein, they will taste no death, beyond the first death. And He will shield them from the torment of Hellfire.
044|057|As a bounty from your Lord. That is the grand success.
044|058|We’ve made it easy in your language, so they may reflect.
044|059|So, wait. They too are waiting.
045|001|Ha. Meem.
045|002|This Book is a revelation from Allah, the Almighty, the All-Wise.
045|003|In the heavens and the earth are signs for the believers.
045|004|And in your creation, and in the various kinds of creatures He scattered, are signs for people who are sure.
045|005|And in the alternation of night and day, in the sustenance that Allah sends down from the sky, reviving the earth after its death, and in His control of the winds, there are signs for people who reason.
045|006|These are Allah’s verses which We convey to you in truth. So, in what message, after Allah and His verses, will they believe?
045|007|Woe to every liar, sinful fabricator.
045|008|Who hears Allah’s verses recited to him, persists in arrogance, as if he didn’t hear them. Inform him of a painful punishment.
045|009|When he becomes aware of some of Our verses, he mocks them. For them, there is a humiliating punishment.
045|010|Ahead of them lies Hell. Neither their wealth nor their allies besides Allah will avail them anything. For them, there is a tremendous punishment.
045|011|This is guidance. Those who reject their Lord’s signs will have a severe punishment of a humiliating nature.
045|012|It is Allah who made the sea submissive to you, so that ships may traverse it by His decree, and you may seek His bounty, and perhaps you may express gratitude.
045|013|He made everything in the heavens and on earth subservient to you—all is from Him. In this, there are signs for those who reflect.
045|014|Tell those who believe to forgive those who don’t anticipate the days of Allah, for He repays people according to their deeds.
045|015|Whoever works righteousness, it is for the good of his own soul; and whoever does evil, it is upon it. Then to your Lord you will be returned.
045|016|We gave the Children of Israel the Scripture, wisdom, and prophethood; and We provided them with good things, and We favored them above all other nations.
045|017|We provided them with clear proofs of the matter. They only began to dispute after knowledge came to them—out of mutual jealousy. Your Lord will judge between them on Resurrection Day regarding their disputes.
045|018|Then We set you on the path of the ordinance, so follow it, and don’t follow the whims of those who don’t know.
045|019|They won’t be able to protect you from Allah in anything. The wrongdoers are allies of each other, but Allah is the Ally of the righteous.
045|020|These are insights for humankind, guidance, and mercy for people who have unwavering faith.
045|021|Do those who commit evil deeds think that We will make them like those who have believed and done righteous deeds, both in their life and after their death? How ill they judge!
045|022|Allah created the heavens and the earth with truth. Each soul will be repaid for what it has earned, and they won’t be wronged.
045|023|Have you seen him who takes his own desires as his god? Allah, knowingly, allows him to stray, seals his hearing and heart, and places a covering over his sight. Who, then, can guide him after Allah? Won’t you then reflect?
045|024|They assert, “There is nothing but our worldly life; we live and we die, and time alone destroys us.” But they have no knowledge of this; they are only guessing.
045|025|When Our clear verses are presented to them, their only argument is, “Bring our ancestors back, if you are truthful.”
045|026|Say, “Allah gives you life, then makes you die, then gathers you for the Day of Resurrection, about which there is no doubt. But most people don’t know.”
045|027|To Allah belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth. On the Day when the Hour is established, on that day, those who falsify will lose.

045|029|This is our record which speaks against you with truth. We were recording what you used to do.”
045|030|Then, as for those who believed and did righteous deeds, their Lord will admit them into His Mercy. That is the clear triumph.
045|031|As for those who disbelieved: “Weren’t My verses recited to you, but you were arrogant and were guilty people?”
045|032|When it was said, “Allah’s promise is true, and there is no doubt about the Hour,” you said, “We don’t know what the Hour is. We conceive it as nothing more than speculation, and we aren’t sure.”

046|014|These are the inhabitants of Paradise, dwelling therein eternally, as a reward for their deeds.
046|015|We commanded the human being to care for his parents. His mother bore him with hardship and gave birth to him with hardship. His pregnancy and nursing total thirty months. When he reaches his prime at forty, he prays, “My Lord, grant me the ability to be grateful for the blessings You’ve bestowed upon me and upon my parents, and to perform righteous deeds that please You. And make my offspring virtuous. I turn to You in repentance, and I am among those who submit.”
046|016|These are the ones from whom We accept the best of what they did, and whose misdeeds We overlook—among the inhabitants of Paradise. The true promise which they had been promised.
046|017|However, the one who says to his parents, “Enough of you! Are you threatening me with resurrection, even though generations have passed before me?” And they both appeal to Allah for help, “Woe to you! Believe! The promise of Allah is true!” Yet, he replies, “This is nothing but tales of the ancients.”
046|018|Such individuals are on par with the previous generations of jinn and humans; they are the losers.
046|019|Everyone will be ranked according to their deeds, so that He may fully compensate them for their deeds, and they won’t be wronged.
046|020|On the Day when those who disbelieved are presented before the Fire: “You used up your good things during your worldly life and enjoyed them. So today, you will receive a shameful punishment for your unwarranted arrogance on earth and due to your sinful deeds.”
046|021|Mention the brother of Aad, when he warned his people amidst the dunes. Numerous warners had come before and after him, saying, “worship only God; I fear for you the punishment of a momentous day.”
046|022|They responded, “Did you come to steer us away from our gods? So bring us what you promise us, if you are truthful.
046|023|He replied, “The knowledge of that is with Allah alone, and I only convey to you what I was sent with. But I see that you are a people behaving ignorantly.”
046|024|When they saw a cloud approaching their valleys, they exclaimed, “This cloud will bring us rain!” But it was what they had requested: a storm wind in which is painful punishment.
046|025|It destroyed everything by the command of its Lord. By morning, nothing could be seen, except their dwellings. Thus We recompense the guilty people.
046|026|We had empowered them, just as We empowered you, giving them hearing, sight, and intellect. However, their hearing, sight, and intellect availed them not when they rejected Allah’s signs. And they were surrounded by what they used to mock.
046|027|We’ve destroyed communities around you, and We displayed various signs, so they may return.
046|028|Why then didn’t those whom they took to draw them closer to Allah come to their aid? They abandoned them, for they were merely their own fabrication.
046|029|When We sent a group of jinn towards you, listened to the Quran. Upon their arrival, they said to each other, “Pay attention!” When the recitation was completed, they went back to their own people as warners.
046|030|They declared, “O our people, we’ve heard a scripture revealed after Moses; it confirms what preceded it; it guides to the truth and to a straight path.

046|032|Those who don’t respond to Allah’s call can’t escape on earth, nor will they have any protectors besides Him. Such are clearly in misguidance.
