We also sent down iron, in which is a great strength and benefits for humankind, so that Allah may distinguish those who support Him and His messengers, although unseen. Allah is Powerful and Mighty.
057|026|We sent Noah and Abraham, and We established prophethood and Scripture among their descendants. Some of them were guided, yet many are sinners.
057|027|Then, following their footsteps, We sent Our messengers, and We sent Jesus, the son of Mary, and We gave him the Gospel. We instilled compassion and mercy into the hearts of his followers. They invented monasticism, which We had not prescribed for them—only seeking Allah’s approval, but they didn’t observe it with due observance. Therefore, We gave those among them who believed their reward, but many of them are sinners.
057|028|O you who believe, be conscious of Allah, and believe in His Messenger; He will give you a double share of His mercy, and He will make for you a light by which you walk, and forgive you. Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.
057|029|The People of the Scripture should know that they have no monopoly whatsoever over Allah’s mercy and grace, and that all grace and mercy are in Allah’s hands. He grants them to whom He wills. Allah is the possessor of vast bounty.
058|001|Allah heard the plea of the woman who argued with you concerning her husband and brought her complaint to Allah. Allah listened to your conversation. Allah is All-Hearing, All-Seeing.
058|002|Among you, those who estrange their wives by equating them with their mothers—they aren’t their mothers. Their mothers are only those who gave birth to them. What they say is unacceptable and false. Nonetheless, Allah is Pardoning, Forgiving.
058|003|Those who estrange their wives by equating them with their mothers, then retract their statement, must free a captive before they may touch each other. This is what you are admonished by; and Allah is aware of your actions.
058|004|Whoever doesn’t find the means, he must fast for two consecutive months before they may touch each other. If he is unable, then he must feed sixty needy people. This is to affirm your faith in Allah and His Messenger. These are the limits Allah sets, and there is a severe punishment for the unbelievers.
058|005|Those who defy Allah and His Messenger will be subdued, just as those before them were subdued. We revealed clear verses, and for the unbelievers, there is a disgraceful punishment.
058|006|On the Day Allah resurrects them all, He will inform them of their deeds. Allah kept a record of it, even though they forgot it. Allah is a witness to all things.
058|007|Are you not aware that Allah knows everything in the heavens and on earth? No three people converse in secret, but He is their fourth, nor among five, but He is their sixth. Regardless of their number, He is with them wherever they may be. Then, on Resurrection Day, He will inform them of what they did. Allah is fully aware of everything.
058|008|Didn’t you see those who were forbidden from secret gatherings, yet they persist in what they were prohibited from, and they conspire in sin, aggression, and disobedience to the Messenger? When they come to you, they greet you in a way Allah didn’t greet you, and they say within themselves, “Why doesn’t Allah punish us for what we say?” Enough for them is Hell; they will roast in it. What a terrible destination!
058|009|O you who believe, when you converse privately, don’t converse in sin, hostility, and disobedience to the Messenger. Instead, converse in righteousness and piety, and fear Allah, to whom you will be gathered.
058|010|Secret counsels are of Satan, to sadden the believers. Yet, he can’t harm them at all except with Allah’s permission. So, let the believers put their trust in Allah.
058|011|O you who believe, when it is said to you, “Make room in assemblies”, then do so. Allah will make room for you. And when asked to disperse, then do so. Allah elevates in rank those of you who believe and those who are given knowledge. Allah is fully aware of what you do.
058|012|O you who believe, when you wish to have a private conversation with the Messenger, precede your private consultation with a charity. This is better and purer for you. However, if you lack the means, Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.
058|013|Are you reluctant to offer charity before your consultation? Since you could not, Allah has forgiven you. So, establish prayer, give the purifying charity, and obey Allah and His Messenger. Allah is fully aware of what you do.
058|014|Did you consider those who befriended a people with whom Allah is angered? They are neither from you nor from them, and they swear falsely while they know.
058|015|Allah prepared for them a severe punishment. How evil is what they used to do!
058|016|They’ve made their oaths a disguise, and they obstruct others from Allah’s way. A humiliating punishment awaits them.
058|017|Their wealth and children won’t avail them against Allah. They are the inhabitants of the Fire, dwelling there for eternity.
058|018|On the Day when Allah will resurrect them all, they will swear to Him as they swear to you, and they think they are upon something. Indeed, they are the liars.
058|019|Satan has gained mastery over them and made them forget the remembrance of Allah. These are the partisans of Satan. Indeed, the partisans of Satan are the losers.
058|020|Those who oppose Allah and His Messenger will be among the most humiliated.
058|021|Allah has decreed, “I will surely overcome, I and My messengers.” Indeed, Allah is Strong, Mighty.
058|022|You won’t find people who believe in Allah and the Last Day befriending those who oppose Allah and His Messenger, even if they are their parents, children, siblings, or kin. In their hearts Allah has imprinted faith and strengthened them with a spirit from Him. He will admit them into Gardens beneath which rivers flow, where they will dwell forever. Allah is pleased with them, and they are pleased with Him. These are the Party of Allah. Surely, the Party of Allah will be the victors.
059|001|Everything in the heavens and on earth praises Allah, the Almighty, the All-Wise.
059|002|It is He who expelled the disbelieving People of the Scripture from their homes during the first gathering. You didn’t anticipate their departure, and they assumed their strongholds would protect them from Allah. However, Allah came upon them from where they didn’t expect, striking fear into their hearts. They demolished their homes with their own hands and the believer’s hands. Therefore, take a lesson, O people of understanding.
059|003|Had Allah not decreed their banishment, He would’ve punished them in this world. And in the Hereafter, they will face the torment of the Fire.
059|004|That is because they opposed Allah and His Messenger. Whoever opposes Allah—Allah is severe in penalty.
059|005|What you cut down of the trees or left standing on their trunks, it was with Allah’s permission, to disgrace the wicked.
059|006|The gains that Allah granted His Messenger from them, without you having to mount on horses or camels, are because Allah gives His messengers authority over whomever He wills. Allah has power over all things.
059|007|The gains that Allah allocated to His Messenger from the town-dwellers are for Allah, the Messenger, the relatives, the orphans, the needy, and the person on the path—so it may not only circulate among the wealthy among you. Accept what the Messenger gives you, and refrain from what he forbids you. Fear Allah, for Allah is severe in retribution.
059|008|For the impoverished emigrants who were expelled from their homes and their properties, seeking favor from Allah and His approval, and supporting Allah and His Messenger—these are the truthful ones.
059|009|Those who had taken up residence and faith before them, love those who emigrated to them, and find no hesitation in their hearts in assisting them. They prioritize them over themselves, despite their own needs. Those who protect themselves from their own stinginess are the successful ones.
059|010|And those who came after them pray: “Our Lord, forgive us and our brethren who preceded us in faith, and leave no resentment in our hearts towards those who have believed. Our Lord, You are Most Kind, Most Merciful.”
059|011|Didn’t you see the hypocrites who say to their disbelieving brethren among the People of the Scripture, “If you are expelled, we will surely go out with you, and we will never obey anyone against you; and if you are fought, we will surely help you.” But Allah testifies that they are liars.
059|012|If they are expelled, they won’t go out with them; if they are attacked, they won’t help them. And even if they were to help them, they would turn their backs, then they wouldn’t be helped.
059|013|Their fear of you is more intense than their fear of Allah. This is because they are people who don’t comprehend.
059|014|They won’t fight you except from within fortified towns or behind walls. Their internal strife is intense. You may perceive them as united, but their hearts are fragmented. This is because they are people who lack understanding.
059|015|Like those before them, they experienced the evil consequences of their conduct, and an agonizing punishment awaits them.
059|016|Like the example of Satan, when he lures a person into disbelief. But when he disbelieves, he says, “I am innocent of you; I fear Allah, the Lord of the worlds.”
059|017|The end result for them is the Fire, where they will dwell forever. This is the recompense for those who do wrong.
059|018|O you who believe, be conscious of Allah, and let each soul consider what it has prepared for tomorrow. And fear Allah, for He knows everything you do.
059|019|And be not like those who forgot Allah, so He made them forget themselves. These are the sinners.
059|020|Not equal are the inhabitants of the Fire and the inhabitants of Paradise. The inhabitants of Paradise—they are the victorious.
059|021|If We had revealed this Quran upon a mountain, you would’ve seen it humbled, shattered from fear of Allah. We present these parables to people, so they may reflect.
059|022|He is Allah, besides whom there is no god, the Knower of the invisible and the visible. He is the Gracious, the Merciful.
059|023|He is Allah, other than whom there is no deity, the Sovereign, the Sacred, the Source of Peace, the Giver of Faith, the Overseer, the Mighty, the Compeller, the Majestic. Glory be to Allah, far beyond what they associate with Him.
059|024|He is Allah, the Creator, the Inventor, the Designer. To Him belong the most beautiful names. All that’s in the heavens and the earth declares His glory. He is the Almighty, the All-Wise.
060|001|O you who believe, don’t take as allies My enemies and yours, showing them affection, even though they have rejected the truth that has come to you. They expelled the Messenger and yourselves because you believe in Allah, your Lord. If you’ve set out to strive in My cause and to seek My approval, how can you secretly express affection to them? I know what you hide and what you reveal. Whoever among you does this has deviated from the right path.
060|002|If they gain dominance over you, they become your adversaries, extend their hands and tongues against you with evil, desiring that you renounce your faith.
060|003|On the Day of Resurrection, neither your relatives nor your offspring will benefit you. He will separate between you. And Allah sees your actions.
060|004|There has been a good example set for you by Abraham and those with him, when they said to their people, “We disassociate ourselves from you and from whatever you worship besides Allah. We renounce you. Enmity and hatred have surfaced between us and you, indefinitely, until you believe in Allah alone.” Except for Abraham’s promise to his father: “I will seek forgiveness for you, but I am powerless to protect you from Allah.” “Our Lord, in You we place our trust, and to You we turn in repentance, and to You is the destiny.
060|005|Our Lord, don’t make us trial for the unbelievers, and forgive us. You are the Mighty and Wise.”
060|006|In them, there is an excellent example for those who hope for Allah and the Last Day. But whoever turns away—Allah is the Self-Sufficient, the Praiseworthy.
060|007|Perhaps Allah will foster love between you and those you consider enemies. Allah is capable of everything, and Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.
060|008|Allah doesn’t prohibit you from being kind and just towards those who don’t fight you because of religion or expel you from your homes. Allah loves those who act justly.
060|009|Allah only forbids you from those who fight you because of religion, expel you from your homes, or assist others in your expulsion. Whoever allies with them—these are the wrongdoers.
060|010|O you who believe, when believing women come to you as refugees, test them. Allah is best aware of their faith. If you ascertain that they are believers, don’t send them back to the unbelievers. They are not lawful for them, nor are they lawful for them. Reimburse them for what they had spent. There is no fault in you if you marry them, provided you give them their dowries. Don’t maintain the marital ties with the unbelieving women; demand what you spent, and let them demand what they spent. This is Allah’s decree. He judges between you. Allah is All-Knowing, All-Wise.
060|011|If any of your wives leave you for the unbelievers, and you subsequently retaliate, then pay those whose wives have gone the equivalent of what they had spent. And be mindful of Allah, in whom you believe.
060|012|O Prophet, when believing women come to you, pledging allegiance to you, that they won’t associate anything with Allah, nor steal, nor commit adultery, nor kill their children, nor fabricate any falsehood, nor disobey you in what is right, then accept their pledge and ask forgiveness for them from Allah. Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.
060|013|O you who believe, don’t befriend people with whom Allah has become angry. They have despaired of the Hereafter, just as the unbelievers have despaired of the occupants of the graves.
061|001|Everything in the heavens and on earth glorifies Allah, the Almighty, the All-Wise.
061|002|O you who believe, why do you say what you don’t do?
061|003|It is greatly displeasing to Allah that you say what you don’t do.
061|004|Allah loves those who fight in His cause, in formation, as if they were a solid structure.
061|005|When Moses said to his people, “O my people, why do you harm me, when you know that I am Allah’s Messenger to you?” When they swerved, Allah swerved their hearts. Allah does not guide the immoral people.
061|006|When Jesus, the son of Mary, said, “O Children of Israel, I am Allah’s Messenger to you, confirming the Torah that preceded me, and announcing a Messenger to come after me, his name will be Ahmad.” However, when he brought them the evident miracles, they said, “This is obvious magic.”
061|007|Who is more unjust than someone who fabricates lies about Allah while being invited to Submission? Allah doesn’t guide the wrongdoing people.
061|008|They wish to extinguish Allah’s light with their words, but Allah insists on completing His light, despite the hatred of the unbelievers.
061|009|It is He who sent His Messenger with the guidance and the religion of truth, to make it prevail over all other religions, despite the associators’ hatred.
061|010|O you who believe, shall I introduce you to a trade that will save you from much suffering?
061|011|Believe in Allah and His Messenger, and strive in Allah’s way with your wealth and your lives. That is better for you, if you only knew.
061|012|He will forgive your sins and admit you into Gardens beneath which rivers flow, and into fine dwellings in the Gardens of Eternity. That’s the ultimate success.
061|013|And another thing you love: victory from Allah and an imminent conquest. So, give the believers good news.
061|014|O you who believe, be supporters of Allah, as Jesus, son of Mary, said to the disciples, “Who are my supporters towards Allah?” The disciples replied, “We are the supporters of Allah.” Then a faction among the Children of Israel believed, while another faction disbelieved. So, We supported those who believed against their enemy, and they became dominant.
062|001|Everything in the heavens and on Earth praises Allah—the Supreme Sovereign, the Sacred, the Almighty, the All-Wise.
062|002|It is He who raised, amidst the illiterate, a messenger from their own, conveying to them His verses, purifying them, and teaching them the Scripture and wisdom. Before this, they were in clear misguidance.
062|003|And others of them who haven’t yet joined them. He is the Almighty, the Wise.
062|004|That is the grace of Allah, which He grants to whom He wills. Allah is the possessor of immense bounty.
062|005|The example of those entrusted with the Torah, yet failed to uphold it, is like that of a donkey carrying heavy books. Pitiful is the example of the people who deny Allah’s revelations. Allah does not guide wrongdoing people.
062|006|Say, “O you who are Jewish, if you claim to be the chosen allies of Allah, excluding all other people, then wish for death, if you are truthful.”
062|007|However, they will never wish for it, because of what their hands have done. Allah is fully aware of the wrongdoers.
062|008|Say, “The death from which you flee will meet you. Then you will be returned to the Knower of the unseen and the seen, and He will inform you of what you used to do.”
062|009|O you who believe, when the call to prayer is made on Friday, hurry to the remembrance of Allah, and leave off business. That’s better for you, if only you knew.
062|010|When the prayer is concluded, disperse in the land, seek Allah’s bounty, and remember Allah frequently, so you may succeed.
062|011|Yet when they see some trade or entertainment, they scatter towards it and leave you standing. Say, “What’s with Allah is better than any amusement or trade, and Allah is the Best of Providers.”
063|001|When the hypocrites come to you, they say, “We testify that you are Allah’s Messenger.” Yet, Allah knows that you are His Messenger, and Allah testifies that the hypocrites are liars.
063|002|They use their oaths as a shield, hindering others from Allah’s path. Their deeds are indeed deplorable.
063|003|This is because they believed, then disbelieved, so their hearts were sealed and they don’t understand.
063|004|When you see them, their physical appearances impress you, and when they speak, you listen to their words. They are like propped-up hollow timber. They think every shout is against them; they are the enemy, so beware of them. May Allah combat them! How deluded they are!
063|005|When they are told, “Come, let the Messenger of Allah seek forgiveness for you,” they turn their heads in disdain, and you see them turning away, while they are arrogant.
063|006|Whether you pray for their forgiveness or not, Allah won’t forgive them. Allah doesn’t guide the rebellious people.
063|007|They say, “Don’t spend on those who are with Allah’s Messenger, until they disband.” To Allah belong the treasures of the heavens and the earth, but the hypocrites can’t comprehend.
063|008|They say, “Once we return to the City, the more honorable will expel the more humble.” However, all honor and power belong to Allah, His Messenger, and the believers, but the hypocrites don’t know.
063|009|O you who believe, don’t let your wealth and children distract you from the remembrance of Allah. Those who do are the losers.
063|010|Spend from what We provide for you before death comes to one of you, and he says, “My Lord, if only You would delay me for a short while, so that I could give charity and be one of the righteous.”
063|011|But never will Allah delay a soul when its appointed time has come. Allah is informed of everything you do.
064|001|Everything in the heavens and the earth glorifies Allah. Sovereignty is His, and to Him praise is due, and He is capable of all things.
064|002|It is He who created you; among you are disbelievers, and among you are believers. Allah sees all that you do.
064|003|He created the heavens and the earth with truth. And He designed you, and He perfected your shapes. To Him is the final return.
064|004|He knows everything in the heavens and the earth, and He knows what you conceal and declare. And Allah knows what’s in the hearts.
064|005|Didn’t the stories of those who disbelieved before you reach you? They tasted the affliction of their actions; for them awaits a painful punishment.
064|006|This is because their messengers came to them with clear signs, but they said, “Are humans to guide us?” So, they disbelieved and turned away. Yet Allah is Self-Sufficient, Worthy of all praise.
064|007|Those who disbelieve claim, “they won’t be resurrected”. Say, “Yes, by my Lord, you will surely be resurrected, then you will be informed of what you did—and that is easy for Allah.”
064|008|So believe in Allah, His Messenger, and the light We revealed. Allah is fully aware of what you do.
064|009|The Day He gathers you for the Day of Assembly—that is the Day of loss and gain. Whoever believes in Allah and performs righteous deeds, He will absolve him of his sins and admit him into Gardens through which rivers flow, to abide therein eternally. That’s the supreme victory.
064|010|However, those who disbelieve and deny Our signs will be the inhabitants of the Fire, to remain therein forever. And what a wretched destination!
064|011|No disaster strikes except by Allah’s permission. Whoever believes in Allah, He will guide his heart. Allah is aware of everything.
064|012|So obey Allah and obey the Messenger. But if you turn away, Our Messenger is only responsible for clear delivery.
064|013|Allah—there is no deity except Him. In Allah should the believers place their trust.
064|014|O you who believe, among your spouses and your children, there are adversaries to you, so beware of them. And if you pardon, overlook, and forgive, then Allah is Forgiving and Merciful.
064|015|Your wealth and your children are a test, and with Allah is a great reward.
064|016|Be conscious of Allah as much as you are capable, and listen, and obey, and give for your own good. Whoever is protected from the greed of his own soul—these are the successful.
064|017|If you lend to Allah a good loan, He will multiply it for you and forgive you. Allah is Appreciative and Forbearing.
064|018|He is the Knower of the unseen and the seen, the Mighty and Wise.
065|001|O Prophet, when you divorce women, divorce them at their prescribed periods, and count their waiting period accurately. Be conscious of Allah, your Lord. Don’t expel them from their homes, nor should they leave, unless they have committed a clearly immoral conduct. These are the limits set by Allah. Whoever oversteps Allah’s limits wrongs his soul. You don’t know; perhaps Allah will thereafter bring about a new situation.
065|002|When they have reached their term, either retain them kindly or separate from them amicably. Call upon two trustworthy witnesses from among you, and establish truthful testimony for Allah. This counsels whoever believes in Allah and the Last Day. Whoever fears Allah, He will make a way out for him.
065|003|He will provide for him from where he doesn’t expect. Whoever puts his trust in Allah—He will be enough for him. Allah will accomplish His purpose. Allah has set a measure for all things.
065|004|As for your women who have passed menopause, if you are in doubt, their waiting period shall be three months, as well as for those who haven’t menstruated yet. As for those who are pregnant, their term lasts until they have given birth. Whoever fears Allah: He will make his affairs easy.
065|005|This is Allah’s commandment, which He revealed to you. Whoever fears Allah, He will erase his sins and magnify his reward.
065|006|Provide them residence where you reside, according to your means, and don’t harass them to make their lives difficult. If they’re pregnant, provide for them until they give birth. If they nurse for you, compensate them and maintain a cordial relationship. If you disagree, then another woman may nurse for him.
065|007|The wealthy should spend according to his means, and the one with limited resources should spend from what Allah has given him. Allah doesn’t burden a soul beyond what He has given it. Allah will bring about, after hardship, ease.
065|008|Many cities rebelled against the command of their Lord and His messengers, so We held them strictly accountable and severely punished them.
065|009|So they tasted the outcome of their deeds, and the result of their deeds was loss.
065|010|Allah has prepared for them a severe punishment. So beware of Allah, O you of understanding who have believed. Allah has sent down to you a reminder.
065|011|A messenger who delivers to you Allah’s clear verses, to bring out those who believe and do righteous deeds from darkness into light. Whoever believes in Allah and acts righteously, He will admit him into Gardens through which rivers flow, to live there forever. Allah has prepared for him an excellent provision.
065|012|It is Allah who created seven heavens and; and of the earth, the like of them. The command descends throughout them, so you may know that Allah has power over all things and that Allah encompasses all things in knowledge.
066|001|O Prophet, why do you prohibit what Allah has made lawful for you, seeking the approval of your wives? And Allah is Forgiving, Merciful.
066|002|Allah has already ordained for you the dissolution of your oaths. And Allah is your protector, He is the All-Knowing, All-Wise.
066|003|When the Prophet disclosed a matter in confidence to one of his wives, but when she disclosed it, and Allah made it known to him, he shared some of it and avoided part. Then, when he told her about it, she said, “Who informed you of this?” He said, “The All-Knowing, the All-Aware informed me.”
066|004|If you two repent to Allah, then your hearts have inclined. But if you cooperate against him—then Allah is his protector, and Gabriel and the righteous believers and the angels, moreover, are his helpers.
066|005|It may be if he divorced you, that his Lord will give him instead of you, wives better than you: submissive, faithful, obedient, penitent, worshippers, fasters, previously married and virgins.
066|006|O you who believe, protect yourselves and your families from a Fire whose fuel is people and stones, over which are angels, harsh and severe; they don’t disobey Allah in what He commands them, but they do what they are commanded.
066|007|O you who have disbelieved, make no excuses today. You are only being recompensed for what you used to do.
066|008|O you who have believed, repent to Allah with sincere repentance. Perhaps your Lord will remit your sins and admit you into Gardens through which rivers flow. On that Day, Allah won’t disappoint the Prophet and those who believed with him. Their light will proceed before them, and on their right, they will say, “Our Lord, perfect our light for us and forgive us. You are over all things competent.”
066|009|O Prophet, strive against the unbelievers and the hypocrites, and be harsh with them. Their abode is Hell, and wretched is the destination.
066|010|Allah presents an example for those who disbelieve: the wife of Noah and the wife of Lot. They were under two of our righteous servants, but they betrayed them, so they didn’t avail them from Allah at all, and it was said, “Enter the Fire with those who enter.”
066|011|And Allah presents an example for those who believe: the wife of Pharaoh, when she said, “My Lord, build for me near You a house in Paradise, save me from Pharaoh and his actions, and save me from the wrongdoing people.”
066|012|And Mary, the daughter of Imran, who guarded her chastity, so We breathed into her of Our Spirit. And she believed in the words of her Lord and His scriptures, and she was devoutly obedient.
067|001|Blessed is He in whose hand lies the dominion, and He is over all things competent.
067|002|He who created life and death to test which of you is best in conduct. And He is the Exalted in Might, the Forgiving.
067|003|He who created seven heavens in layers. You will see no discrepancy in the creation of the Merciful. Look again: do you see any flaws?
067|004|Look again, and yet again, and your sight will return to you dazzled and fatigued.
067|005|We adorned the lowest heaven with lamps, and We made them projectiles to drive away the devils. We prepared for them the torment of the Blaze.
067|006|For those who deny their Lord, the punishment of Hell awaits—a terrible destination.
067|007|When they are thrown into it, they will hear it gasping as it boils over.
067|008|It almost bursts with rage. Every time a batch is hurled into it, its keepers will ask them, “Did no Warner come to you?”
067|009|They will answer, “Yes, a warner did come to us, but we denied and said, ‘Allah didn’t reveal anything; you are greatly mistaken.’”
067|010|And they will say, “If only we had listened or used reason, we wouldn’t be among the inhabitants of the Fiery Blaze.”
067|011|They confessed their sin. So, away with the dwellers of the Blaze.
067|012|For those who fear their Lord unseen, for them is forgiveness and a grand reward.
067|013|Whether you conceal your words or declare them, He knows the secrets of the hearts.
067|014|Wouldn’t He know, He who created? He is the Kind, the Expert.
067|015|It is He who made the earth manageable for you. So traverse its tracks and eat from His provision. To Him is the resurgence.
067|016|Are you certain that the One in the heavens won’t cause the earth to swallow you as it shakes?
067|017|Are you sure that the One in the heavens won’t send upon you a violent wind? Then you will know how My warning was.
067|018|Those before them also denied. So, how was My condemnation?
067|019|Don’t they see the birds above them, spreading and folding their wings? None holds them up except the Merciful. He is watchful over all things.
067|020|Who could be an army to aid you, other than the Most Merciful? The unbelievers are in nothing but delusion.
067|021|Who will sustain you if He withholds His provision? Yet, they persist in defiance and aversion.

067|026|Respond, “Its knowledge lies only with Allah, and I am but a clear warner.”

067|030|Say, “Consider this: if your water were to sink, who could supply you with fresh, flowing water?”

106|004|Who fed them against hunger, and made them safe from fear.
107|001|Didn’t you see the one who denies the religion?
107|002|It is he who repulses the orphan.
107|003|And doesn’t encourage the feeding of the needy.
107|004|So woe to those who pray.
107|005|Those who are unmindful in their prayers.
107|006|Those who make a show.
107|007|And withhold assistance.
108|001|We’ve given you abundance.
108|002|So, pray to your Lord and sacrifice.
108|003|He who hates you, he will be cut off.
109|001|Say, “O unbelievers.
109|002|I don’t worship what you worship.
109|003|Nor are you worshipers of what I worship.
109|004|Nor will I worship what you worship.
109|005|Nor will you be worshippers of what I worship.
109|006|For you is your religion, and for me is mine.”
110|001|When Allah’s assistance and victory come.
110|002|And you see people entering Allah’s religion in multitudes.
110|003|Then, glorify the praises of your Lord, and seek His forgiveness. He is ever accepting of repentance.
111|001|Perish the hands of Abu Lahab, and perish he.
111|002|Neither his wealth nor his earnings will avail him.
111|003|He will enter a flaming Fire.
111|004|And his wife, the carrier of firewood.
111|005|Around her neck is a rope of palm fiber.
112|001|Say, “He is Allah, One and only.
112|002|Allah, the Eternal, the Absolute.
112|003|He neither begets nor is He begotten.
112|004|And there is none comparable or equivalent to Him.”
113|001|Say, “I take refuge in the Lord of Daybreak.
113|002|From the evil of what He created.
113|003|And from the evil of the darkness when it settles.
113|004|And from the evil of those who blow on knots.
113|005|And from the evil of the envier when he envies.”
114|001|Say, “I take refuge in the Lord of humanity.
114|002|The King of humanity.
114|003|The God of humanity.
114|004|From the evil of the retreating whisperer.
114|005|Who whispers into the hearts of people.
114|006|From among jinn and humans.”
